function createInventoryItem(data) {
  const sheet = SpreadsheetApp.openById(SPREADSHEET_ID).getSheetByName(SHEET_INVENTORY);
  if (!sheet) return responseJSON({status: 'error', message: 'Inventory sheet not found'});
  
  sheet.appendRow([
    data.channel, data.articleCode, data.sku, data.spIncTax || 0, data.stock || 0, data.ean || '', data.itemName || '', data.mrp || 0
  ]);
  return responseJSON({status: 'success', message: 'Item created'});
}

function updateInventoryPrice(data) {
  const sheet = SpreadsheetApp.openById(SPREADSHEET_ID).getSheetByName(SHEET_INVENTORY);
  const rows = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
  
  // Find indexes
  const headers = rows[0].map(h => String(h).toLowerCase().trim());
  const colChannel = headers.indexOf('channel');
  let colArticle = headers.indexOf('channel item code');
  if (colArticle === -1) colArticle = headers.findIndex(h => h.includes('item code') || h.includes('article'));
  let colPrice = headers.indexOf('selling price');
  if (colPrice === -1) colPrice = headers.findIndex(h => h.includes('selling') || h.includes('sp'));

  if (colChannel === -1 || colArticle === -1 || colPrice === -1) {
    return responseJSON({status: 'error', message: 'Required columns not found'});
  }
  
  for (let i = 1; i < rows.length; i++) {
    const rowChannel = String(rows[i][colChannel]).trim();
    const rowArticle = String(rows[i][colArticle]).trim();
    if (rowChannel.toLowerCase() === data.channel.toLowerCase() && rowArticle === String(data.articleCode)) {
      sheet.getRange(i + 1, colPrice + 1).setValue(data.newPrice);
      return responseJSON({status: 'success', message: 'Price updated'});
    }
  }
  return responseJSON({status: 'error', message: 'Item not found'});
}

function saveChannelConfig(data) {
  const sheet = SpreadsheetApp
    .openById(SPREADSHEET_ID)
    .getSheetByName(SHEET_CHANNEL_CONFIG);

  const rows = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
  const headers = rows[0].map(h => String(h).toLowerCase().trim());

  const nameIdx = headers.indexOf('channel name');
  if (nameIdx === -1) {
    throw new Error('Channel Name column not found');
  }

  let rowIndex = -1;

  // Find existing row
  for (let i = 1; i < rows.length; i++) {
    if (
      String(rows[i][nameIdx]).toLowerCase() ===
      String(data.channelName).toLowerCase()
    ) {
      rowIndex = i + 1;
      break;
    }
  }

  const getCol = (name) => {
    const idx = headers.indexOf(name.toLowerCase());
    return idx === -1 ? -1 : idx + 1;
  };

  const mapping = {
    status: getCol('status'),
    sourceEmail: getCol('source email'),
    searchKeyword: getCol('search keyword'),
    minOrderThreshold: getCol('min order threshold'),
    pocName: getCol('poc name'),
    pocEmail: getCol('poc email'),
    pocPhone: getCol('poc phone'),
    appointmentTo: getCol('appointment to'),
    appointmentCc: getCol('appointment cc')
  };

  if (rowIndex > 0) {
    // Update
    Object.keys(mapping).forEach(key => {
      if (mapping[key] > 0 && key in data) {
        sheet.getRange(rowIndex, mapping[key]).setValue(data[key]);
      }
    });
    return responseJSON({ status: 'success', message: 'Channel updated' });
  } else {
    // Create
    const newRow = new Array(headers.length).fill('');
    newRow[nameIdx] = data.channelName;

    Object.keys(mapping).forEach(key => {
      if (mapping[key] > 0 && key in data) {
        newRow[mapping[key] - 1] = data[key];
      }
    });

    sheet.appendRow(newRow);
    return responseJSON({ status: 'success', message: 'Channel created' });
  }
}


function saveSystemConfig(data) {
  const props = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
  if (data.easyecom_token) props.setProperty('EASY_ECOM_TOKEN', data.easyecom_token);
  if (data.easyecom_email) props.setProperty('EASY_ECOM_EMAIL', data.easyecom_email);
  if (data.nimbus_notification_email) props.setProperty('NIMBUS_NOTIFICATION_EMAIL', data.nimbus_notification_email);
  if (data.nimbus_cc_emails !== undefined) props.setProperty('NIMBUS_CC_EMAILS', data.nimbus_cc_emails);
  return {status: 'success', message: 'Config saved'};
}

// --- USER MANAGEMENT FUNCTIONS ---

function saveUser(data) {
  const sheet = SpreadsheetApp.openById(SPREADSHEET_ID).getSheetByName(SHEET_USERS);
  const rows = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
  const headers = rows[0];
  const idIdx = headers.indexOf('ID');
  
  let found = false;
  // Check if user exists to update
  for (let i = 1; i < rows.length; i++) {
    if (String(rows[i][idIdx]) === String(data.id)) {
      const range = sheet.getRange(i + 1, 1, 1, headers.length);
      const newRow = headers.map(h => {
        if (h === 'ID') return data.id;
        if (h === 'Name') return data.name;
        if (h === 'Email') return data.email;
        if (h === 'Contact') return data.contactNumber;
        if (h === 'Role') return data.role;
        if (h === 'Avatar') return data.avatarInitials;
        return '';
      });
      range.setValues([newRow]);
      found = true;
      break;
    }
  }
  
  if (!found) {
    sheet.appendRow([data.id, data.name, data.email, data.contactNumber, data.role, data.avatarInitials]);
  }
  return responseJSON({status: 'success', message: 'User saved'});
}

function deleteUser(userId) {
  const sheet = SpreadsheetApp.openById(SPREADSHEET_ID).getSheetByName(SHEET_USERS);
  const rows = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
  const idIdx = rows[0].indexOf('ID');
  for (let i = 1; i < rows.length; i++) {
    if (String(rows[i][idIdx]) === String(userId)) {
      sheet.deleteRow(i + 1);
      break;
    }
  }
  return responseJSON({status: 'success', message: 'User deleted'});
}

// ==========================================
// 4. AUTOMATION: EMAIL PROCESSING (Gmail)
// ==========================================

function processPurchaseOrders() {

  updateZohoItemIDs();
  SpreadsheetApp.flush();

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const configSheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_CHANNEL_CONFIG);
  const logSheet = getOrCreateLogSheet(ss, SHEET_PO_REPO);
  const folder = DriveApp.getFolderById(DRIVE_FOLDER_ID);

  // -------------------------------
  // Gmail Label Setup
  // -------------------------------
  const LABEL_NAME = 'ProcessedPO';
  let processedLabel = GmailApp.getUserLabelByName(LABEL_NAME);
  if (!processedLabel) {
    processedLabel = GmailApp.createLabel(LABEL_NAME);
  }

  const lastRow = configSheet.getLastRow();
  if (lastRow < 2) return;

  const configData = configSheet.getRange(2, 1, lastRow - 1, 4).getValues();

  const scriptProperties = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();

  const BUFFER_SECONDS = 5 * 60;
  let startTime = parseInt(scriptProperties.getProperty('LAST_RUN_TIME') || '0');

  if (startTime === 0) {
    const d = new Date();
    d.setDate(d.getDate() - 1);
    startTime = Math.floor(d.getTime() / 1000);
  }

  startTime = startTime - BUFFER_SECONDS;

  const currentRunTime = Math.floor(new Date().getTime() / 1000);
  const newLogs = [];


  const processedMessageIds = new Set();

  // =============================================
  // PROCESS CHANNELS
  // =============================================

  configData.forEach(row => {

    const [channelName, status, rawEmails, subjectKeyword] = row;

    if (!channelName || !rawEmails || String(status).toLowerCase() !== 'active') return;

    const channelKey = channelName.toLowerCase();

    const emailList = rawEmails.split(',').map(e => e.trim()).filter(Boolean);

    if (emailList.length === 0) return;

    const fromClause = `from:(${emailList.join(' OR ')})`;

    // ✅ INCLUDE AMAZON EMAILS ALSO
    let query = `${fromClause} -from:me after:${startTime} -label:${LABEL_NAME}`;
    if (subjectKeyword) query += ` subject:("${subjectKeyword}")`;

    try {

      const threads = GmailApp.search(query);
      if (threads.length === 0) return;

      const allMessages = GmailApp.getMessagesForThreads(threads);

      allMessages.forEach(messages => {

        messages.forEach(message => {

          const messageId = message.getId();
          if (processedMessageIds.has(messageId)) return;

          if (Math.floor(message.getDate().getTime() / 1000) <= startTime) return;

          const sender = message.getFrom().toLowerCase();
          const subject = message.getSubject();
          const emailBody = message.getPlainBody();
          const attachments = message.getAttachments();

          Logger.log(`Processing Email → ${subject}`);

          // ======================================================
          // 🔥 AMAZON PICKUP HANDLING
          // ======================================================

          if (isAmazonPickupEmail(sender, subject)) {

            

            const shipmentName = extractShipmentId(emailBody );
            const pickupSlotRaw = extractPickupSlot(emailBody);
            const pickupSlot = formatPickupSlot(pickupSlotRaw);

            if (shipmentName && pickupSlot) {
              updateAmazonPickup(shipmentName, pickupSlot);
            } else {
              Logger.log("Amazon extraction failed");
            }

            message.getThread().addLabel(processedLabel);
            processedMessageIds.add(messageId);
            return;
          }
          

          // ======================================================
          // 🔍 METADATA
          // ======================================================

          const metadata = analyzeEmailMetadata(
            channelKey,
            subject,
            subject.toUpperCase(),
            emailBody
          );

          // ======================================================
          // 🔥 REVISION HANDLING
          // ======================================================

          const isRevised = isRevisedEmail(subject, emailBody);

          if (isRevised && metadata.poNumber !== "Not Found") {

            const poNumber = metadata.poNumber;
            const finalChannel = channelName || channelKey;

            Logger.log(`Revision detected → ${poNumber}`);

            // -----------------------
            // Appointment (BODY)
            // -----------------------
            const appointmentDate = extractAppointmentFromBody(emailBody);

            let expiryDate = "";

            // -----------------------
            // Expiry (ATTACHMENT)
            // -----------------------

            if (attachments.length > 0) {

              const skuMapping = loadSkuMapping(ss);
              const channelThresholds = loadChannelThresholds(ss);

              for (let att of attachments) {

                try {

                  const fileName = att.getName().toLowerCase();
                  const blob = att.copyBlob();

                  let rawData = null;

                  if (fileName.endsWith(".csv")) {
                    rawData = Utilities.parseCsv(blob.getDataAsString());
                  }
                  else if (fileName.endsWith(".xls") || fileName.endsWith(".xlsx")) {
                    rawData = getExcelDataViaBlobFromAttachment(blob);
                  }
                  else if (fileName.endsWith(".pdf")) {

                    const tempFile = DriveApp.createFile(blob);
                    rawData = _extractTextFromPdf(tempFile.getId());
                    tempFile.setTrashed(true);
                  }

                  if (!rawData) continue;

                  const extracted = getExtractedDataByChannel(
                    rawData,
                    finalChannel,
                    poNumber,
                    metadata.storeCode,
                    skuMapping,
                    {},
                    channelThresholds,
                    new Date()
                  );

                  if (extracted && extracted.length > 0) {
                    expiryDate = extracted[0][6];
                    break;
                  }

                } catch (e) {
                  Logger.log("Attachment parse error: " + e.message);
                }
              }
            }

            if (!expiryDate) {
              Logger.log(`No expiry extracted for ${poNumber}`);
            }

            // -----------------------
            // UPDATE DB
            // -----------------------

            const changes = updateExistingPO(poNumber, {
              appointmentDate,
              expiryDate
            });

            // -----------------------
            // UPDATE REPO STATUS
            // -----------------------

            try {

              const repoSheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_PO_REPO);
              const repoData = repoSheet.getDataRange().getValues();
              const headers = repoData[0];

              const col = name => headers.indexOf(name);

              const IDX = {
                PO: col("PO Number"),
                STATUS: col("Status")
              };

              for (let i = 1; i < repoData.length; i++) {

                const repoPo = String(repoData[i][IDX.PO]).trim();

                if (repoPo === poNumber) {

                  if (changes.length > 0) {
                    repoSheet.getRange(i + 1, IDX.STATUS + 1)
                      .setValue(`Updated → ${changes.join(" | ")}`);
                  } else {
                    repoSheet.getRange(i + 1, IDX.STATUS + 1)
                      .setValue("Checked (No Change)");
                  }
                }
              }

            } catch (e) {
              Logger.log("Repo update error: " + e.message);
            }

            message.getThread().addLabel(processedLabel);
            processedMessageIds.add(messageId);
            return;
          }

          // ======================================================
          // 🟢 NORMAL PO FLOW (UNCHANGED)
          // ======================================================

          let successfullyProcessed = false;

          if (attachments.length > 0) {

            attachments.forEach(att => {

              try {

                const blob = att.copyBlob();
                const file = folder.createFile(blob);
                file.setName(`[${channelName}] ${att.getName()}`);

                newLogs.push([
                  message.getDate(),
                  channelName,
                  sender,
                  subject,
                  att.getName(),
                  file.getUrl(),
                  metadata.category,
                  metadata.poNumber,
                  metadata.storeCode,
                  ""
                ]);

                successfullyProcessed = true;

              } catch (e) {

                newLogs.push([
                  message.getDate(),
                  channelName,
                  sender,
                  subject,
                  att.getName(),
                  "SAVE FAILED",
                  "Error",
                  metadata.poNumber,
                  metadata.storeCode,
                  e.message
                ]);
              }
            });

          } else {

            if (metadata.poNumber !== "Not Found") {

              newLogs.push([
                message.getDate(),
                channelName,
                sender,
                subject,
                "No Attachment",
                "",
                metadata.category,
                metadata.poNumber,
                metadata.storeCode,
                ""
              ]);

              successfullyProcessed = true;
            }
          }

          if (successfullyProcessed) {
            message.getThread().addLabel(processedLabel);
            processedMessageIds.add(messageId);
          }

        });
      });

    } catch (e) {
      Logger.log(`Error processing ${channelName}: ${e.message}`);
    }

  });

  // =============================================
  // FINAL WRITE
  // =============================================

  if (newLogs.length > 0) {

    logSheet
      .getRange(logSheet.getLastRow() + 1, 1, newLogs.length, newLogs[0].length)
      .setValues(newLogs);
  }

  const SAFE_OFFSET = 60;
  const newRunTime = currentRunTime - SAFE_OFFSET;

  scriptProperties.setProperty('LAST_RUN_TIME', newRunTime.toString());
}

// =================================================================================
// FRONT-END FILE UPLOAD PROCESSOR
// =================================================================================

/**
 * **NEW MAIN FUNCTION FOR UPLOADS:** Called from a front-end UI. It receives a file,
 * analyzes it to determine the channel, uploads it to Drive, and logs the details
 * to the 'PO_Repository' sheet, mirroring the email processing logic.
 *
 * @param {string} base64Data - The base64 encoded string of the file.
 * @param {string} fileName - The original name of the uploaded file.
 * @return {object} A JSON object with a status ('success' or 'error') and a message.
 */
/**
 * **UPDATED:** Called from a front-end UI. It now includes specific logic
 * to extract the PO number directly from filenames formatted as 'purchase_order_{PO_ID}'.
 *
 * @param {string} base64Data - The base64 encoded string of the file.
 * @param {string} fileName - The original name of the uploaded file.
 * @return {object} A JSON object with a status ('success' or 'error') and a message.
 */
function ProcessFlipkartMinutesPO(base64Data, fileName) {
  try {
    if (!base64Data || !fileName) {
      throw new Error("File data or file name is missing.");
    }
    
    const folder = DriveApp.getFolderById(DRIVE_FOLDER_ID);
    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    const logSheet = getOrCreateLogSheet(ss, SHEET_PO_REPO);

    const decoded = Utilities.base64Decode(base64Data);
    const blob = Utilities.newBlob(decoded, MimeType.MICROSOFT_EXCEL_LEGACY, fileName);
    // =========================================================================
    // THE CHANGE IS HERE: Extract the PO Number from the filename first.
    // =========================================================================
    let poNum = "";
    
    // Use a regex to match the pattern 'purchase_order_{PO_ID}'
    const poMatch = fileName.match(/purchase_order_([A-Z0-9]+)/i);
    if (poMatch && poMatch[1]) 
    {
      poNum = poMatch[1];
      Logger.log(`Extracted PO Number "${poNum}" directly from the filename.`);
    }
        
    // --- The rest of the function continues as before ---
    
    const file = folder.createFile(blob);
    file.setName(`${fileName}`);
    const fileUrl = file.getUrl();
    
    const newLog = [
      new Date(),
      "FlipkartMinutes",
      "Manual Upload",
      fileName,
      fileName,
      fileUrl,
      "New PO",
      poNum
    ];

    logSheet.getRange(logSheet.getLastRow() + 1, 1, 1, newLog.length).setValues([newLog]);
    
    const successMessage = `Successfully processed and logged PO "${poNum}" for Flipkartminutes".`;
    Logger.log(successMessage);
    extractDatabaseDetails();
    return { status: "success", message: successMessage, fileUrl: fileUrl, poNumber: poNum };

  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log(`ERROR during manual upload processing: ${e.message}`);
    return { status: "error", message: e.message };
  }
}


  /**
 * **CORRECTED & ROBUST:** Analyzes email metadata with a proper if/else if structure
 * to ensure only one channel's logic runs per email.
 */
function analyzeEmailMetadata(channelKey, subjectOriginal, subjectUpper, emailBody) {
  // These calls get the category and PO number using your other existing functions.
  let category = determineCategory(subjectUpper); 
  let poNumber = extractPOFromText(channelKey, subjectUpper); 
  let storeCode = ""; // Default to blank

  // Safety check for the email body, which is required by some parsers.
  const body = emailBody || "";

  // Use a proper if/else if chain to ensure only one block executes.
  if (channelKey.includes("instamart") && category === "New PO") {
    const match = subjectOriginal.match(PATTERNS.INSTAMART_STORE_NEW);
    if (match) storeCode = match[1].trim();
  } 
  // --- FIX: Changed 'if' to 'else if' ---
  else if (channelKey.includes("bb") || channelKey.includes("bigbasket")) {
    const storeMatch = subjectOriginal.match(PATTERNS.BIGBASKET_STORE);
    if (storeMatch && storeMatch[1]) {
      storeCode = storeMatch[1].trim();
      Logger.log("SUCCESS: Extracted BigBasket store code: '" + storeCode + "'");
    } else {
      Logger.log("Warning: Could not extract BigBasket store code from subject: " + subjectOriginal);
    }
  }
  else if (channelKey.includes("blinkit") && subjectUpper.includes("PO_BCPL")) {
    category = "New PO";
    const extractionRegex = /^\*?\s*Bill To:\*?\s*BCPL - (.*)/im;
    const storeMatch = body.match(extractionRegex);
    if (storeMatch && storeMatch[1]) {
      let rawStoreCode = storeMatch[1].trim();
      Logger.log("Found raw store code: '" + rawStoreCode + "'");

      // =========================================================================
      // THE FINAL FIX IS HERE: A simple, non-regex, step-by-step method.
      // =========================================================================
      
      let lowerCaseCode = rawStoreCode.toLowerCase();
      let basePart = "";
      let warehousePart = "";

      // 1. Identify which warehouse suffix the string has.
      if (lowerCaseCode.endsWith(' feeder warehouse')) {
        // Get the part of the string BEFORE " feeder warehouse"
        basePart = rawStoreCode.substring(0, rawStoreCode.length - 17);
        warehousePart = 'Feeder Warehouse';
      } else if (lowerCaseCode.endsWith(' warehouse')) {
        // Get the part of the string BEFORE " warehouse"
        basePart = rawStoreCode.substring(0, rawStoreCode.length - 10);
        warehousePart = 'Warehouse';
      }

      // 2. If we found a warehouse part, clean up the base and re-join them.
      if (basePart && warehousePart) {
        // This is the key step: Remove any trailing space or hyphen from the base part.
        // The regex `/\s*-?\s*$/` matches optional spaces, an optional hyphen, and optional spaces at the end of the string.
        let cleanedBase = basePart.replace(/\s*-?\s*$/, '');
        
        // Reconstruct the string with the standardized separator.
        storeCode = `${cleanedBase} - ${warehousePart}`;
      } else {
        // If the string doesn't end with a known warehouse type, use it as-is.
        storeCode = rawStoreCode;
      }
      
      Logger.log("SUCCESS: Final formatted Blinkit store code: '" + storeCode + "'");
      
    }
    else {
      Logger.log("Warning: Could not find Blinkit 'Bill To:' details in email body.");
    }
  }
   
  return { category, poNumber, storeCode };
}



function determineCategory(text) {

  // 🔥 1. AMAZON FIRST (highest priority)
  if (PATTERNS.CAT_AMAZON_PICKUP.test(text)) {
    return "Amazon Pickup";
  }

  // Existing logic
  if (PATTERNS.CAT_GRN.test(text)) return "GRN";
  if (PATTERNS.CAT_REV.test(text)) return "Revision";
  if (PATTERNS.CAT_CANC.test(text)) return "Cancellation";
  if (PATTERNS.CAT_APP.test(text)) return "Appointment Confirmation";

  return "New PO";
}

function extractPOFromText(channelKey, text) {
  if (!text) return "Not Found";
  let match;
  if (channelKey.includes("zepto")) match = text.match(PATTERNS.ZEPTO_PO);
  else if (channelKey.includes("instamart")) {
    match = text.match(PATTERNS.INSTAMART_UNDERSCORE) || text.match(PATTERNS.INSTAMART_STANDARD);
    if (match && text.match(PATTERNS.INSTAMART_UNDERSCORE)) return match[1]; 
  }
  else if (channelKey.includes("bb")) {
  match = text.match(PATTERNS.BIGBASKET_ID); // Use the new, correct regex
  if (match) return match[1]; // Return ONLY the captured part (e.g., "IRM30207487")
  }
  else if (channelKey.includes("rbl") || channelKey.includes("reliance")) match = text.match(PATTERNS.RBL_PO);
  else if (channelKey.includes("blinkit")) {
    match = text.match(PATTERNS.BLINKIT_PO);
    if (match) return match[1];
  }
  
  if (!match) match = text.match(PATTERNS.GENERIC_PO);
  return match ? match[0] : "Not Found";
}

// ==========================================
// 5. AUTOMATION: DATA EXTRACTION (Repo -> DB)
// ==========================================

function normalizePoKey(po) {
  return String(po || "").trim().toUpperCase();
}

function buildPdfMap(repoData, IDX) {
  const pdfMap = {};

  repoData.forEach(row => {
    const channel = String(row[IDX.CHANNEL] || "").toLowerCase().trim();
    const fileName = String(row[IDX.FILE_NAME] || "").toLowerCase().trim();
    const category = String(row[IDX.CATEGORY] || "").trim().toLowerCase();
    const poKey = normalizePoKey(row[IDX.PO_NUMBER]);
    const url = String(row[IDX.FILE_URL] || "").trim();

    if (!poKey || !url || category !== "new po") return;

    const isPdf = /\.pdf$/i.test(fileName);
    const isExcel = /\.(xls|xlsx)$/i.test(fileName);

    // Prefer actual PDF for all channels
    if (isPdf) {
      pdfMap[poKey] = url;
      return;
    }

    // Fallback for channels where PO doc may come as Excel
    if ((channel === "bb" || channel === "flipkartminutes") && isExcel && !pdfMap[poKey]) {
      pdfMap[poKey] = url;
    }
  });

  Logger.log(`PDF Map built for ${Object.keys(pdfMap).length} PO(s).`);
  return pdfMap;
}

function extractDatabaseDetails() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const repoSheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_PO_REPO);
  const dbSheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_PO_DB);

  const skuMapping = loadSkuMapping(ss);
  const channelThresholds = loadChannelThresholds(ss);

  const repoLastRow = repoSheet.getLastRow();
  if (repoLastRow < 2) return;

  const repoData = repoSheet.getRange(1, 1, repoLastRow, repoSheet.getLastColumn()).getValues();
  const repoHeaders = repoData.shift();

  const col = name => repoHeaders.indexOf(name);

  const IDX = {
    CHANNEL: col("Channel Name"),
    FILE_NAME: col("File Name"),
    FILE_URL: col("Drive Link"),
    CATEGORY: col("Category"),
    PO_NUMBER: col("PO Number"),
    STATUS: col("Status"),
    STORE_CODE: col("Store Code"),
    APPOINTMENT_DATE: col("Appointment Date")
  };

  // -----------------------------
  // Build PDF Map first
  // -----------------------------
  const pdfMap = buildPdfMap(repoData, IDX);

  // -----------------------------
  // DB headers + duplicate guard
  // -----------------------------
  const dbHeaders = dbSheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, dbSheet.getLastColumn()).getValues()[0];
  const dbPoIndex = dbHeaders.indexOf("PO Number");
  const dbPoPdfIndex = dbHeaders.indexOf("PO PDF");

  const existingPoSet = new Set();

  if (dbSheet.getLastRow() > 1 && dbPoIndex !== -1) {
    const poValues = dbSheet
      .getRange(2, dbPoIndex + 1, dbSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 1)
      .getValues()
      .flat();

    poValues.forEach(p => {
      const key = normalizePoKey(p);
      if (key) existingPoSet.add(key);
    });
  }

  let databaseRows = [];
  let statusUpdates = {};

  // =============================================
  // MAIN LOOP
  // =============================================
  repoData.forEach((row, i) => {

    const sheetRow = i + 2;

    const status = String(row[IDX.STATUS] || "").trim();
    const category = String(row[IDX.CATEGORY] || "").trim();
    const fileUrl = row[IDX.FILE_URL];
    const fileName = String(row[IDX.FILE_NAME] || "").toLowerCase();
    const channel = String(row[IDX.CHANNEL] || "").trim();
    const poNumber = String(row[IDX.PO_NUMBER] || "").trim();
    const poKey = normalizePoKey(poNumber);

    if (status !== "" || !fileUrl) return;

    // ======================================================
    // REVISION LOGIC
    // ======================================================
    if (category === "Revision") {
      try {
        let expiryDate = "";

        const fileId = extractFileIdFromUrl(fileUrl);
        if (!fileId) return;

        let rawData = null;

        if (fileName.endsWith(".csv")) {
          rawData = getCsvData(fileId);
        } else if (fileName.endsWith(".xls") || fileName.endsWith(".xlsx")) {
          rawData = getExcelDataViaBlob(fileId);
        } else if (fileName.endsWith(".pdf")) {
          if ( channel.toLowerCase().includes("starmark") ||channel.toLowerCase().includes("rbl"))
          {
            rawData = _extractTextFromPdf(fileId);
            // ✅ FIX: Convert PDF text → structured array
            if (typeof rawData === "string") {
              rawData = rawData
              .split("\n")
              .map(line => line.split(/\s{2,}/));
              }
          }
        }

        if (rawData) {
          const extracted = getExtractedDataByChannel(
            rawData,
            channel,
            poNumber,
            row[IDX.STORE_CODE],
            skuMapping,
            pdfMap,
            channelThresholds,
            row[0]
          );

          if (extracted && extracted.length > 0) {
            expiryDate = extracted[0][6];
          }
        }

        const appointmentDate = row[IDX.APPOINTMENT_DATE];

        const changes = updateExistingPO(poNumber, {
          appointmentDate,
          expiryDate
        });

        statusUpdates[sheetRow] = changes.length > 0
          ? `Revision Updated → ${changes.join(" | ")}`
          : "Revision Checked (No Change)";

      } catch (e) {
        statusUpdates[sheetRow] = "Revision Error: " + e.message;
        Logger.log(e);
      }

      return;
    }

    // ======================================================
    // NEW PO LOGIC
    // ======================================================
    if (String(category).toLowerCase() !== "new po") return;

    if (existingPoSet.has(poKey)) {
      statusUpdates[sheetRow] = "Skipped (PO Already Exists)";
      return;
    }

    if (!fileName.match(/\.(xls|xlsx|csv|pdf)$/i)) {
      statusUpdates[sheetRow] = "Skipped (Not Data)";
      return;
    }

    try {
      const fileId = extractFileIdFromUrl(fileUrl);
      if (!fileId) return;

      let rawData = null;

      if (fileName.endsWith(".pdf")) {
          if ( channel.toLowerCase().includes("starmark") ||channel.toLowerCase().includes("rbl"))
          {
            rawData = _extractTextFromPdf(fileId);
            // ✅ FIX: Convert PDF text → structured array
            if (typeof rawData === "string") {
              rawData = rawData
              .split("\n")
              .map(line => line.split(/\s{2,}/));
              }
          }
        
      } else if (fileName.endsWith(".csv")) {
        rawData = getCsvData(fileId);
      } else {
        rawData = getExcelDataViaBlob(fileId);
      }

      if (!rawData) return;

      const extracted = getExtractedDataByChannel(
        rawData,
        channel,
        poNumber,
        row[IDX.STORE_CODE],
        skuMapping,
        pdfMap,
        channelThresholds,
        row[0]
      );

      if (extracted && extracted.length) {

        // 🔥 Force-fill PO PDF column before write
        if (dbPoPdfIndex !== -1) {
          const poPdfUrl = pdfMap[poKey] || "";
          extracted.forEach(r => {
            if (!r[dbPoPdfIndex]) {
              r[dbPoPdfIndex] = poPdfUrl;
            }
          });
        }

        databaseRows.push(...extracted);
        existingPoSet.add(poKey);
        statusUpdates[sheetRow] = "Extracted";

      } else {
        statusUpdates[sheetRow] = "Extracted (No Items)";
      }

    } catch (e) {
      statusUpdates[sheetRow] = "Error: " + e.message;
      Logger.log(e);
    }

  });

  // =============================================
  // WRITE NEW DATA
  // =============================================
  if (databaseRows.length) {
    dbSheet
      .getRange(dbSheet.getLastRow() + 1, 1, databaseRows.length, databaseRows[0].length)
      .setValues(databaseRows);
  }

  // =============================================
  // UPDATE STATUS
  // =============================================
  Object.keys(statusUpdates).forEach(r => {
    repoSheet.getRange(Number(r), IDX.STATUS + 1).setValue(statusUpdates[r]);
  });

  SpreadsheetApp.flush();

  syncInventoryAndCalculateAllocation();
  updateCustomerIdsInPoDatabase();
}

/**
 * **CORRECTED HELPER:** Extracts text from a PDF file using Google Drive OCR.
 * It correctly identifies the input as a PDF and asks Drive to convert it.
 * Requires the Drive API Advanced Service to be enabled.
 */
function _extractTextFromPdf(fileId) {

    Utilities.sleep(1500); // ✅ throttle

  try {
    const file = DriveApp.getFileById(fileId);
    const blob = file.getBlob();
    
    // =========================================================================
    // THE FIX IS HERE: Do NOT set the target MIME type in the resource object.
    // Let Drive infer the input type (PDF) and convert it based on the flags.
    // =========================================================================
    const resource = {
      title: "Temp_OCR_" + new Date().getTime()
      // Do NOT include mimeType: MimeType.GOOGLE_DOCS here.
    };
    
    // Insert the PDF.
    // ocr: true tells Drive to extract text from images/PDFs.
    // convert: true is usually required alongside ocr to force the creation of a Google Doc.
    const docFile = Drive.Files.insert(resource, blob, { ocr: true, ocrLanguage: 'en', convert: true });
    
    // Open the newly created Google Doc and extract the text.
    const doc = DocumentApp.openById(docFile.id);
    const text = doc.getBody().getText();
    
    // Clean up: delete the temporary Google Doc.
    Drive.Files.remove(docFile.id);
    
    return text;
    
  } catch (e) {
    throw new Error(`Failed to extract text from PDF via OCR: ${e.message}`);
  }
}

// Function to find all PO row indexes in the PO database sheet (for multiple rows with the same PO Number)
function findRowIndexesByPoNumber(dbSheet, poNumber) {
  //Logger.log(`Searching for PO Number: ${poNumber}`);

  const dbData = dbSheet.getDataRange().getValues();
  const rowIndexes = []; // To store all row indexes where PO number matches

  for (let i = 0; i < dbData.length; i++) {
    // Assuming PO Number is in column D (index 3, since columns are 0-based)
    const dbPoNumber = String(dbData[i][3]).trim(); // Convert to string for comparison
    if (dbPoNumber === String(poNumber).trim()) {
      //Logger.log(`Found PO Number: ${dbPoNumber} at row ${i + 1}`);
      rowIndexes.push(i + 1); // Push the 1-based row index into the array
    }
  }

  if (rowIndexes.length === 0) {
    Logger.log(`PO Number not found: ${poNumber}`);
  }

  return rowIndexes; // Return an array of row indexes (1-based)
}

// Channel Parsers
function getExtractedDataByChannel(
  data,
  channelName,
  poNum,
  storeCode,
  mapping,
  pdfMap,
  thresholds,
  poDate
  ) {
  if (!data || !Array.isArray(data)) return [];

  const key = (channelName || "").toLowerCase();

  try {

    if (key.includes("instamart"))
      return parseInstamartExcel(data, channelName, poNum, storeCode, mapping, pdfMap, thresholds);

    if (key.includes("zepto"))
      return parseZeptoExcel(data, channelName, poNum, storeCode, mapping, pdfMap, thresholds);

    if (key.includes("blinkit"))
      return parseBlinkitExcel(data, channelName, poNum, storeCode, mapping, pdfMap, thresholds, poDate);

    if (key.includes("bb"))
      return parseBigbasketExcel(data, channelName, poNum, storeCode, mapping, pdfMap, thresholds);

    if (key.includes("flipkartminutes"))
      return parseFlipkartMinutesExcel(data, channelName, mapping, pdfMap, thresholds);

    if (key.includes("amazon"))
      return parseAmazonExcel(data, channelName, mapping);

    if (key.includes("starmark"))
      return parseStarmarkPdf(data, channelName, poNum, mapping, pdfMap);

    if (key.includes("rbl"))
      return parseRBLPdf(data, channelName, poNum,storeCode, mapping, pdfMap);

  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log(`❌ Parser failed for ${channelName}: ${e.message}`);
    return [];
  }
}
function parseRBLPdf(data, channel, poNum, storeCode, skuMapping, pdfMap) {
  let tempItems = [];
  let poDate    = "";
  let poEDD     = "";
  let siteCode  = "";

  // ─── Flatten every row into a single trimmed string ───────────────────────
  const lines = data
    .map(row => (Array.isArray(row) ? row : [row]).join(" ").replace(/\s+/g, " ").trim())
    .filter(l => l.length > 0);

  Logger.log(`📄 Total flat lines: ${lines.length}`);
  Logger.log(`📋 First 30 lines: ${JSON.stringify(lines.slice(0, 30))}`);

  // ─── PASS 1 — Extract metadata (scan ALL lines) ────────────────────────────
  lines.forEach(line => {
    const l = line.toLowerCase();

    // PO Date:  "PO Date : 29.04.2026"
    if (l.includes("po date") && !poDate) {
      const m = line.match(/(\d{2})\.(\d{2})\.(\d{4})/);
      if (m) poDate = m[0];
    }

    // Delivery Date: "DELIVERY DATE : 30.05.2026"
    if (l.includes("delivery date") && !poEDD) {
      const m = line.match(/(\d{2})\.(\d{2})\.(\d{4})/);
      if (m) poEDD = m[0];
    }

    // Site: "PO NO.: 5000691435 Site : S2OP"
    if (!siteCode && l.includes("site")) {
      const m = line.match(/[Ss]ite\s*:\s*([A-Z0-9]{2,10})/);
      if (m && m[1] !== "S2OP".slice(0, 0)) siteCode = m[1].trim();
    }
  });

  Logger.log(`📌 Meta → PO Date: ${poDate} | EDD: ${poEDD} | Site: ${siteCode}`);
  if (!siteCode) siteCode = storeCode;

  // ─── PASS 2 — Find item table header then parse rows ──────────────────────
  // The header line contains "Sr.No" or "Article No" — mark it, then read items.
  //
  // Per the PDF, item lines on Page 2 look like ONE of:
  //
  //   A) All on one line (if PDF parser merged them):
  //   "1 494514278 95030020 8906163952670 ABC1 NE CBL DRIFT 4X4 SPEED CUBE 30.05.2026 S2OP 350.000 EA 195.00 5.00 0.00 0.00 3,412.50 0.00 0.00 68,250.00"
  //
  //   B) Split across multiple lines (common in PDF parsers):
  //   line i  : "1 494514278"
  //   line i+1: "95030020"
  //   line i+2: "8906163952670"
  //   ...
  //
  // Strategy: collect all tokens between the header and "Grand Total",
  // then re-chunk by Sr.No pattern (a line starting with a bare integer 1-999).

  let headerFound = false;
  let itemTokens  = [];   // flat token stream from the item table area

  for (let i = 0; i < lines.length; i++) {
    const line  = lines[i];
    const lower = line.toLowerCase();

    if (!headerFound) {
      if (lower.includes("sr.no") || lower.includes("article no") || lower.includes("hsn code")) {
        headerFound = true;
        Logger.log(`✅ Header found at line ${i}: ${line}`);
      }
      continue;
    }

    // Stop collecting at grand total or payment terms
    if (lower.includes("grand total") || lower.includes("terms of payment")) break;

    // Append tokens from this line
    const tokens = line.split(/\s+/).filter(t => t.length > 0);
    itemTokens = itemTokens.concat(tokens);
  }

  Logger.log(`🪣 Raw item tokens collected: ${itemTokens.length}`);
  Logger.log(`🪣 Token sample: ${JSON.stringify(itemTokens.slice(0, 40))}`);

  // ─── PASS 3 — Re-chunk tokens into item records ───────────────────────────
  //
  // Each item starts with a Sr.No (1, 2, 3...) followed by a 9-digit Article No.
  // We find all positions where tokens[i] is a small integer and tokens[i+1] is
  // a 9-digit number — those are item boundaries.

  const itemStartPositions = [];
  for (let i = 0; i < itemTokens.length - 1; i++) {
    const isSrNo      = /^\d{1,3}$/.test(itemTokens[i]);
    const isArticleNo = /^\d{9}$/.test(itemTokens[i + 1]);
    if (isSrNo && isArticleNo) {
      itemStartPositions.push(i);
    }
  }

  Logger.log(`📦 Item boundaries found: ${itemStartPositions.length} → at positions ${JSON.stringify(itemStartPositions)}`);

  for (let b = 0; b < itemStartPositions.length; b++) {
    const start = itemStartPositions[b];
    const end   = (b + 1 < itemStartPositions.length) ? itemStartPositions[b + 1] : itemTokens.length;
    const parts = itemTokens.slice(start, end);

    Logger.log(`🔍 Item ${b + 1} tokens (${parts.length}): ${JSON.stringify(parts)}`);

    // Minimum viable token count:
    // Sr.No, ArticleNo, HSN, EAN, VendorCode, [1+ desc words],
    // Date(dd.mm.yyyy), Site, Qty, UOM, MRP, IGST%, CESS%, CesFxRt,
    // IGST-amt, CESS-amt, CesFxVl, TotalBaseVal  = 18 minimum
    if (parts.length < 18) {
      Logger.log(`⚠️ Skipping — too few tokens (${parts.length})`);
      continue;
    }

    // Fixed head fields
    const srNo      = parts[0];                  // "1"
    const articleNo = parts[1];                  // "494514278"
    const hsnCode   = parts[2];                  // "95030020"
    const eanNo     = parts[3];                  // "8906163952670"
    const vendorArt = parts[4];                  // "ABC1"

    // Fixed tail fields (from the end — these are always the same count)
    // [last]    TotalBaseVal  "68,250.00"
    // [last-1]  CesFxdVl      "0.00"
    // [last-2]  CESS          "0.00"
    // [last-3]  IGST-amt      "3,412.50"
    // [last-4]  CesFxdRt      "0.00"
    // [last-5]  CESS%         "0.00"
    // [last-6]  IGST%         "5.00"
    // [last-7]  MRP           "195.00"
    // [last-8]  UOM           "EA"
    // [last-9]  Qty           "350.000"
    // [last-10] Site          "S2OP"
    // [last-11] Date          "30.05.2026"

    const L          = parts.length - 1;
    const totalBase  = parseFloat(parts[L    ].replace(/,/g, "")) || 0;
    const igstAmt    = parseFloat(parts[L - 3].replace(/,/g, "")) || 0;
    const igstPct    = parseFloat(parts[L - 6].replace(/,/g, "")) || 0;
    const mrp        = parseFloat(parts[L - 7].replace(/,/g, "")) || 0;
    const uom        =            parts[L - 8];
    const qty        = parseFloat(parts[L - 9].replace(/,/g, "")) || 0;
    const itemSite   =            parts[L - 10];
    const itemDate   =            parts[L - 11];

    // Description = everything between vendorArt (index 4) and itemDate (index L-11)
    const descTokens = parts.slice(5, L - 11);
    const description = descTokens.join(" ").trim();

    // Per-unit base cost
    const baseCostPerUnit = qty > 0 ? (totalBase / qty).toFixed(2) : "0.00";

    // Effective values with fallback
    const effectiveEDD  = /\d{2}\.\d{2}\.\d{4}/.test(itemDate) ? itemDate : poEDD;
    const effectiveSite = itemSite && /^[A-Z0-9]{2,10}$/.test(itemSite) ? itemSite : siteCode;

    if (!articleNo || qty === 0) {
      Logger.log(`⚠️ Skipping item ${srNo} — no articleNo or qty=0`);
      continue;
    }

    const masterSKU  = findMasterSku(skuMapping, "rbl", articleNo);
    const zohoItemId = findZohoItemId(skuMapping, "rbl", articleNo);

    Logger.log(`✅ Item ${srNo}: ${articleNo} | "${description}" | Qty:${qty} | MRP:${mrp} | Cost/unit:${baseCostPerUnit} | EDD:${effectiveEDD} | Site:${effectiveSite}`);

    tempItems.push([
       "New",
       convertRBLDate(poDate),      // ← was formatDate(poDate)
      channel,
      poNum,
      effectiveSite,
      convertRBLDate(effectiveEDD), // ← was formatDate(effectiveEDD)
      convertRBLDate(effectiveEDD),                  // expiry date set as EDD
      articleNo,
      masterSKU,
      description,
      qty,
      mrp,
      baseCostPerUnit,
      pdfMap[poNum],
      zohoItemId
    ]);
  }

  Logger.log(`✅ RBL done — ${tempItems.length} items extracted | PO: ${poNum}`);
  return tempItems;
}

function convertRBLDate(ddmmyyyy) {
  if (!ddmmyyyy) return "";
  const parts = ddmmyyyy.split(".");
  if (parts.length !== 3) return ddmmyyyy;
  return parts[2] + "-" + parts[1] + "-" + parts[0]; // → "2026-04-29" (ISO)
  // OR return parts[0] + "/" + parts[1] + "/" + parts[2]; // → "29/04/2026"
  // Use whichever format your formatDate() / DB expects
}

function cleanRBLName(rawName) {
  if (!rawName) return "";

  return rawName
    .toString()
    .replace(/\n/g, " ")
    .replace(/\s{2,}/g, " ")
    .trim();
}




function parseStarmarkPdf(data, channel, poNum, skuMapping, pdfMap) {
  const rows = [];


  // -------------------------
  // HEADER EXTRACTION
  // -------------------------
  let poDate = "";
  let poExpiry = "";
  let extractedPoNum = poNum || "";

  
  // PO Number
  const poMatch =
  data.match(/PURCHASE\s+ORDER\s+([A-Z0-9\-\/]+)/i) ||
  data.match(/PO\s*NO\.?\s*[:\-]?\s*([A-Z0-9\-\/]+)/i) ||
  data.match(/\bMI-\d{2}-POR-\d+\b/i);

  if (poMatch) {
  extractedPoNum = poMatch[1] || poMatch[0];
  } 

  const dateMatch = data.match(/Date\s+(\d{2}-\d{2}-\d{4})/i);
  if (dateMatch) poDate = _formatStarmarkDate(dateMatch[1]);

  const expiryMatch = data.match(/Valid Till\s+(\d{2}-\d{2}-\d{4})/i);
  if (expiryMatch) poExpiry = _formatStarmarkDate(expiryMatch[1]);

  const poEDD = poDate;

  // Normalize text
  const text = data.replace(/\n+/g, " ").replace(/\s+/g, " ");

  const rsRegex = /RS\./g;
  const rsMatches = [...text.matchAll(rsRegex)];

  for (let i = 0; i < rsMatches.length; i++) {
    const rsIndex = rsMatches[i].index;
    const prevRsIndex = i === 0 ? 0 : rsMatches[i - 1].index + 3;
    const nextRsIndex = i < rsMatches.length - 1
      ? rsMatches[i + 1].index
      : text.length;

    const leftWindow = text.substring(prevRsIndex, rsIndex).trim();
    const rightWindow = text.substring(rsIndex + 3, nextRsIndex).trim();

    const qtyMatch = leftWindow.match(/(\d+)\s*$/);
    const qty = qtyMatch ? Number(qtyMatch[1]) : 0;
    if (!qty) continue;

    const priceMatch = rightWindow.match(/^([\d.]+)/);
    const cost = priceMatch ? Number(priceMatch[1]) : 0;
    if (!cost) continue;

    const skuMatches = leftWindow.match(/\b(TB\d{5}|\d{7})\b/g);
    const itemCode = skuMatches ? skuMatches[skuMatches.length - 1] : "";
    if (!itemCode) continue;

    const safeChannel = String(channel).toLowerCase();
    const masterSKU = findMasterSku(skuMapping, safeChannel, itemCode) || "Not Found";
    const zohoItemId = findZohoItemId(skuMapping, safeChannel, itemCode) || "";

    const cleanName = leftWindow
      .replace(/\b(TB\d{5}|\d{7})\b/g, "")
      .replace(/\d+\s*$/, "")
      .replace(/CODE/ig, "")
      .replace(/\b\d{13}\b/g, "")
      .replace(/\b\d+\.\d+\b/g, "")
      .replace(/\b\d+\b/g, "")
      .replace(/\s{2,}/g, " ")
      .trim();

    rows.push([
      "New",
      poDate,
      channel,
      extractedPoNum,
      "Kolkata Warehouse",
      poEDD,
      poExpiry,
      itemCode,
      masterSKU,
      cleanName,
      qty,
      0,
      cost,
      pdfMap ? pdfMap[poNum] || "" : "",
      zohoItemId
    ]);
  }

  return rows;
}

function extractStarmarkSKU(text) {
  if (!text) return "";

  // TBxxxxx
  let m = text.match(/\bTB\d{5}\b/i);
  if (m) return m[0];

  // Exactly 7-digit numeric SKU
  m = text.match(/\b\d{7}\b/);
  if (m) return m[0];

  return "";
}

/**
 * **NEW HELPER:** Specifically parses the 'DD-MM-YYYY' format from Starmark POs.
 */
function _formatStarmarkDate(dateStr) {
  if (!dateStr || typeof dateStr !== 'string') return "";
  const parts = dateStr.split('-');
  if (parts.length !== 3) return dateStr;
  
  const day = parts[0];
  const month = parts[1];
  const year = parts[2].length === 2 ? "20" + parts[2] : parts[2];

  return `${year}-${month}-${day}`;
}

function parseInstamartExcel(data, channel, poNum, storeCode, skuMapping, pdfMap, channelThresholds) {

  let tempItems = [];
  let totalPoValue = 0;

  let poDate = "", poEDD = "", poExpiry = "";

  // -------------------------------
  // A. Extract Metadata (SAFE)
  // -------------------------------
  for (let r = 0; r < Math.min(data.length, 20); r++) {

    const row = data[r];
    if (!row || !Array.isArray(row)) continue;

    const rowStr = row.join(" ").toLowerCase();

    if (rowStr.includes("po date")) {
      const val = findValueInRowAfterKey(row, "PO Date");
      if (val) poDate = val;
    }

    if (rowStr.includes("expected delivery")) {
      const val = findValueInRowAfterKey(row, "Expected Delivery");
      if (val) poEDD = val;
    }

    if (rowStr.includes("expiry")) {
      const val = findValueInRowAfterKey(row, "Expiry");
      if (val) poExpiry = val;
    }
  }

  // -------------------------------
  // B. Find Header Row (ROBUST)
  // -------------------------------
  let headerRowIndex = -1;

  for (let r = 0; r < Math.min(30, data.length); r++) {

    const row = data[r];
    if (!row || !Array.isArray(row)) continue;

    const rowStr = row.join(" ").toLowerCase();

    // 🔥 Flexible detection
    if (
      (rowStr.includes("item") || rowStr.includes("product")) &&
      (rowStr.includes("qty") || rowStr.includes("quantity"))
    ) {
      headerRowIndex = r;
      break;
    }
  }

  if (headerRowIndex === -1) {
    Logger.log("❌ Header not found");
    return [];
  }

  const headerRow = data[headerRowIndex];

  // -------------------------------
  // C. Dynamic Column Detection
  // -------------------------------
  const colIndex = (keywords) => {
    for (let i = 0; i < headerRow.length; i++) {
      const cell = (headerRow[i] || "").toString().toLowerCase();
      if (keywords.some(k => cell.includes(k))) return i;
    }
    return -1;
  };

  const idxItemCode = colIndex(["item code", "item id", "product code", "code"]);
  const idxName = colIndex([
  "item desc",        // ✅ ADD THIS (critical)
  "item description",
  "product description",
  "description",
  "item name",
  "product name",
  "name",
  "desc"
]);
  const idxQty      = colIndex(["qty", "quantity", "order qty"]);
  const idxMrp      = colIndex(["mrp"]);
  const idxCost     = colIndex(["cost", "rate", "landing"]);

  Logger.log("📊 Column Mapping: " + JSON.stringify({
    idxItemCode, idxName, idxQty, idxMrp, idxCost
  }));

  // -------------------------------
  // D. Iterate Items (SAFE + SMART)
  // -------------------------------
  for (let r = headerRowIndex + 1; r < data.length; r++) {

    const row = data[r];
    if (!row || !Array.isArray(row)) continue;

    const itemCode = idxItemCode >= 0 ? row[idxItemCode] : "";

    if (!itemCode || itemCode.toString().trim() === "") continue;

    const rawName = idxName >= 0 ? row[idxName] : "";
    const cleanName = cleanInstamartItemName(rawName);

    const qty  = parseFloat(idxQty >= 0 ? row[idxQty] : 0) || 0;
    const mrp  = parseFloat(idxMrp >= 0 ? row[idxMrp] : 0) || 0;
    const cost = parseFloat(idxCost >= 0 ? row[idxCost] : 0) || 0;

    // skip empty rows
    if (qty === 0 && cost === 0) continue;

    totalPoValue += (qty * cost);

    const masterSKU = findMasterSku(skuMapping, "instamart", itemCode);
    const zohoItemId = findZohoItemId(skuMapping, "instamart", itemCode);

    tempItems.push({
      poDate,
      channel,
      poNum,
      storeCode,
      poEDD,
      poExpiry,
      itemCode,
      masterSKU,
      cleanName,
      qty,
      mrp,
      cost,
      pdfLink: pdfMap[poNum],
      zohoItemId
    });
  }

  // -------------------------------
  // E. Threshold Logic
  // -------------------------------
  const channelKey = (channel || "").toLowerCase();
  const threshold = channelThresholds[channelKey] || 0;

  const status =
    (threshold > 0 && totalPoValue * 1.05 < threshold)
      ? "Below Threshold"
      : "New";

  // -------------------------------
  // F. Final Mapping
  // -------------------------------
  const finalData = tempItems.map(i => [
    status,
    formatDate(i.poDate),
    i.channel,
    i.poNum,
    i.storeCode,
    formatDate(i.poEDD),
    formatDate(i.poExpiry),
    i.itemCode,
    i.masterSKU,
    i.cleanName,
    i.qty,
    i.mrp.toFixed(2),
    i.cost.toFixed(2),
    i.pdfLink,
    i.zohoItemId
  ]);

  Logger.log(`✅ Extracted ${finalData.length} items | PO: ${poNum}`);

  return finalData;
}

/**
 * **NEW & ROBUST:** Cleans a raw, multi-line item name from an Instamart PO.
 * It finds the start of the metadata (e.g., "1.0 Piece", "Colour:") and removes
 * everything after it, then cleans up all newline characters and extra spaces.
 *
 * @param {string} rawName - The original, potentially multi-line item name.
 * @return {string} The cleaned, single-line product name.
 */
function cleanInstamartItemName(rawName) {
  // Safety check for empty or invalid input.
  if (!rawName || typeof rawName !== 'string') {
    return "";
  }

  // --- Step 1: Define the patterns that signal the end of the product name ---
  // This regex looks for the FIRST occurrence of:
  // - A number (like 1 or 1.0) followed by "piece" or "pcs"
  // - OR the word "Colour:"
  // - OR the word "Size:"
  // - OR the word "Brand:"
  // The 'i' flag makes it case-insensitive.
  const stopPattern = /(\d+(\.\d+)?\s*pieces?\b|colour:|size:|brand:)/i;

  // --- Step 2: Find the index where the metadata begins ---
  const match = stopPattern.exec(rawName);
  let cleanName = rawName;

  // If a match is found, cut the string off just before the match.
  if (match) {
    cleanName = rawName.substring(0, match.index);
  }
  
  // --- Step 3: Clean up newlines and extra spaces ---
  
  // Replace all newline characters (\n) with a single space.
  cleanName = cleanName.replace(/\n/g, '');
  
  // Replace two or more consecutive spaces with a single space.
  cleanName = cleanName.replace(/\s{2,}/g, ' ');
  
  // Trim any leading or trailing whitespace.
  cleanName = cleanName.trim();
  
  return cleanName;
}

function parseZeptoExcel(data, channel, poNum, storeCode, skuMapping, pdfMap, channelThresholds) {
  let tempItems = [];
  let totalPoValue = 0;
  
  if (data.length < 2) return [];

  const headers = data[0].map(h => h.toString().trim());
  const getIdx = (name) => headers.indexOf(name);

  // Column Mappings
  const idxPoDate   = getIdx("PoDate");
  const idxStore    = getIdx("StoreName");
  const idxExpiry   = getIdx("PoExpiryDate");
  const idxItemCode = getIdx("Sku"); 
  const idxItemName = getIdx("SkuDesc");      
  const idxQty      = getIdx("Quantity");
  const idxMRP      = getIdx("MRP");
  const idxCost     = getIdx("UnitBaseCost");

  if (idxItemCode === -1 || idxQty === -1) return [];

  const timeZone = Session.getScriptTimeZone();

  for (let r = 1; r < data.length; r++) {
    const row = data[r];
    const itemCode = row[idxItemCode];

    if (!itemCode || itemCode.toString().trim() === "") continue;

    const cleanName = row[idxItemName]; 
    const masterSKU = findMasterSku(skuMapping, "zepto", itemCode);
    const zohoItemId = findZohoItemId(skuMapping, "zepto", itemCode);

    Logger.log(zohoItemId);

    // Dates
    const rawPoDate = row[idxPoDate];     
    const rawExpiry = row[idxExpiry];
    let finalPoDate = "", finalExpiry = "", finalEDD = "";

    if (rawPoDate) {
      const dateObj = new Date(rawPoDate);
      if (!isNaN(dateObj.getTime())) {
        finalPoDate = Utilities.formatDate(dateObj, timeZone, "dd-MMM-yyyy");
        const eddDate = new Date(dateObj); 
        eddDate.setDate(eddDate.getDate() + 10);
        finalEDD = Utilities.formatDate(eddDate, timeZone, "dd-MMM-yyyy");
      } else { finalPoDate = rawPoDate; }
    }

    if (rawExpiry) {
      const dateObj = new Date(rawExpiry);
      if (!isNaN(dateObj.getTime())) {
        finalExpiry = Utilities.formatDate(dateObj, timeZone, "dd-MMM-yyyy");
      } else { finalExpiry = rawExpiry; }
    }

    const qty = parseFloat(row[idxQty]) || 0;
    const mrp = parseFloat(row[idxMRP]) || 0;
    const cost = parseFloat(row[idxCost]) || 0;

    const finalStore = storeCode || row[idxStore];

    // Accumulate Value
    totalPoValue += (qty * cost);

    tempItems.push({
      finalPoDate, channel, poNum, finalStore, finalEDD, finalExpiry,
      itemCode, masterSKU, cleanName, qty, mrp, cost,
      pdfLink: pdfMap[poNum],zohoItemId
    });
  }

  // CHECK THRESHOLD
  const channelKey = channel.toLowerCase();
  const threshold = channelThresholds[channelKey] || 0;
  const status = (threshold > 0 && totalPoValue*1.05 < threshold) ? "Below Threshold" : "New";

  return tempItems.map(i => [
    status, // Col A: Status
    i.finalPoDate, 
    i.channel, 
    i.poNum, 
    i.finalStore,
    i.finalEDD,    
    i.finalExpiry, 
    i.itemCode, 
    i.masterSKU, 
    i.cleanName, 
    i.qty, 
    i.mrp.toFixed(2), 
    i.cost.toFixed(2),
    i.pdfLink,
    i.zohoItemId
  ]);
}

function parseBlinkitExcel(data, channel, poNum, storeCode, skuMapping, pdfMap, channelThresholds, repoPoDate) {
  let tempItems = [];
  let totalPoValue = 0;
  
  if (!data || data.length < 2) return [];

  // 1. Headers
  const headers = data[0].map(h => h.toString().trim());
  const getIdx = (name) => headers.indexOf(name);

  const idxItemCode = getIdx("Item Code");
  const idxItemName = getIdx("Product Description");
  const idxQty      = getIdx("Quantity");
  const idxMRP      = getIdx("MRP");
  const idxCost     = getIdx("Basic Cost Price"); 

  if (idxItemCode === -1 || idxQty === -1) {
    console.log(`Blinkit Headers not found in ${poNum}. Headers seen: ${headers.join(",")}`);
    return [];
  }

  // 2. CALCULATE DATES
  const timeZone = Session.getScriptTimeZone();
  let poDateFormatted = "";
  let poEddFormatted = "";
  let poExpiryFormatted = "";

  if (repoPoDate) {
    const d = new Date(repoPoDate);
    if (!isNaN(d.getTime())) {
      // PO Date
      poDateFormatted = Utilities.formatDate(d, timeZone, "dd-MMM-yyyy");
      
      // Expiry = PO Date + 15 Days
      const expD = new Date(d);
      expD.setDate(d.getDate() + 15);
      poExpiryFormatted = Utilities.formatDate(expD, timeZone, "dd-MMM-yyyy");

      // EDD = PO Date + 13 Days
      const eddD = new Date(d);
      eddD.setDate(d.getDate() + 13);
      poEddFormatted = Utilities.formatDate(eddD, timeZone, "dd-MMM-yyyy");
    }
  }

  // 3. ITERATE ROWS
  for (let r = 1; r < data.length; r++) {
    const row = data[r];
    const itemCode = row[idxItemCode];

    // STOP Condition
    const firstCell = row[0] ? row[0].toString() : "";
    if (firstCell.toLowerCase().includes("total")) break;

    if (!itemCode || String(itemCode).trim() === "") continue;

    // --- MAPPING ---
    const rawName = row[idxItemName];
    // Clean name: Blinkit names often have (Box)[SkuID] at the end.
    let cleanName = rawName ? rawName.toString() : "";
    if (cleanName.includes("[")) {
      cleanName = cleanName.split("[")[0].trim();
    }

    const masterSKU = findMasterSku(skuMapping, "blinkit", itemCode);
    const zohoItemId = findZohoItemId(skuMapping, "blinkit", itemCode);

    
    
    // --- NUMBERS ---
    const qty = parseFloat(row[idxQty]) || 0;
    const mrp = parseFloat(row[idxMRP]) || 0;
    const cost = parseFloat(row[idxCost]) || 0;

    totalPoValue += (qty * cost);

    tempItems.push({
      poDate: poDateFormatted,
      channel: channel,
      poNum: poNum,
      store: storeCode,
      poEDD: poEddFormatted,
      poExpiry: poExpiryFormatted,
      itemCode: itemCode,
      masterSKU: masterSKU,
      name: cleanName,
      qty: qty,
      mrp: mrp,
      cost: cost,
      pdfLink: pdfMap[poNum],
      zohoItemId : zohoItemId
    });
  }

  // 4. CHECK THRESHOLD
  const channelKey = channel.toLowerCase();
  const threshold = channelThresholds[channelKey] || 0;
  const status = (threshold > 0 && totalPoValue*1.05 < threshold) ? "Below Threshold" : "New";

  // 5. FORMAT OUTPUT
  return tempItems.map(i => [
    status,
    i.poDate,
    i.channel,
    i.poNum,
    i.store,
    i.poEDD,
    i.poExpiry,
    i.itemCode,
    i.masterSKU,
    i.name,
    i.qty,
    i.mrp.toFixed(2),
    i.cost.toFixed(2),
    i.pdfLink,
    i.zohoItemId
  ]);
}

// =================================================================================
// BIGBASKET - EXCEL PARSER (ROBUST FOR SPARSE 2D ARRAY)
// =================================================================================

/**
 * **NEW & CORRECTED:** Parses the sparse 2D array data from a BigBasket PO Excel file.
 * This function is specifically designed to "scan" each row for keywords and find
 * the corresponding values in adjacent cells.
 *
 * @param {Array<Array>} data - The full Excel data as a 2D array from getExcelDataViaBlob.
 * @return {Array<Array>} A 2D array of the parsed and formatted line items.
 */
function parseBigbasketExcel(data, channel, poNum, storeCode, skuMapping, pdfMap, channelThresholds) {
  
  let tempItems = [];
  let totalPoValue = 0;

  if (!data || data.length === 0) return [];

  // --- A. Scan for Header-Level Information ---
  let poDate = "", poExpiry = "";
  
  // First, convert the entire 2D array into a single block of text for easy searching.
  const fullText = data.map(row => row.join(',')).join('\n');

   // Use regex to find and capture the values directly from the text block.
  const poDateMatch = fullText.match(/PO Date:([^,\n]+)/i);
  if (poDateMatch && poDateMatch[1]) {
    poDate = _formatBigbasketDate(poDateMatch[1].trim());
  }

  const poExpiryMatch = fullText.match(/PO Expiry date:([^,\n]+)/i);
  if (poExpiryMatch && poExpiryMatch[1]) {
    poExpiry = _formatBigbasketDate(poExpiryMatch[1].trim());
  }
  Logger.log
  
  Logger.log(`Extracted PO Date: ${poDate}, PO Expiry: ${poExpiry}`);
  if (!poDate) {
    Logger.log("Warning: Could not find 'PO Date:' in the document.");
    // Fallback if needed, e.g., using today's date
    poDate = new Date();
  }

  // --- B. Find the Item Table Header Row ---
  let headerRowIndex = -1;
  for (let r = 0; r < data.length; r++) {
    // A more reliable way to find the header is by looking for specific, non-sparse headers.
    const row = data[r].map(h => String(h).trim());
    if (row.includes("S.No") && row.includes("SKU Code") && row.includes("Description") && row.includes("Quantity")) {
      headerRowIndex = r;
      break;
    }
  }

  if (headerRowIndex === -1) {
    Logger.log("Error in parseBigbasketExcel: Could not find the item table header row. Aborting.");
    return []; 
  }

  // --- C. Create a Dynamic Map of Header Names to Column Indexes ---
  const headerMap = {};
  data[headerRowIndex].forEach((header, index) => {
    if (header) headerMap[String(header).trim()] = index;
  });
  
  const requiredHeaders = ['SKU Code', 'Quantity', 'Basic Cost', 'MRP', 'Description'];
  for (const h of requiredHeaders) {
    if (!(h in headerMap)) {
      Logger.log(`Error: Essential column '${h}' not found in header map.`);
      return [];
    }
  }

  // --- D. Iterate Through Item Rows and Extract Data ---
  for (let r = headerRowIndex + 1; r < data.length; r++) {
    const row = data[r];
    const firstCell = String(row[0]).trim();
    
    // Stop if we hit an empty row or the "Total" row.
    if (firstCell === "" || firstCell.toLowerCase().includes("total")) {
      break;
    }
    
    const itemCode = row[headerMap['SKU Code']];
    if (!itemCode) continue;

    const masterSKU = findMasterSku(skuMapping, "bb", itemCode);
    const zohoItemId = findZohoItemId(skuMapping, "bb", itemCode);

    const qty = parseFloat(row[headerMap['Quantity']]) || 0;
    const mrp = parseFloat(row[headerMap['MRP']]) || 0;
    const cost = parseFloat(row[headerMap['Basic Cost']]) || 0;

    totalPoValue += (qty * cost);

           // First, find the original file ID from the map.
    const originalFileId = extractFileIdFromUrl(pdfMap[poNum] || "");
    Logger.log(originalFileId);
    
    // Now, get the PDF version URL using our new helper.
    const finalPdfUrl = _getOrCreatePdfVersion(originalFileId);
    Logger.log(finalPdfUrl);

    tempItems.push({
      itemCode: String(itemCode).replace(/E\d+/, ''), // Handle scientific notation like 4.035...E7
      masterSKU, 
      cleanName: String(row[headerMap['Description']]).trim(), 
      qty, mrp, cost, pdfLink: finalPdfUrl, zohoItemId
    });
  }


  //Logger.log(tempItems);

  // --- D. DETERMINE STATUS BASED ON THRESHOLD ---
  const channelKey = channel.toLowerCase();  
  // Get the threshold, defaulting to 0 if not found.
  const threshold = channelThresholds[channelKey] || 0;
    
  const status = (threshold > 0 && totalPoValue*1.05 < threshold) ? "Below Threshold" : "New";

  //Logger.log(`Total PO Value: ${totalPoValue}, Threshold: ${threshold}, Status: ${status}`);

  return tempItems.map(i => [
    status,
    poDate, 
    channel, 
    poNum, 
    storeCode,
    poExpiry,
    poExpiry,
    i.itemCode, 
    i.masterSKU, 
    i.cleanName, 
    i.qty, 
    (i.mrp || 0).toFixed(2),
    (i.cost || 0).toFixed(2),
    i.pdfLink || "", // Add a fallback for null pdfLink
    i.zohoItemId || ""      // 15 Zoho Item ID ✅
  ]);
}

/**
 * **NEW & ROBUST HELPER:** Specifically converts a 'DD/Mon/YYYY' date string
 * (e.g., '22/Dec/2025') into a standard 'YYYY-MM-DD' format.
 *
 * @param {string} dateStr - The date string from the BigBasket PO.
 * @return {string} The formatted 'YYYY-MM-DD' date string, or an empty string if invalid.
 */
function _formatBigbasketDate(dateStr) {
  Logger.log(dateStr);
  if (!dateStr || typeof dateStr !== 'string') return "";

  const parts = dateStr.split('/');
  if (parts.length !== 3) return dateStr; // Return original if format is wrong

  const day = parts[0];
  const monthStr = parts[1];
  const year = parts[2];
  
  const monthMap = {
    'Jan': '01', 'Feb': '02', 'Mar': '03', 'Apr': '04', 'May': '05', 'Jun': '06',
    'Jul': '07', 'Aug': '08', 'Sep': '09', 'Oct': '10', 'Nov': '11', 'Dec': '12'
  };
  
  const month = monthMap[monthStr];
  if (!month) return dateStr; // Return original if month is not found
  return `${year}-${month}-${day}`;
}

// You will need a robust formatDate function that can handle different formats.
function formatDate(dateString) {
    if (!dateString) return "";
    try {
        // Handles "DD/Mon/YYYY" like "22/Dec/2025" and standard formats
        const date = new Date(dateString);
        return Utilities.formatDate(date, SpreadsheetApp.getActive().getSpreadsheetTimeZone(), 'yyyy-MM-dd');
    } catch (e) {
        return dateString; // Return original if parsing fails
    }
}
// You will also need this helper function if you don't have it already.
// It's used to robustly find values in sparse rows from the Excel conversion.
function findValueInRowAfterKey(row, key) {
  const keyIndex = row.findIndex(cell => String(cell).toLowerCase().includes(key.toLowerCase()));
  if (keyIndex !== -1) {
    // Look for the first non-empty value in the cells immediately after the key.
    for (let i = keyIndex + 1; i < row.length; i++) {
      if (row[i] && String(row[i]).trim() !== "") {
        return row[i];
      }
    }
  }
  return ""; // Return empty string if not found
}

// AMAZON - B2B SHIPMENT PLAN PARSER
// =================================================================================

/**
 * **Parses the 2D array data from an Amazon B2B Shipment Plan CSV.**
 * It extracts and transforms the data to match the 15-column format required
 * by the 'PO_Database' sheet, applying all specified business rules.
 *
 * @param {Array<Array>} data - The full CSV data as a 2D array.
 * @return {Array<Array>} A 2D array of the parsed and formatted line items.
 */
function parseAmazonExcel(data,channelName,mapping) {
  if (!data || data.length < 2) {
    Logger.log("Error in parseAmazonExcel: Input data is empty or missing headers. Aborting.");
    return [];
  }

  // --- 1. Find the Header Row and Create a Dynamic Column Map ---
  const headers = data.shift().map(h => String(h).trim()); // Get headers and remove from data
  const headerMap = {};
  headers.forEach((h, i) => { if (h) headerMap[h] = i; });

  const requiredHeaders = ['sku', 'seller-sku', 'item-name', 'qty', 'declared_cost', 'FC ID', 'Shipment ID'];
  for (const h of requiredHeaders) {
    if (!(h in headerMap)) {
      Logger.log(`Error in parseAmazonExcel: Essential column '${h}' not found. Aborting.`);
      return [];
    }
  }

  // --- 2. Prepare Calculated Date Fields (do this once) ---
  const today = new Date();
  const tenDaysFromNow = new Date();
  tenDaysFromNow.setDate(today.getDate() + 10);
  
  const timezone = SpreadsheetApp.getActive().getSpreadsheetTimeZone();
  const poDate = Utilities.formatDate(today, timezone, 'yyyy-MM-dd');
  const eddAndExpiryDate = Utilities.formatDate(tenDaysFromNow, timezone, 'yyyy-MM-dd');

  // --- 3. Iterate Through Item Rows and Transform Data ---
  const finalOutput = data.map(row => {

    // Extract data using the header map
    const itemCode = row[headerMap['seller-sku']];
    const masterSKU = findMasterSku(mapping, "amazon_fba", itemCode);
    const zohoItemId = findZohoItemId(mapping, "amazon_fba", itemCode);


    const itemName = row[headerMap['item-name']];
    const quantity = parseFloat(row[headerMap['qty']]) || 0;
    const cost = parseFloat(row[headerMap['declared_cost']]) || 0;
    const shipmentId = row[headerMap['Shipment ID']];
    const fcId = row[headerMap['FC ID']];

    // Apply your business rules to create the final row
    return [
      "New",                  // Status
      poDate,                 // PO Date (today)
      "Amazon_FBA",               // Channel Name
      shipmentId,             // PO Number (from Shipment ID)
      fcId,       // Store Code ("Amazon_" + FC ID)
      eddAndExpiryDate,       // PO EDD (today + 10 days)
      eddAndExpiryDate,       // PO Expiry Date (today + 10 days)
      itemCode,               // Item Code (from sku)
      masterSKU,              // Master SKU (from seller-sku)
      itemName,               // Item Name
      quantity,               // Qty
      "-",                     // MRP (blank as requested)
      cost,                   // Unit Cost (Tax Exclusive)
      "-",                     // PO PDF (blank as requested)
      zohoItemId                      // Zoho Item ID (leave blank to be filled later)
    ];
  }).filter(Boolean); // .filter(Boolean) removes any null rows that were skipped

  Logger.log(`Successfully parsed and transformed ${finalOutput.length} items from the Amazon shipment plan.`);
  return finalOutput;
}
