/**
 * **FINAL & ROBUST:** Parses the sparse 2D array data from a Flipkart Minutes PO.
 * This version "scans" the sheet for header data instead of relying on fragile,
 * fixed cell positions (e.g., data[1][23]).
 *
 * @param {Array<Array>} data - The full Excel data as a 2D array from getExcelDataViaBlob.
 * @return {Array<Array>} A 2D array of the parsed and formatted line items.
 */

function parseFlipkartMinutesExcel(data, channelName, skuMapping,pdfMap, channelThresholds) {
  let tempItems = [];
  let totalPoValue = 0;

  if (!data || data.length < 10) {
    Logger.log("Error in parseFlipkartMinutesCsv: Input data is too short or empty.");
    return [];
  }

  // =========================================================================
  // THE FIX IS HERE: Replaced fixed cell reads with a robust scanning method.
  // =========================================================================

  // --- 1. Scan the top of the document for Header-Level Information ---
  let poDateRaw = "", poExpiryRaw = "", targetAddress = "", poNum ="";
  
  for (let r = 0; r < Math.min(data.length, 10); r++) { // Scan the first 10 rows
    const row = data[r];
    for (let c = 0; c < row.length; c++) {
      const cellValue = String(row[c]).trim();
      
      // Find keywords and then look for the value in the next non-empty cell.
      if (cellValue.includes("ORDER DATE")) {
        poDateRaw = findValueInRowAfterKey(row, "ORDER DATE");
      }
      if (cellValue.includes("PO Expiry")) {
        poExpiryRaw = findValueInRowAfterKey(row, "PO Expiry");
      }
      if (cellValue.includes("SHIPPED TO ADDRESS")) {
        targetAddress = findValueInRowAfterKey(row, "SHIPPED TO ADDRESS");
      }
      if (cellValue.includes("PO#")) {
        poNum = findValueInRowAfterKey(row, "PO#");
      }
    }
  }
  Logger.log(`Scanned Headers - PO Date: ${poDateRaw}, Expiry: ${poExpiryRaw}, Address: ${targetAddress.substring(0,30)}...`);

  const poDate = _formatFlipkartDate(poDateRaw);
  const poExpiry = _formatFlipkartDate(poExpiryRaw);

  // --- 2. Find the Store Code (No change to this logic) ---
  const storeCode = _findClosestStoreCode(targetAddress, 'FlipkartMinutes');

  // --- 3. Find the Item Table Header Row (No change to this logic) ---
  let headerRowIndex = -1;
  for (let r = 0; r < data.length; r++) {
    const rowStr = data[r].join(",").toLowerCase();
    if (rowStr.includes("s. no.") && rowStr.includes("fsn/isbn13") && rowStr.includes("supplier price")) {
      headerRowIndex = r;
      break;
    }
  }
  if (headerRowIndex === -1) {
    Logger.log("Error: Could not find item table header row in Flipkart Minutes CSV.");
    return [];
  }
  
  // --- 4. Create Header Map (No change) ---
  const headerMap = {};
  data[headerRowIndex].forEach((h, i) => { if (h) headerMap[String(h).trim()] = i; });
  
  // ... (The rest of your function from Step 5 onwards is correct and does not need to change)

  // --- 5. Iterate Through Item Rows and Extract All Details ---
  for (let r = headerRowIndex + 1; r < data.length; r++) {
    const row = data[r];
    const itemCode = row[headerMap['FSN/ISBN13']];
    if (!itemCode || String(itemCode).trim() === "" || String(row[0]).toLowerCase().includes('total')) break;

    const masterSKU = findMasterSku(skuMapping, "flipkartminutes", itemCode);

    const zohoItemId = findZohoItemId(skuMapping, "flipkartminutes", itemCode);
    const qty = parseFloat(row[headerMap['Quantity']]) || 0;
    const mrp = parseFloat(String(row[headerMap['Supplier MRP']]).replace(' INR', '')) || 0;
    const cost =(parseFloat(String(row[headerMap['Supplier Price']]).replace(' INR', '')) || 0) / 1.05;
    totalPoValue += (qty * cost);

    
    // First, find the original file ID from the map.
    const originalFileId = extractFileIdFromUrl(pdfMap[poNum] || "");
    Logger.log(originalFileId);
    
    // Now, get the PDF version URL using our new helper.
    const finalPdfUrl = _getOrCreatePdfVersion(originalFileId);
    Logger.log(finalPdfUrl);

    tempItems.push({
      poDate, channel: channelName, poNum, storeCode, poEDD: poExpiry, poExpiry, 
      itemCode, masterSKU,
      cleanName: String(row[headerMap['Title']]).trim(),
      qty, mrp, cost,
      pdfLink: finalPdfUrl,zohoItemId
    });
  }

  // --- 6 & 7. Determine Status and Map to Final Array ---
  const channelKey = channelName.toLowerCase();
  const threshold = channelThresholds[channelKey] || 0;
  const status = (threshold > 0 && (parseFloat(totalPoValue.toFixed(2)) * 1.05) < threshold) ? "Below Threshold" : "New";

  return tempItems.map(i => [
    status, formatDate(i.poDate), i.channel, i.poNum, i.storeCode,
    formatDate(i.poEDD), formatDate(i.poExpiry),
    i.itemCode, i.masterSKU, i.cleanName, i.qty, 
    (i.mrp || 0).toFixed(2), (i.cost || 0).toFixed(2),
    i.pdfLink || "", i.zohoItemId || ""
  ]);
}

// =================================================================================
// FILE CONVERSION HELPER
// =================================================================================

/**
 * **NEW HELPER:** Takes a Google Drive file ID, checks its type, and returns a
 * URL to a PDF version. If the original is an Excel file, it converts it to PDF,
 * saves it to a designated archive folder, and returns the new PDF's URL.
 *
 * @param {string} fileId - The ID of the file to process.
 * @return {string} The URL of the PDF version of the file.
 */
/**
 * **FINAL & CORRECTED:** Takes a Google Drive file ID and returns a URL to a
 * PDF version. It now correctly handles native Excel files (.xls/.xlsx) by first
 * converting them to a temporary Google Sheet, and then converting that sheet to a PDF.
 *
 * @param {string} fileId - The ID of the original file (e.g., the .xls file).
 * @return {string} The URL of the PDF version of the file.
 */
function _getOrCreatePdfVersion(fileId) {
  if (!fileId) {
    Logger.log("Warning in _getOrCreatePdfVersion: Received an empty fileId.");
    return "";
  }
  
  let tempSheetId = null; // Variable to hold the ID of the temporary Google Sheet

  try {
    const originalFile = DriveApp.getFileById(fileId);
    const originalMimeType = originalFile.getMimeType();
    
    // Case 1: The file is already a PDF. Nothing to do.
    if (originalMimeType === MimeType.PDF) {
      return originalFile.getUrl();
    }
    
    // --- The Two-Step Conversion Process ---
    const convertibleMimeTypes = [
      MimeType.MICROSOFT_EXCEL,
      MimeType.MICROSOFT_EXCEL_LEGACY,
      MimeType.CSV
    ];
    
    if (convertibleMimeTypes.includes(originalMimeType)) {
      Logger.log(`File ID ${fileId} is a spreadsheet. Starting two-step conversion to PDF...`);
      
      // Step 1: Convert the Excel/CSV file to a temporary Google Sheet.
      // This uses the same robust logic as your getExcelDataViaBlob function.
      const resource = {
        title: "Temp_PDF_Conversion_" + new Date().getTime(),
        mimeType: MimeType.GOOGLE_SHEETS
      };
      const tempFile = Drive.Files.insert(resource, originalFile.getBlob(), {convert: true});
      tempSheetId = tempFile.id; // Store the ID so we can delete it later

      if (!tempSheetId) {
        throw new Error("Failed to create the temporary Google Sheet for conversion.");
      }

      // Step 2: Convert the NEW temporary Google Sheet to a PDF Blob.
      const tempSheetFile = DriveApp.getFileById(tempSheetId);
      const pdfBlob = tempSheetFile.getAs(MimeType.PDF);
      
      // --- Now, save the final PDF to your archive ---
      const archiveFolder = DriveApp.getFolderById(DRIVE_FOLDER_ID);
      
      const newPdfName = originalFile.getName().replace(/\.(xlsx?|xls|csv)$/i, '.pdf');
      
      // Check for and return existing file to avoid duplicates.
      const existingFiles = archiveFolder.getFilesByName(newPdfName);
      if (existingFiles.hasNext()) {
          const existingPdf = existingFiles.next();
          Logger.log(`A PDF with the name "${newPdfName}" already exists. Returning its URL.`);
          return existingPdf.getUrl();
      }

      const finalPdfFile = archiveFolder.createFile(pdfBlob).setName(newPdfName);
      const finalPdfUrl = finalPdfFile.getUrl();
      
      Logger.log(`Successfully converted to PDF. New file URL: ${finalPdfUrl}`);
      return finalPdfUrl;
    }

    // Case 3: Not a convertible type. Return the original URL.
    return originalFile.getUrl();

  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log(`Error in _getOrCreatePdfVersion for file ID ${fileId}: ${e.message}`);
    return "";
  } finally {
    // --- CRITICAL CLEANUP STEP ---
    // This 'finally' block ensures that the temporary Google Sheet is ALWAYS
    // deleted, even if an error occurs during the process.
    if (tempSheetId) {
      try {
        Drive.Files.remove(tempSheetId);
        Logger.log(`Successfully cleaned up temporary sheet with ID: ${tempSheetId}`);
      } catch (cleanupError) {
        Logger.log(`WARNING: Failed to clean up temporary sheet with ID: ${tempSheetId}. Error: ${cleanupError.message}`);
      }
    }
  }
}


/**
 * **HELPER 1:** Finds the best matching store code by comparing an address string
 * against a filtered list of customers from the EE_Customers sheet.
 * @param {string} targetAddress - The address to find a match for.
 * @param {string} filterKeyword - The keyword to filter customers by (e.g., 'FlipkartMinutes').
 * @return {string} The Company Name of the best match, or "Not Found".
 */
/**
 * **UPDATED:** Finds the best matching store code and now processes the result
 * to remove the 'filterKeyword_' prefix, returning only the store's specific name.
 *
 * @param {string} targetAddress - The address to find a match for.
 * @param {string} filterKeyword - The keyword to filter customers by (e.g., 'FlipkartMinutes').
 * @return {string} The processed Company Name of the best match, or "Not Found".
 */
function _findClosestStoreCode(targetAddress, filterKeyword) {
  const customerSheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName('EE_Customers');
  if (!customerSheet) return "EE_Customers sheet not found";

  const data = customerSheet.getDataRange().getValues();
  const headers = data.shift();
  const nameIndex = headers.indexOf('Company Name');
  const addressIndex = headers.indexOf('Billing Street');

  if (nameIndex === -1 || addressIndex === -1) return "Required columns not found in EE_Customers";

  // Filter for relevant customers (no change here)
  const candidates = data
    .filter(row => String(row[nameIndex]).includes(filterKeyword))
    .map(row => ({ name: row[nameIndex], address: row[addressIndex] }));

  if (candidates.length === 0) return "No matching customers found";

  let bestMatch = { name: "Not Found", score: 0.0 };

  // Find the best match (no change here)
  candidates.forEach(candidate => {
    const score = _calculateStringSimilarity(targetAddress, candidate.address);
    if (score > bestMatch.score) {
      bestMatch = { name: candidate.name, score: score };
    }
  });

  Logger.log(`Closest store match found: "${bestMatch.name}" with a score of ${bestMatch.score.toFixed(2)}`);

  // =========================================================================
  // THE FIX IS HERE
  // =========================================================================
  
  // If a good match was found, process the name to remove the prefix.
  if (bestMatch.name !== "Not Found") {
    // Create a case-insensitive regular expression to find the keyword and the underscore.
    // For example, if filterKeyword is "FlipkartMinutes", this will look for "FlipkartMinutes_".
    const prefixToRemove = new RegExp(filterKeyword + "_", "i"); 
    
    // Replace the found prefix with an empty string and trim any extra whitespace.
    const finalStoreName = bestMatch.name.replace(prefixToRemove, "").trim();
    
    Logger.log(`Returning processed store name: "${finalStoreName}"`);
    return finalStoreName;
  } else {
    // If no match was found, just return "Not Found".
    return bestMatch.name;
  }
}

/**
 * **HELPER 2:** Calculates a similarity score between two strings (Levenshtein distance).
 * A score of 1.0 is a perfect match.
 * @return {number} The similarity score between 0.0 and 1.0.
 */
function _calculateStringSimilarity(s1, s2) {
  let longer = s1, shorter = s2;
  if (s1.length < s2.length) { longer = s2; shorter = s1; }
  const longerLength = longer.length;
  if (longerLength === 0) return 1.0;
  return (longerLength - editDistance(longer, shorter)) / parseFloat(longerLength);
  
  function editDistance(s1, s2) {
    s1 = s1.toLowerCase(); s2 = s2.toLowerCase();
    const costs = [];
    for (let i = 0; i <= s1.length; i++) {
      let lastValue = i;
      for (let j = 0; j <= s2.length; j++) {
        if (i === 0) costs[j] = j;
        else if (j > 0) {
          let newValue = costs[j - 1];
          if (s1.charAt(i - 1) !== s2.charAt(j - 1))
            newValue = Math.min(Math.min(newValue, lastValue), costs[j]) + 1;
          costs[j - 1] = lastValue;
          lastValue = newValue;
        }
      }
      if (i > 0) costs[s2.length] = lastValue;
    }
    return costs[s2.length];
  }
}


/**
 * **HELPER 3:** Converts a 'DD-MM-YY' date string (e.g., '26-12-25')
 * into a standard 'YYYY-MM-DD' format.
 * @param {string} dateStr - The date string from the Flipkart PO.
 * @return {string} The formatted date string.
 */
function _formatFlipkartDate(dateStr) {
  if (!dateStr || typeof dateStr !== 'string') return "";
  const parts = dateStr.split('-');
  if (parts.length !== 3) return dateStr;
  
  const day = parts[0];
  const month = parts[1];
  const year = "20" + parts[2]; // Add "20" to the 'YY' part
  
  // Reassemble in a format that new Date() can reliably parse
  const parsableDate = new Date(`${year}-${month}-${day}`);
  if (isNaN(parsableDate.getTime())) return dateStr;

  return Utilities.formatDate(parsableDate, SpreadsheetApp.getActive().getSpreadsheetTimeZone(), 'yyyy-MM-dd');
}

// ==========================================
// 6. AUTOMATION: INVENTORY & EASYECOM SYNC 
// ==========================================

/**
 * **FINAL & OPTIMIZED:** This single function performs the entire end-to-end process:
 * 1. Fetches the latest inventory and product details from the external EasyEcom sheet.
 * 2. Updates the 'Master_SKU_Mapping' sheet with this fresh inventory and details.
 * 3. Performs FIFO allocation and price checks on the 'PO_Database' sheet.
 */
function syncInventoryAndCalculateAllocation() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const mapSheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_INVENTORY);
  const dbSheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_PO_DB);

  updateMasterSkuInventory();

  Logger.log("Starting Phase 2: FIFO Allocation & Price Check...");

  // 1. Load Updated Mapping Data (Inventory, Prices, Zoho Item ID) into memory
  const mapData = mapSheet.getDataRange().getValues();
  const inventoryMap = new Map(); // Key: MasterSKU, Value: Qty
  const priceMap = new Map();     // Key: Channel|MasterSKU, Value: SellingPrice
  const zohoItemMap = new Map();  // Key: MasterSKU, Value: Zoho Item ID

  mapData.slice(1).forEach(row => {
    const channel = String(row[0]).toLowerCase().trim();
    const sku = String(row[2]).trim();
    const sellingPrice = Number(row[3]) || 0;
    const qty = Number(row[4]) || 0;
    const zohoItemId = String(row[9]).trim(); // Column J

    if (sku) {
      inventoryMap.set(sku, qty);
      zohoItemMap.set(sku, zohoItemId);

      if (channel) {
        priceMap.set(`${channel}|${sku}`, sellingPrice);
      }
    }
  });

  // 2. Load PO Database
  const dbLastRow = dbSheet.getLastRow();
  if (dbLastRow < 2) return;

  const dbRange = dbSheet.getRange(2, 1, dbLastRow - 1, 20);
  const dbData = dbRange.getValues();

  // 3. Sort eligible orders by date (FIFO)
  const newOrders = dbData
    .map((row, index) => ({ row, index }))
    .filter(({ row }) => {
      const status = String(row[0]).toLowerCase().trim();
      const eeRefId = String(row[19]).trim();
      return (status === 'new' || status === 'confirmed') && eeRefId === '';
    })
    .sort((a, b) => new Date(a.row[1]) - new Date(b.row[1]));

  // 4. Reset allocation for waiting for confirmation
  dbData.forEach((row, index) => {
    const status = String(row[0]).toLowerCase().trim();
    const eeRefId = String(row[19]).trim();

    if (status === 'waiting for confirmation' && eeRefId === '') {
      dbData[index][15] = 0; // Fulfillable Qty
    }
  });

  // 5. Allocate Inventory + update Zoho Item ID
  newOrders.forEach(({ row, index }) => {
    const sku = String(row[8]).trim();
    const reqQty = Number(row[10]) || 0;
    let available = inventoryMap.get(sku) || 0;
    let fulfillable = 0;

    if (available >= reqQty) {
      fulfillable = reqQty;
      inventoryMap.set(sku, available - reqQty);
    } else {
      fulfillable = available;
      inventoryMap.set(sku, 0);
    }

    dbData[index][15] = fulfillable;                 // Fulfillable Qty
    dbData[index][14] = zohoItemMap.get(sku) || ""; // Zoho Item ID
  });

  // 6. Prepare Final Output
  const finalOutput = dbData.map(row => {
    const eeRefId = String(row[19]).trim();
    const poStatus = String(row[0]).toLowerCase().trim();

    let priceCheckVal = row[16]; // existing value by default

    if ((poStatus === 'new' || poStatus === 'confirmed') && eeRefId === '') {
      const channelName = String(row[2]).toLowerCase().trim();
      const masterSku = String(row[8]).trim();
      const unitCost = Number(row[12]) || 0;
      const priceKey = `${channelName}|${masterSku}`;
      const expectedPrice = priceMap.get(priceKey);

      if (expectedPrice === undefined) {
        priceCheckVal = "Price Not Found";
      } else {
        const costRounded = Math.round(unitCost);
        const expRounded = Math.round(expectedPrice);
        priceCheckVal =
          costRounded === expRounded
            ? "Match"
            : `Mismatch (PO:${costRounded} vs Exp:${expRounded})`;
      }
    }

    return [row[14], row[15], priceCheckVal]; // Zoho Item ID, Fulfillable Qty, Price Check
  });

  // 7. Write back columns 15,16,17
  dbSheet.getRange(2, 15, finalOutput.length, 3).setValues(finalOutput);

  Logger.log("Phase 2 Complete: FIFO Allocation, Zoho Item ID & Price Checks Updated.");
  SpreadsheetApp.flush();

  fetchEasyEcomShipments();
}

function manual_sync_inventory_allocation() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const mapSheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_INVENTORY);
  const dbSheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_PO_DB);

  Logger.log("Starting Manual FIFO Inventory Allocation...");

  /* ======================================================
     STEP 1: LOAD INVENTORY INTO MEMORY
  ====================================================== */

  const mapData = mapSheet.getDataRange().getValues();
  const inventoryMap = new Map(); // MasterSKU → Available Qty

  mapData.slice(1).forEach(row => {
    const sku = String(row[2]).trim();
    const qty = Number(row[4]) || 0;

    if (sku) inventoryMap.set(sku, qty);
  });

  /* ======================================================
     STEP 2: LOAD PO DATABASE
  ====================================================== */

  const dbLastRow = dbSheet.getLastRow();
  if (dbLastRow < 2) return;

  const dbRange = dbSheet.getRange(2, 1, dbLastRow - 1, 20);
  const dbData = dbRange.getValues();

  /* ======================================================
     STEP 2.5: RESET ALLOCATION FOR WAITING CONFIRMATION
  ====================================================== */

  dbData.forEach((row, index) => {
    const status = String(row[0]).toLowerCase().trim();
    const eeRefId = String(row[19]).trim();

    if (status === 'waiting for confirmation' && eeRefId === '') {
      dbData[index][15] = 0; // Fulfillable Qty
    }
  });

  /* ======================================================
     STEP 3: FILTER FIFO ELIGIBLE ORDERS
  ====================================================== */

  const fifoOrders = dbData
    .map((row, index) => ({ row, index }))
    .filter(({ row }) => {
      const status = String(row[0]).toLowerCase().trim();
      const eeRefId = String(row[19]).trim();
      return (status === 'new' || status === 'confirmed') && eeRefId === '';
    })
    .sort((a, b) => new Date(a.row[1]) - new Date(b.row[1]));

  /* ======================================================
     STEP 4: FIFO INVENTORY ALLOCATION
  ====================================================== */

  fifoOrders.forEach(({ row, index }) => {
    const sku = String(row[8]).trim();
    const reqQty = Number(row[10]) || 0;
    let available = inventoryMap.get(sku) || 0;

    const fulfillable = Math.min(reqQty, available);
    inventoryMap.set(sku, available - fulfillable);

    dbData[index][15] = fulfillable; // Fulfillable Qty
  });

  /* ======================================================
     STEP 5: WRITE BACK (ONLY FULFILLABLE QTY)
  ====================================================== */

  const allocationOutput = dbData.map(row => [row[15]]);
  dbSheet.getRange(2, 16, allocationOutput.length, 1).setValues(allocationOutput);

  Logger.log("Manual FIFO Inventory Allocation Completed.");
  SpreadsheetApp.flush();
}

/**
 * **NEW FUNCTION 1: Updates Customer IDs.**
 * This function reads the PO_Database and efficiently updates any blank
 * 'EE Customer ID' and 'Zoho Contact ID' columns by looking them up.
 */
function updateCustomerIdsInPoDatabase() {
  Logger.log("--- Starting Customer ID & GST Update Process (Selective Update) ---");

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const dbSheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_PO_DB);
  const eeCustSheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_EE_CUSTOMERS);
  const zohoCustSheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_ZOHO_CUSTOMERS);

  if (dbSheet.getLastRow() < 2) return;

  /* ---------- STEP 1: BUILD LOOKUP MAPS ---------- */

  // EE Map: channel_store → EE Customer ID
  const eeCustomerMap = new Map();
  eeCustSheet.getDataRange().getValues().slice(1).forEach(row => {
    if (row[1] && row[0]) {
      const key = String(row[1]).toLowerCase().trim();
      eeCustomerMap.set(key, String(row[0]).trim());
    }
  });

  // Zoho Map: channel_store → { contactId, gst }
  const zohoCustomerMap = new Map();
  zohoCustSheet.getDataRange().getValues().slice(1).forEach(row => {
    if (row[1]) {
      const key = String(row[1]).toLowerCase().trim();
      zohoCustomerMap.set(key, {
        contactId: String(row[0] || "").trim(),
        gst: String(row[11] || "").trim() // GST column
      });
    }
  });

  /* ---------- STEP 2: READ PO DATABASE ---------- */

  const dataRange = dbSheet.getDataRange();
  const values = dataRange.getValues();
  const headers = values[0];

  const channelIndex     = headers.indexOf("Channel Name");
  const storeCodeIndex   = headers.indexOf("Store Code");
  const eeCustIdIndex    = headers.indexOf("EE Customer ID");
  const zohoCustIdIndex  = headers.indexOf("Zoho Contact ID");
  const gstIndex         = headers.indexOf("GST");

  if ([channelIndex, storeCodeIndex, eeCustIdIndex, zohoCustIdIndex, gstIndex].includes(-1)) {
    throw new Error("Required columns missing in PO_Database");
  }

  let updatesMade = 0;

  /* ---------- STEP 3: UPDATE ONLY REQUIRED CELLS ---------- */

  for (let i = 1; i < values.length; i++) {
    const row = values[i];

    const eeId   = row[eeCustIdIndex];
    const zohoId = row[zohoCustIdIndex];
    const gst    = row[gstIndex];

    // Skip rows where nothing is missing
    if (eeId && zohoId && gst) continue;

    const channelName = String(row[channelIndex]).trim();
    const storeCode   = String(row[storeCodeIndex]).trim();
    const lookupKey   = `${channelName}_${storeCode}`.toLowerCase();

    const sheetRow = i + 1; // 1-based row index

    // EE Customer ID
    if (!eeId && eeCustomerMap.has(lookupKey)) {
      dbSheet.getRange(sheetRow, eeCustIdIndex + 1)
        .setValue(eeCustomerMap.get(lookupKey));
      updatesMade++;
    }

    // Zoho Contact ID + GST
    if (zohoCustomerMap.has(lookupKey)) {
      const zohoData = zohoCustomerMap.get(lookupKey);

      if (!zohoId && zohoData.contactId) {
        dbSheet.getRange(sheetRow, zohoCustIdIndex + 1)
          .setValue(zohoData.contactId);
        updatesMade++;
      }

      if (!gst && zohoData.gst) {
        dbSheet.getRange(sheetRow, gstIndex + 1)
          .setValue(zohoData.gst);
        updatesMade++;
      }
    }
  }

  Logger.log(
    updatesMade > 0
      ? `Successfully updated ${updatesMade} individual cells`
      : "No Customer IDs or GST values needed updating"
  );
}


function getBranchIdByGstFast_(gstNumber) {
  if (!gstNumber) return null;

  const raw = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().getProperty("BRANCH_GST_MAP");
  if (!raw) throw new Error("Branch GST map not cached. Run cacheBranchGstMap_()");

  const map = JSON.parse(raw);
  return map[String(gstNumber).trim().toUpperCase()] || null;
}


function _cacheBranchGstMap() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const sheet = ss.getSheetByName("Branch List");
  if (!sheet) throw new Error("Branch List sheet not found");

  const data = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
  const headers = data.shift();

  const gstIndex = headers.indexOf("Tax Reg No");
  const branchIdIndex = headers.indexOf("Branch Id");
  const vendorIdIndex = headers.indexOf("Vendor ID");
  const branchNameIndex = headers.indexOf("Branch Name");

  if (
    gstIndex === -1 ||
    branchIdIndex === -1 ||
    vendorIdIndex === -1 ||
    branchNameIndex === -1
  ) {
    throw new Error(
      "Required columns missing in Branch List. Required: Tax Reg No, Branch Id, Vendor ID, Branch Name"
    );
  }

  const mapObj = {};
  const stateMapObj = {};

  data.forEach(row => {
    const gst = String(row[gstIndex] || "").trim().toUpperCase();
    const branchId = String(row[branchIdIndex] || "").trim();
    const vendorId = String(row[vendorIdIndex] || "").trim();
    const branchName = String(row[branchNameIndex] || "").trim();

    if (!gst || !branchId) return;

    const stateCode = getZohoStateCodeFromGstOrState_(gst);

    const branchData = {
      gst: gst,
      branchId: branchId,
      vendorId: vendorId,
      branchName: branchName,
      stateCode: stateCode
    };

    // GST-wise lookup
    mapObj[gst] = branchData;

    // State-wise lookup: CG, GJ, MH etc.
    if (stateCode) {
      stateMapObj[stateCode] = branchData;
    }
  });

  const props = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();

  props.setProperty("BRANCH_GST_MAP", JSON.stringify(mapObj));
  props.setProperty("BRANCH_STATE_MAP", JSON.stringify(stateMapObj));

  Logger.log(`Cached ${Object.keys(mapObj).length} GST → Branch mappings`);
  Logger.log(`Cached ${Object.keys(stateMapObj).length} State → Branch mappings`);
}
function getBranchIdByGstFast_(gstNumber) {
  if (!gstNumber) return null;

  const raw = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().getProperty("BRANCH_GST_MAP");
  if (!raw) throw new Error("Branch GST map not cached. Run cacheBranchGstMap_()");

  const map = JSON.parse(raw);
  return map[String(gstNumber).trim().toUpperCase()] || null;
}


function updateShipmentDetailsInPoDatabase() {
  Logger.log("--- Starting Shipment Details Update Process (Selective Update) ---");

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const dbSheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_PO_DB);
  const shipSheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_EE_SHIPMENTS);

  if (shipSheet.getLastRow() < 2 || dbSheet.getLastRow() < 2) return;

  /* ---------- STEP 1: BUILD SHIPMENT MAP (AGGREGATED) ---------- */

  const shipmentMap = new Map();
const shipData = shipSheet.getDataRange().getValues();
const shipHeaders = shipData.shift();

const idxRefCode      = shipHeaders.indexOf('reference_code');
const idxSku          = shipHeaders.indexOf('item_sku');
const idxItemQty      = shipHeaders.indexOf('item_item_quantity');
const idxCancelledQty = shipHeaders.indexOf('item_cancelled_quantity');
const idxShippedQty   = shipHeaders.indexOf('item_shipped_quantity');
const idxReturnedQty  = shipHeaders.indexOf('item_returned_quantity');

const idxOrderDate    = shipHeaders.indexOf('order_date');
const idxOrderId      = shipHeaders.indexOf('order_id');
const idxOrderStatus  = shipHeaders.indexOf('order_status');
const idxBatch        = shipHeaders.indexOf('batch_created_at');
const idxInvoice      = shipHeaders.indexOf('invoice_date');
const idxManifest     = shipHeaders.indexOf('manifest_date');
const idxItemStatus   = shipHeaders.indexOf('item_item_status');

shipData.forEach(row => {

  const ref = String(row[idxRefCode]).trim().toLowerCase();
  const sku = String(row[idxSku]).trim().toLowerCase();
  const key = `${ref}|${sku}`;

  const cancelledQty = Number(row[idxCancelledQty]) || 0;
  const shippedQty   = Number(row[idxShippedQty]) || 0;

  if (!shipmentMap.has(key)) {

    shipmentMap.set(key, {
      reference_code: row[idxRefCode],
      order_date: row[idxOrderDate],
      order_id: row[idxOrderId],
      order_status: row[idxOrderStatus],
      batch_created_at: row[idxBatch],
      invoice_date: row[idxInvoice],
      manifest_date: row[idxManifest],
      item_item_status: row[idxItemStatus],
      item_item_quantity: Number(row[idxItemQty]) || 0,
      item_cancelled_quantity: cancelledQty,
      item_shipped_quantity: shippedQty,
      item_returned_quantity: Number(row[idxReturnedQty]) || 0
    });

  } else {

    const existing = shipmentMap.get(key);

    existing.item_item_quantity += Number(row[idxItemQty]) || 0;
    existing.item_cancelled_quantity += cancelledQty;
    existing.item_shipped_quantity += shippedQty;
    existing.item_returned_quantity += Number(row[idxReturnedQty]) || 0;

    // Always prefer non-cancelled rows for lifecycle fields
    if (cancelledQty === 0) {
      existing.order_status = row[idxOrderStatus];
      existing.batch_created_at = row[idxBatch];
      existing.invoice_date = row[idxInvoice];
      existing.manifest_date = row[idxManifest];
      existing.item_item_status = row[idxItemStatus];
    }
  }

});
  /* ---------- STEP 2: READ PO DATABASE ---------- */

  const dbRange = dbSheet.getDataRange();
  const dbValues = dbRange.getValues();
  const dbHeaders = dbValues[0];

  const dbEeRefCodeIndex = dbHeaders.indexOf("EE Order Ref ID");
  const dbMasterSkuIndex = dbHeaders.indexOf("Master SKU");
  const startUpdateIndex = dbHeaders.indexOf("EE_reference_code");

  if ([dbEeRefCodeIndex, dbMasterSkuIndex, startUpdateIndex].includes(-1)) {
    throw new Error("Required shipment columns missing in PO_Database");
  }

  let updatedCellCount = 0;

  /* ---------- STEP 3: UPDATE ONLY REQUIRED CELLS ---------- */

  for (let i = 1; i < dbValues.length; i++) {
    const row = dbValues[i];
    const lookupKey =
      `${String(row[dbEeRefCodeIndex]).trim().toLowerCase()}|${String(row[dbMasterSkuIndex]).trim().toLowerCase()}`;

    if (!shipmentMap.has(lookupKey)) continue;

    const details = shipmentMap.get(lookupKey);
    const sheetRow = i + 1;

    const updates = [
      details.reference_code,
      details.order_date,
      details.order_id,
      details.order_status,
      details.batch_created_at,
      details.invoice_date,
      details.manifest_date,
      details.item_item_status,
      details.item_item_quantity,
      details.item_cancelled_quantity,
      details.item_shipped_quantity,
      details.item_returned_quantity
    ];

    updates.forEach((val, offset) => {
      if (val !== "" && val !== null && val !== undefined) {
        dbSheet
          .getRange(sheetRow, startUpdateIndex + 1 + offset)
          .setValue(val);
        updatedCellCount++;
      }
    });
  }

  Logger.log(
    updatedCellCount > 0
      ? `Successfully updated ${updatedCellCount} shipment-related cells`
      : "No matching shipment rows required updates"
  );
}

/**
 * **NEW FUNCTION 2: Updates Shipment Details.**
 * This function performs a targeted update, modifying only the shipment-related
 * columns for rows that have new data in the 'SHEET_EE_SHIPMENTS' sheet.

/**
 * **REVISED & UPGRADED:** This function now acts as a master orchestrator.
 * It inspects the channel name from the incoming data and decides whether to
 * create an EasyEcom B2B order or an Amazon FBA Inbound Shipment Plan.
 *
 * @param {object} data - The data object from the front-end. It MUST include a
 *   'channelName' property (e.g., 'Amazon_FBA' or 'Zepto').
 * @return {object} A standard JSON response for the front-end.
 */
function pushToEasyEcom(data) 
{
  try {

    // --- Input Validation ---
    if (!data || !data.poNumber || !data.items || !data.channel) {
      throw new Error(
        "Invalid data received. Required properties are: poNumber, items, channel."
      );
    }

    const channel = data.channel.toLowerCase();

    

    let poRef = data.poNumber;
    if (data.isPartial) {
      poRef = getNextPoVariant(data.poNumber);
    }

    let amazonResult = null;
    let easyEcomResult = null;

    // SHIPPING CHARGE
    const shippingCharge = Number(data.shippingCharge || 0);
    const locationKey = data.locationKey;
  // ==========================================================
    // WORKFLOW A — Amazon FBA (only if channel = amazon_fba)
    // ==========================================================
    if (channel === 'amazon_fba' && (!data.pushTarget||data.pushTarget==='AMZ')) {

      Logger.log(
        `Channel is 'amazon_fba'. Creating Amazon FBA inbound shipment for PO: ${data.poNumber}`
      );

      amazonResult = createAmazonFbaInboundPlan(data, poRef);

      if (amazonResult?.status !== 'success') {

        throw new Error(
          `Amazon FBA workflow failed: ${amazonResult?.message || 'Unknown error'}`
        );

      }
      if(data.pushTarget==='AMZ'){
        return responseJSON({
          status: 'success',
          message:'Amazon FBA workflow completed successfully',
          data:{
            amazon:amazonResult,
            easyecom:null
          }
        });
      }

    }
    
    // ==========================================================
    // WORKFLOW B — EasyEcom (runs for ALL channels incl. amazon_fba)
    // ==========================================================
    if(!data.pushTarget||data.pushTarget==='EE'){
    Logger.log(
      `Pushing PO to EasyEcom for channel '${channel}', PO: ${poRef}`
    );

    const formattedItems = data.items.map(item => ({
      Sku: item.masterSku || item.articleCode,
      Quantity: Number(item.qty),
      Price: Number(item.unitCost || 0.01)
    }));


    easyEcomResult = createEasyEcomB2BOrder(
      poRef,
      data.eeCustomerId,
      formattedItems,
      shippingCharge,   // ✅ added shipping charge,
      locationKey
    );


    const eeMessage = (easyEcomResult.message || "").toLowerCase();

    const isAlreadyExists =
      eeMessage.includes("already exists") ||
      eeMessage.includes("order number") && eeMessage.includes("exists");


    if (easyEcomResult.status === 'success' || isAlreadyExists) {

      updatePOStatus(data.poNumber, "New");

      Logger.log(
        isAlreadyExists
          ? `EasyEcom order already exists for PO ${poRef}. Treating as success.`
          : `EasyEcom order created successfully for PO ${poRef}`
      );

      // Update PO flag
      updatePoDatabaseFlag(data.poNumber, poRef, data.items);

    } else {

      throw new Error(
        `EasyEcom order creation failed: ${easyEcomResult.message}`
      );

    }
  }



  

    // ==========================================================
    // FINAL RESPONSE
    // ==========================================================
    return responseJSON({
      status: 'success',
      message: 'Amazon (if applicable) and EasyEcom workflows completed successfully',
      data: {
        amazon: amazonResult,
        easyecom: easyEcomResult
      }
    });

  } catch (e) {

    Logger.log(`CRITICAL ERROR in pushToEasyEcom: ${e.message}`);

    return responseJSON({
      status: 'error',
      message: e.message
    });

  }
}

function updatePoDatabaseFlag(originalPoNum, generatedRef, items) {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const sheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_PO_DB); // 'PO_Database'
  if (!sheet) return;

  const lastRow = sheet.getLastRow();
  if (lastRow < 2) return;

  // READ DATA (Columns A to AD)
  // Assuming 'EE Order Push' is Column 30 (AD) - Adjust if different
  const COL_PO_NUM = 3; // Column D (Index 3)
  const COL_SKU = 8;    // Column I (Index 8)
  const COL_FLAG = 32;  
  // Fetch PO Numbers and SKUs to find matches
  const range = sheet.getRange(2, 1, lastRow - 1, COL_FLAG);
  const values = range.getValues();
  
  // Create a Set of SKUs that were pushed (to only flag specific items if partial)
  const pushedSkus = new Set(items.map(i => String(i.masterSku || i.articleCode).trim()));
  
  

  for (let i = 0; i < values.length; i++) {
    const rowPo = String(values[i][COL_PO_NUM]).trim();
    const rowSku = String(values[i][COL_SKU]).trim();

    // MATCH: Same PO Number AND SKU is in the pushed list
    if (rowPo === String(originalPoNum).trim() && pushedSkus.has(rowSku)) {
      // Update the Flag Column (Row is i + 2 because of header + 0-index)
      sheet.getRange(i + 2, COL_FLAG).setValue(generatedRef);
      
    }
  }
  
  console.log(`Updated PO Database flag for ${originalPoNum} -> ${generatedRef}`);
}

function getNextPoVariant(basePoNumber) {

  // 🔐 Always normalize input first
  const basePo = String(basePoNumber || "").trim();

  if (!basePo) {
    throw new Error("Invalid basePoNumber passed to getNextPoVariant");
  }

  const sheet = SpreadsheetApp
    .openById(SPREADSHEET_ID)
    .getSheetByName(SHEET_SHIPMENT_LOG);

  if (!sheet) return basePo + "-1";

  const lastRow = sheet.getLastRow();
  if (lastRow < 2) return basePo + "-1";

  // Get PO Number column (Column 2)
  const poNumbers = sheet
    .getRange(2, 2, lastRow - 1, 1)
    .getValues()
    .flat();

  let maxSuffix = 0;

  // Escape basePo for regex safety
  const escapedBase = basePo.replace(/[.*+?^${}()|[\]\\]/g, '\\$&');
  const regex = new RegExp(`^${escapedBase}-(\\d+)$`, 'i');

  poNumbers.forEach(po => {
    const strPo = String(po || "").trim();
    const match = strPo.match(regex);

    if (match) {
      const suffix = parseInt(match[1], 10);
      if (suffix > maxSuffix) maxSuffix = suffix;
    }
  });

  return basePo + "-" + (maxSuffix + 1);
}

// ==========================================
// CORE LOGIC: Create Order in EasyEcom
// ==========================================

function createEasyEcomB2BOrder(poRef, customerId, items, shippingCharge = 0, locationKey = null) {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  
  // 1. Fetch & Clean Address
  const addressDetails = getCustomerAddressFromSheet(ss, customerId);
  
  if (!addressDetails) {
    return { status: 'error', message: `Customer ID ${customerId} not found in EE_Customers.` };
  }

  // 2. Prepare Dates
  const timeZone = Session.getScriptTimeZone();
  const now = new Date();
  const deliveryDate = new Date();
  deliveryDate.setDate(now.getDate() + 10); 

  const orderDateStr = Utilities.formatDate(now, timeZone, "yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss");
  const deliveryDateStr = Utilities.formatDate(deliveryDate, timeZone, "yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss");

  shippingCharge = Number(shippingCharge || 0);

  // 3. Construct Payload
  const payload = {
    "orderType": "businessorder",
    "orderNumber": String(poRef),
    "orderDate": orderDateStr,
    "expDeliveryDate": deliveryDateStr,
    "remarks1": "B2B Shipment via API",
    "paymentMode": "5",
    "shippingMethod": "1",
    "shippingCharges": shippingCharge,

    "customer": [{
      "customerId": String(customerId),
      "billing": addressDetails,
      "shipping": addressDetails
    }],

    "items": items,
    "queue": 1
  };

  Logger.log(payload);

  // 4. Generate token based on passed locationKey, otherwise default location
  const token = getEasyEcomToken(locationKey);

  if (!token) {
    const msg = "Auth Token Failed.";
    logOrderCreation(ss, poRef, customerId, "Failed", "", msg);
    return { status: 'error', message: msg };
  }

  const scriptProperties = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
  const X_API_KEY = scriptProperties.getProperty('EASY_ECOM_API_KEY');
  const url = "https://api.easyecom.io/webhook/v2/createOrder";
 
  const options = {
    method: "POST",
    headers: {
      "Authorization": "Bearer " + token,
      "x-api-key": X_API_KEY,
      "Content-Type": "application/json"
    },
    payload: JSON.stringify(payload),
    muteHttpExceptions: true
  };

  try {
    const response = UrlFetchApp.fetch(url, options);
    const text = response.getContentText();

    if (text.trim().startsWith("<")) {
      console.error("API Returned HTML Error: " + text);
      const msg = "API Error (500/404): Endpoint issue.";
      logOrderCreation(ss, poRef, customerId, "Error", "", msg);
      return { status: 'error', message: msg };
    }

    const json = JSON.parse(text);

    if (response.getResponseCode() === 200 && json.code === 200) {

      const orderId = json.data ? json.data.order_id : (json.order_id || "");
      logOrderCreation(ss, poRef, customerId, "Success", orderId, JSON.stringify(json));
      
      return {
        status: 'success',
        message: "Order Created in EasyEcom: " + poRef,
        orderId: orderId
      };

    } else {

      const errorMsg = json.message || JSON.stringify(json);
      logOrderCreation(ss, poRef, customerId, "Failed", "", errorMsg);

      return {
        status: 'error',
        message: errorMsg
      };
    }

  } catch (e) {

    logOrderCreation(ss, poRef, customerId, "Error", "", e.toString());

    return {
      status: 'error',
      message: e.toString()
    };
  }
}
// ==========================================
// HELPER: GET CLEAN ADDRESS (API FORMAT)
// ==========================================


function getCustomerAddressFromSheet(ss, targetCId) {
  const sheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_EE_CUSTOMERS);
  if (!sheet) return null;


  const data = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
 
  // Iterate rows (skip header)
  for (let i = 1; i < data.length; i++) {
    const rowId = String(data[i][0]).trim();
   
    if (rowId === String(targetCId).trim()) {
     
      // --- CLEAN DATA ---
     
      // Fix Phone (Scientific Notation)
      let rawPhone = data[i][3];
      let cleanPhone = "";
      if (typeof rawPhone === 'number') {
        cleanPhone = Math.floor(rawPhone).toString();
        if (cleanPhone === "0") cleanPhone = "";
      } else {
        cleanPhone = String(rawPhone || "").trim();
      }


      // Fix Pincode
      let rawZip = data[i][6];
      let cleanZip = "";
      if (typeof rawZip === 'number') {
        cleanZip = Math.floor(rawZip).toString();
      } else {
        cleanZip = String(rawZip || "").trim();
      }


      // --- RETURN API-READY OBJECT ---
      return {
        "name": String(data[i][1] || "").trim(),
        "addressLine1": String(data[i][4] || "").trim(), // Mapped to address_line_1
        "addressLine2": "",
        "postalCode": cleanZip,                               // Mapped to pincode
        "city": String(data[i][5] || "").trim(),
        "state": String(data[i][7] || "").trim(),
        "country": String(data[i][8] || "India").trim(),
        "contact": cleanPhone,                       // Mapped to mobile_number
        "email": String(data[i][2] || "").trim()
      };
    }
  }
  return null;
}


// ==========================================
// HELPER: LOGGING
// ==========================================


function logOrderCreation(ss, poRef, customerId, status, eeOrderId, message) {
  let sheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_SHIPMENT_LOG);
  if (!sheet) {
    sheet = ss.insertSheet(SHEET_SHIPMENT_LOG);
    sheet.appendRow(["Timestamp", "PO Reference", "Customer ID", "Status", "EE Order ID", "API Message"]);
    sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, 6).setFontWeight("Bold");
  }


  const timestamp = new Date();
  sheet.appendRow([timestamp, poRef, customerId, status, eeOrderId || "N/A", message]);
}


// ==========================================
// 7. UTILITIES
// ==========================================

function getEasyEcomToken(location_key) {
  var scriptProperties = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();

  const email = scriptProperties.getProperty('EASY_ECOM_EMAIL');
  const password = scriptProperties.getProperty('EASY_ECOM_PASSWORD');

  // If location_key is passed, use it. Otherwise use default from Script Properties.
  const finalLocationKey = location_key || scriptProperties.getProperty('EASY_ECOM_LOCATION_KEY');

  const X_API_KEY = scriptProperties.getProperty('EASY_ECOM_API_KEY');

  const url = "https://api.easyecom.io/access/token";

  const cred = {
    email: email,
    password: password,
    location_key: finalLocationKey
  };

  const options = {
    method: "post",
    headers: {
      "x-api-key": X_API_KEY,
      "Content-Type": "application/json"
    },
    payload: JSON.stringify(cred),
    muteHttpExceptions: true
  };

  try {
    const response = UrlFetchApp.fetch(url, options);
    const text = response.getContentText();

    if (text.startsWith("<")) {
      throw new Error("Received HTML — check credentials, API key, or token URL.");
    }

    const result = JSON.parse(text);
    const token = result?.data?.token?.jwt_token;

    if (!token) {
      throw new Error("Token not found in response: " + text);
    }

    Logger.log("✅ Token generated successfully");
    return token;

  } catch (err) {
    Logger.log("❌ Token Error: " + err.message);
    return null;
  }
}

function getOrCreateLogSheet(ss, name) {
  let sheet = ss.getSheetByName(name);
  if (!sheet) {
    sheet = ss.insertSheet(name);
    sheet.appendRow(['Date', 'Channel', 'Sender', 'Subject', 'File', 'Link', 'Category', 'PO#', 'Store', 'Status']);
  }
  return sheet;
}

function getDataAsJSON(sheet) {
  const data = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
  if (data.length < 2) return [];
  const headers = data[0];
  const result = [];
  for (let i = 1; i < data.length; i++) {
    const obj = {};
    headers.forEach((h, j) => obj[h] = data[i][j]);
    result.push(obj);
  }
  return result;
}

function extractFileIdFromUrl(url) {
  if (!url) return null;
  const match = url.match(/\/d\/([a-zA-Z0-9-_]+)/) || url.match(/id=([a-zA-Z0-9-_]+)/);
  return match ? match[1] : null;
}

function getCsvData(id) {
  const file = DriveApp.getFileById(id);
  return Utilities.parseCsv(file.getBlob().getDataAsString());
}

/**
 * **FINAL & CORRECTED:** Converts an Excel or CSV file in Drive to a 2D array.
 * It now correctly handles both modern (.xlsx) and legacy (.xls) Excel formats
 * by using the robust Drive API (Advanced Service) for conversion.
 *
 * @param {string} id - The Google Drive file ID of the Excel/CSV file.
 * @return {Array<Array>} The data from the first sheet of the file.
 */
function getExcelDataViaBlob(id) {
  try {
    const file = DriveApp.getFileById(id);
    let blob = file.getBlob();

    const fileName = file.getName().toLowerCase();

    // ✅ Fix MIME
    if (fileName.endsWith(".xlsx")) {
      blob = blob.setContentType("application/vnd.openxmlformats-officedocument.spreadsheetml.sheet");
    } else if (fileName.endsWith(".xls")) {
      blob = blob.setContentType("application/vnd.ms-excel");
    }

    const resource = {
      title: "Temp_Conversion_" + new Date().getTime(),
      mimeType: MimeType.GOOGLE_SHEETS
    };

    const tempFile = Drive.Files.insert(resource, blob, { convert: true });
    const tempSheetId = tempFile.id;

    if (!tempSheetId) {
      throw new Error("No Sheet ID returned");
    }

    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.openById(tempSheetId);
    const data = ss.getSheets()[0].getDataRange().getValues();

    // ✅ SAFE CLEANUP (FIXED)
    try {
      DriveApp.getFileById(tempSheetId).setTrashed(true);
    } catch (e) {
      Logger.log("⚠️ Cleanup failed: " + e.message);
    }

    return data;

  } catch (e) {
    console.error(`❌ Excel conversion failed for ${id}: ${e.message}`);
    console.error(e);
    return [];
  }
}
/**
 * **MODIFIED:** Loads the mapping from the inventory sheet into a more complex object.
 * The map now stores both the Master SKU and the Zoho Item ID for each channel item.
 *
 * @param {SpreadsheetApp.Spreadsheet} ss - The active spreadsheet object.
 * @return {object} A nested object structured as: { channel: { itemCode: { masterSku: '...', zohoItemId: '...' } } }
 */
function loadSkuMapping(ss) {
  const sheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_INVENTORY); // Assumes SHEET_INVENTORY is defined
  const data = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
  const map = {};

  // Find column indexes dynamically for robustness
  const headers = data[0];
  const idxChannel = headers.indexOf('Channel'); // Assuming Column A
  const idxItemCode = headers.indexOf('Channel Item Code'); // Assuming Column B
  const idxMasterSku = headers.indexOf('Master SKU'); // Assuming Column C
  const idxZohoId = headers.indexOf('Zoho Item ID'); // Assuming Column I

  if (idxChannel === -1 || idxItemCode === -1 || idxMasterSku === -1 || idxZohoId === -1) {
    console.error("One or more required columns not found in the mapping sheet.");
    return {};
  }

  for (let i = 1; i < data.length; i++) {
    const row = data[i];
    const ch = String(row[idxChannel]).toLowerCase().trim();
    const code = String(row[idxItemCode]).trim();
    const master = String(row[idxMasterSku]).trim();
    const zohoId = String(row[idxZohoId]).trim(); // Get the Zoho ID from Column I

    if (ch && code && master) { // Only create an entry if the key identifiers exist
      if (!map[ch]) map[ch] = {};
      
      // --- THE CHANGE IS HERE ---
      // Instead of just a string, store an object with both values.
      map[ch][code] = {
        masterSku: master,
        zohoItemId: zohoId
      };
    }
  }
  return map;
}


/**
 * **MODIFIED:** Finds the Master SKU from the new, complex mapping object.
 * Its external behavior remains the same.
 *
 * @param {object} map - The mapping object from loadSkuMapping.
 * @param {string} ch - The channel key (e.g., 'bigbasket').
 * @param {string} code - The channel's item code.
 * @return {string} The found Master SKU, or "Not Found".
 */
function findMasterSku(map, ch, code) {
  const cKey = String(code).trim();
  
  // Look for the details object.
  const details = map[ch] && map[ch][cKey];
  
  // Return the 'masterSku' property from the object.
  return details ? details.masterSku : "Not Found";
}


/**
 * **NEW FUNCTION:** Finds the Zoho Item ID from the new, complex mapping object.
 *
 * @param {object} map - The mapping object from loadSkuMapping.
 * @param {string} ch - The channel key (e.g., 'bigbasket').
 * @param {string} code - The channel's item code.
 * @return {string} The found Zoho Item ID, or an empty string if not found.
 */
function findZohoItemId(map, ch, code) {
  const cKey = String(code).trim();
  
  // Look for the details object.
  const details = map[ch] && map[ch][cKey];
  
  // Return the 'zohoItemId' property from the object.
  return details ? details.zohoItemId : "";
}

function loadChannelThresholds(ss) {
  const sheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_CHANNEL_CONFIG);
  const data = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
  const map = {};
  // Assuming threshold is col 5 (index 4)
  for(let i=1; i<data.length; i++) {
    map[String(data[i][0]).toLowerCase()] = Number(data[i][4]);
  }
  return map;
}
