get.gs


function fetchEasyEcomCustomers() {
  var scriptProperties = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.openById(SPREADSHEET_ID);
  let sheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_EE_CUSTOMERS);
  
  // --- 1. LOAD ACTIVE CHANNELS ---
  // Ensure this function returns an array of strings like ["Instamart", "Zepto"]
  // If it's not defined in this file, copy the helper function at the bottom.
  let activeChannels = getActiveChannels(ss); 
  
  // SANITIZE CHANNELS: Convert to lowercase and remove empty strings to prevent matching everything
  activeChannels = activeChannels
    .map(c => String(c).toLowerCase().trim())
    .filter(c => c !== "");

  if (activeChannels.length === 0) {
    console.error("No active channels found in Config. Stopping.");
    return;
  }

  console.log("Filtering customers for channels: " + activeChannels.join(", "));

  // --- 2. GENERATE TOKEN ---
  const token = getEasyEcomToken(); 
  if (!token) {
    console.error("Failed to generate EasyEcom Token.");
    return;
  }

  const baseUrl = "https://api.easyecom.io/Wholesale/v2/UserManagement";
  const X_API_KEY =  scriptProperties.getProperty('EASY_ECOM_API_KEY');
  
  const options = {
    method: "GET",
    headers: {
      "Authorization": "Bearer " + token,
      "x-api-key": X_API_KEY,
      "Content-Type": "application/json"
    },
    muteHttpExceptions: true
  };

  let allCustomers = [];
  let processedIds = new Set();
  let page = 1;
  let hasMoreData = true;

  console.log("Fetching Customers from EasyEcom...");

  while (hasMoreData) {
    const url = `${baseUrl}?type=b2b&limit=250&page=${page}`;
    
    try {
      const response = UrlFetchApp.fetch(url, options);
      //Logger.log(response);
      const responseCode = response.getResponseCode();
      
      if (responseCode === 200) {
        const json = JSON.parse(response.getContentText());
        
        if (json.code === 200 && json.data && json.data.length > 0) {
          
          const rawCount = json.data.length;

          // --- FILTER LOGIC (UPDATED) ---
          const filteredBatch = json.data.filter(c => {
            const id = String(c.c_id);
            
            // 1. Duplicate Check
            if (processedIds.has(id)) return false; 
            
            // 2. Channel Name Check
            const companyName = String(c.companyname || "").toLowerCase().trim();
            
            // Match against cleaned activeChannels list
            const matchesChannel = activeChannels.some(channelKey => {
              // Exact check: Does "swiggy instamart" include "instamart"? -> YES
              return companyName.includes(channelKey);
            });
            
            if (!matchesChannel) return false; 

            processedIds.add(id); 
            return true;
          });

          // Process valid records
          if (filteredBatch.length > 0) {
            const batchRows = filteredBatch.map(c => [
              String(c.c_id || "").trim(),
              String(c.companyname || "").trim(),
              String(c.customer_support_email || "").trim(),
              String(c.customer_support_contact || "").trim(),
              String(c.dispatchStreet || "").trim(),
              String(c.dispatchCity || "").trim(),
              String(c.dispatchZipcode || "").trim(),
              String(c.dispatchState || "").trim(),
              String(c.dispatchCountry || "").trim(),
              String(c.gstNum || "").trim()
            ]);
            allCustomers = allCustomers.concat(batchRows);
          }
          
          console.log(`Page ${page}: Fetched ${rawCount} raw, Kept ${filteredBatch.length} matching.`);

          // Pagination logic
          if (rawCount < 250) {
            hasMoreData = false;
          } else {
            page++; 
          }
        } else {
          hasMoreData = false; 
        }
      } else {
        console.error(`API Error on page ${page}: ${response.getContentText()}`);
        hasMoreData = false;
      }
    } catch (e) {
      console.error(`Fetch Error: ${e.message}`);
      hasMoreData = false;
    }
    
    // UPDATED SAFETY BREAK: 5000 customers / 250 per page = 20 pages.
    // Set safety to 30 to cover future growth.
    if (page > 2) { 
      console.warn("Safety break at page 30.");
      hasMoreData = false;
    }
  }

  // --- 3. WRITE TO SHEET ---
  if (allCustomers.length > 0) {
    sheet.clearContents(); // Use clearContents to keep formatting
    
    const headers = [
      "Customer ID", "Company Name", "Support Email", "Support Contact", 
      "Billing Street", "Billing City", "Billing Zip", "Billing State", "Billing Country","GST"
    ];
    
    sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, headers.length).setValues([headers]).setFontWeight("Bold").setBackground("#D9EAD3");
    sheet.getRange(2, 1, allCustomers.length, allCustomers[0].length).setValues(allCustomers);
    
    console.log(`Success: Saved ${allCustomers.length} relevant customers to ${SHEET_EE_CUSTOMERS}.`);
  } else {
    console.log("No customers matched your Channel Config names.");
  }
  updateCustomerIdsInPoDatabase();

}
function getActiveChannels(ss) {
  const sheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_CHANNEL_CONFIG);
  if (!sheet) return [];
 
  const data = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
  let channels = [];
 
  // Assuming Col A = Name, Col B = Status
  for (let i = 1; i < data.length; i++) {
    const name = String(data[i][0]).trim();
    const status = String(data[i][1]).toLowerCase().trim();
   
    if (name && status === 'active') {
      channels.push(name);
    }
  }
  return channels;
}
// =================================================================================
// EASYECOM - MASTER SKU INVENTORY & DETAILS SYNC (UPDATED)
// =================================================================================

/**
 * **FINAL & CORRECTED:** Updates the 'Inventory', 'EAN', 'Itemname', and 'MRP' columns.
 * This version correctly handles all fetched batches and performs a reliable
 * batch update on the correct range.
 */
function updateMasterSkuInventory() {
  Logger.log('--- Starting Master SKU Inventory & Details Sync from EasyEcom ---');
    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.openById(SPREADSHEET_ID);
  let mappingSheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_INVENTORY);
  
  if (mappingSheet.getLastRow() < 2) return;

  // --- Step 1: Get unique Master SKUs from the mapping sheet ---
  const masterSkuColumnIndex = 3; // Column C
  const skuRange = mappingSheet.getRange(2, masterSkuColumnIndex, mappingSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 1);
  const masterSkuValues = skuRange.getDisplayValues().flat();
  const uniqueSkus = [...new Set(masterSkuValues.filter(Boolean))];

  if (uniqueSkus.length === 0) return;
  Logger.log(`Found ${uniqueSkus.length} unique Master SKUs to fetch details for.`);

  // --- Step 2: Fetch full product details for ALL SKUs in batches ---
  const productDetailsMap = _fetchInventoryDetailsInBatches(uniqueSkus);
  if (productDetailsMap.size === 0) {
    Logger.log('Failed to fetch any product details from EasyEcom.');
    return;
  }

  // =========================================================================
  // THE FIX IS HERE: A more robust method for preparing and writing the data.
  // =========================================================================

  // --- Step 3: Prepare the 4-column wide update for the sheet ---
  // Create a 2D array with the new data, ensuring the order matches the sheet.
  const dataToWrite = masterSkuValues.map(masterSku => {
    const trimmedSku = masterSku.trim();
    if (productDetailsMap.has(trimmedSku)) {
      const details = productDetailsMap.get(trimmedSku);
      return [
        details.inv,        // Inventory
        details.ean,        // EAN
        details.name,       // Itemname
        details.mrp,
        details.size         // MRP
      ];
    } else {
      // If a SKU wasn't found in the API response, return blank values
      // to avoid overwriting existing data with zeros.
      return [null, null, null, null,null];
    }
  });

  // --- Step 4: Perform a single, efficient batch write operation ---
  const startColumn = 5; // Update starts at Column E (Inventory)
  const updateRange = mappingSheet.getRange(2, startColumn, dataToWrite.length, 5);
  
  // To avoid overwriting good data with blanks, we need to be more careful.
  // We'll get the existing data and only change what's new.
  const existingValues = updateRange.getValues();
  const finalValues = existingValues.map((row, i) => {
    return [
      dataToWrite[i][0] !== null ? dataToWrite[i][0] : row[0],
      dataToWrite[i][1] !== null ? dataToWrite[i][1] : row[1],
      dataToWrite[i][2] !== null ? dataToWrite[i][2] : row[2],
      dataToWrite[i][3] !== null ? dataToWrite[i][3] : row[3],
      dataToWrite[i][4] !== null ? dataToWrite[i][4] : row[4]
    ];
  });

  updateRange.setValues(finalValues);
  
  Logger.log(`Sync complete. Processed ${productDetailsMap.size} SKUs from API and updated the sheet.`);
}


/**
 * **HELPER (UPDATED):** Fetches inventory and product details from EasyEcom's V3 API.
 * This version uses a slightly different limit parameter that may be more reliable.
 */
function _fetchInventoryDetailsInBatches(skus) {
  const token = getEasyEcomToken();
  const apiKey = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().getProperty('EASY_ECOM_API_KEY');
  if (!token || !apiKey) return new Map();

  const baseUrl = 'https://api.easyecom.io/getInventoryDetailsV3?includeLocations=0&limit=20';
  const batchSize = 20;
  const detailsMap = new Map();

  for (let i = 0; i < skus.length; i += batchSize) {
    const batch = skus.slice(i, i + batchSize);
    const url = `${baseUrl}&sku=${batch.join(',')}`;
    Logger.log(url);
    Logger.log(`Fetching details for batch ${Math.floor(i / batchSize) + 1}...`);

    const options = {
      method: 'GET',
      headers: {
        'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + token,
        'x-api-key': apiKey
      },
      muteHttpExceptions: true
    };

    try {
      const response = UrlFetchApp.fetch(url, options);
      //Logger.log(response);

      if (response.getResponseCode() === 200) {
        const json = JSON.parse(response.getContentText());

        if (json.data && json.data.inventoryData) {
          json.data.inventoryData.forEach(item => {
            const sku = item.sku;
            if (!sku) return;

            // 🔹 Extract dimensions safely
            const length  = Number(item.length)  || '';
            const breadth = Number(item.width) || '';
            const height  = Number(item.height)  || '';

            const size =
              length && breadth && height
                ? `${length}x${breadth}x${height}`
                : '';

            detailsMap.set(String(sku).trim(), {
              inv: item.availableInventory || 0,
              name: item.productName || '',
              ean: item.productUniqueCode || '',
              mrp: item.accountingUnit || 0,
              size: size // ✅ LxBxH
            });
          });
        }
      } else {
        Logger.log(`API Error for batch: ${response.getContentText()}`);
      }
    } catch (e) {
      Logger.log(`Exception for batch: ${e.message}`);
    }

    Utilities.sleep(1100); // rate-limit safety
  }

  return detailsMap;
}

function old_fetchEasyEcomShipments() {
  const SS = SpreadsheetApp.openById(SPREADSHEET_ID);
  const SHEET_NAME = 'EE_Shipments';
  let sheet = SS.getSheetByName(SHEET_NAME);

  if (!sheet) {
    sheet = SS.insertSheet(SHEET_NAME);
  }

  // --- CONFIG ---
  const WEEKS_TO_FETCH = 8;
  const BATCH_DAYS = 7;
  const API_LIMIT = 250;

  const TARGET_COLUMNS = [
    'order_date',
    'reference_code',
    'order_id',
    'customer_name',
    'order_status',
    'order_status_id',
    'courier',
    'awb_number',
    'item_sku',
    'item_item_status',
    'item_item_quantity',
    'item_cancelled_quantity',
    'item_shipped_quantity',
    'item_returned_quantity',
    'contact_num',
    'email',
    'batch_created_at',
    'invoice_date',
    'manifest_date'
  ];

  // --- CHANNEL FILTER ---
  let activeChannels = getActiveChannels(SS)
    .map(c => String(c).toLowerCase().trim())
    .filter(c => c !== "");

  if (activeChannels.length === 0) {
    console.error("No active channels found.");
    return;
  }

  console.log("Filtering Shipments for: " + activeChannels.join(", "));

  // --- AUTH ---
  const props = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
  const apiKey = props.getProperty('EASY_ECOM_API_KEY');
  const token = getEasyEcomToken();

  if (!token || !apiKey) {
    console.error("Missing EasyEcom credentials.");
    return;
  }

  let allRows = [];
  const uniqueSet = new Set(); // 🔥 Deduplication set

  const today = new Date();

  // =========================
  // DATE LOOP (FIXED)
  // =========================
  for (let i = 0; i < WEEKS_TO_FETCH; i++) {

    let end = new Date(today);
    end.setDate(today.getDate() - (i * BATCH_DAYS));
    end.setHours(23, 59, 59, 999);

    let start = new Date(end);
    start.setDate(end.getDate() - BATCH_DAYS + 1); // ✅ FIX: no overlap
    start.setHours(0, 0, 0, 0);

    const startDateStr = Utilities.formatDate(start, Session.getScriptTimeZone(), "yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss");
    const endDateStr = Utilities.formatDate(end, Session.getScriptTimeZone(), "yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss");

    console.log(`Fetching Batch ${i + 1}: ${startDateStr} -> ${endDateStr}`);

    let nextPageUrl = `https://api.easyecom.io/orders/V2/getAllOrders?start_date=${startDateStr}&end_date=${endDateStr}&limit=${API_LIMIT}&order_type=1&marketplaceId=64&status_id=`;

    while (nextPageUrl) {
      try {
        const options = {
          method: "GET",
          headers: {
            "Authorization": "Bearer " + token,
            "x-api-key": apiKey,
            "Content-Type": "application/json"
          },
          muteHttpExceptions: true
        };

        const res = UrlFetchApp.fetch(nextPageUrl, options);
        //Logger.log(res);
        const code = res.getResponseCode();

        if (code !== 200) {
          console.error(`API Error (${code}): ${res.getContentText()}`);
          break;
        }

        const json = JSON.parse(res.getContentText());

        if (json.code === 200 && json.data?.orders?.length > 0) {

          json.data.orders.forEach(order => {

            // --- CHANNEL FILTER ---
            const custName = String(order.customer_name || "").toLowerCase();
            const isMatch = activeChannels.some(ch => custName.includes(ch));
            if (!isMatch) return;

            const parentData = flattenItem(order, '', ['suborders']);

            // --- HANDLE SUBORDERS ---
            if (order.suborders && order.suborders.length > 0) {

              order.suborders.forEach(sub => {
                const subData = flattenItem(sub, 'item');
                const combinedRow = { ...parentData, ...subData };

                // ✅ DEDUP KEY
                const key = `${combinedRow.reference_code}|${combinedRow.item_sku}`;

                if (!uniqueSet.has(key)) {
                  uniqueSet.add(key);
                  allRows.push(combinedRow);
                }
              });

            } else {
              // No suborders
              const key = `${parentData.reference_code}|NO_SKU`;

              if (!uniqueSet.has(key)) {
                uniqueSet.add(key);
                allRows.push(parentData);
              }
            }
          });

          // --- PAGINATION ---
          if (json.data.pagination?.next_page_url) {
            nextPageUrl = json.data.pagination.next_page_url;
            Utilities.sleep(500);
          } else {
            nextPageUrl = null;
          }

        } else {
          nextPageUrl = null;
        }

      } catch (e) {
        console.error("Fetch Exception: " + e.message);
        nextPageUrl = null;
      }
    }
  }

  // =========================
  // WRITE TO SHEET
  // =========================
  if (allRows.length > 0) {

    const output = [TARGET_COLUMNS];

    allRows.forEach(rowObj => {
      const rowArray = TARGET_COLUMNS.map(header => {
        const val = rowObj[header];
        return (val === undefined || val === null) ? "" : String(val);
      });
      output.push(rowArray);
    });

    sheet.clearContents();
    sheet.getRange(1, 1, output.length, output[0].length).setValues(output);
    sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, output[0].length)
      .setFontWeight("Bold")
      .setBackground("#FFF2CC");

    console.log(`✅ Success: Wrote ${allRows.length} unique rows.`);
  } else {
    console.log("No matching orders found.");
  }

  SpreadsheetApp.flush();

  updateTrackingStatusAll();
  updateShipmentDetailsInPoDatabase();
}
function fetchEasyEcomShipments() {
  const SS = SpreadsheetApp.openById(SPREADSHEET_ID);
  const SHEET_NAME = 'EE_Shipments';
  let sheet = SS.getSheetByName(SHEET_NAME);

  if (!sheet) {
    sheet = SS.insertSheet(SHEET_NAME);
  }

  // --- CONFIG ---
  const WEEKS_TO_FETCH = 2;
  const BATCH_DAYS = 7;
  const API_LIMIT = 250;

  const TARGET_COLUMNS = [
    'order_date',
    'reference_code',
    'order_id',
    'customer_name',
    'order_status',
    'order_status_id',
    'courier',
    'awb_number',
    'item_sku',
    'item_item_status',
    'item_item_quantity',
    'item_cancelled_quantity',
    'item_shipped_quantity',
    'item_returned_quantity',
    'contact_num',
    'email',
    'batch_created_at',
    'invoice_date',
    'manifest_date'
  ];

  const QUANTITY_FIELDS = [
    'item_item_quantity',
    'item_cancelled_quantity',
    'item_shipped_quantity',
    'item_returned_quantity'
  ];

  // --- CHANNEL FILTER ---
  let activeChannels = getActiveChannels(SS)
    .map(c => String(c).toLowerCase().trim())
    .filter(c => c !== "");

  if (activeChannels.length === 0) {
    console.error("No active channels found.");
    return;
  }

  console.log("Filtering Shipments for: " + activeChannels.join(", "));

  // --- AUTH ---
  const props = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
  const apiKey = props.getProperty('EASY_ECOM_API_KEY');
  const token = getEasyEcomToken();

  if (!token || !apiKey) {
    console.error("Missing EasyEcom credentials.");
    return;
  }

  let allRows = [];

  const today = new Date();

  // =========================
  // DATE LOOP
  // =========================
  for (let i = 0; i < WEEKS_TO_FETCH; i++) {

    let end = new Date(today);
    end.setDate(today.getDate() - (i * BATCH_DAYS));
    end.setHours(23, 59, 59, 999);

    let start = new Date(end);
    start.setDate(end.getDate() - BATCH_DAYS + 1);
    start.setHours(0, 0, 0, 0);

    const startDateStr = Utilities.formatDate(start, Session.getScriptTimeZone(), "yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss");
    const endDateStr = Utilities.formatDate(end, Session.getScriptTimeZone(), "yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss");

    console.log(`Fetching Batch ${i + 1}: ${startDateStr} -> ${endDateStr}`);

    let nextPageUrl = `https://api.easyecom.io/orders/V2/getAllOrders?start_date=${startDateStr}&end_date=${endDateStr}&limit=${API_LIMIT}&order_type=1&marketplaceId=64&status_id=`;

    while (nextPageUrl) {
      try {
        const options = {
          method: "GET",
          headers: {
            "Authorization": "Bearer " + token,
            "x-api-key": apiKey,
            "Content-Type": "application/json"
          },
          muteHttpExceptions: true
        };

        const res = UrlFetchApp.fetch(nextPageUrl, options);
        //Logger.log(res);
        const code = res.getResponseCode();

        if (code !== 200) {
          console.error(`API Error (${code}): ${res.getContentText()}`);
          break;
        }

        const json = JSON.parse(res.getContentText());

        if (json.code === 200 && json.data?.orders?.length > 0) {

          json.data.orders.forEach(order => {

            // --- CHANNEL FILTER ---
            const custName = String(order.customer_name || "").toLowerCase();
            const isMatch = activeChannels.some(ch => custName.includes(ch));
            if (!isMatch) return;

            const parentData = flattenItem(order, '', ['suborders']);

            // --- HANDLE SUBORDERS ---
            if (order.suborders && order.suborders.length > 0) {
              order.suborders.forEach(sub => {
                const subData = flattenItem(sub, 'item');
                const combinedRow = { ...parentData, ...subData };
                allRows.push(combinedRow); // Collect everything, merge later
              });
            } else {
              allRows.push(parentData); // No suborders
            }
          });

          // --- PAGINATION ---
          if (json.data.pagination?.next_page_url) {
            nextPageUrl = json.data.pagination.next_page_url;
            Utilities.sleep(500);
          } else {
            nextPageUrl = null;
          }

        } else {
          nextPageUrl = null;
        }

      } catch (e) {
        console.error("Fetch Exception: " + e.message);
        nextPageUrl = null;
      }
    }
  }

  // =========================
  // MERGE ROWS BY order_id + item_sku
  // =========================
  const mergeMap = new Map();

  allRows.forEach(row => {
    const key = `${row.order_id}|${row.item_sku}`;

    if (!mergeMap.has(key)) {
      mergeMap.set(key, { ...row }); // First occurrence — clone it
    } else {
      const existing = mergeMap.get(key);
      QUANTITY_FIELDS.forEach(field => {
        const a = parseFloat(existing[field]) || 0;
        const b = parseFloat(row[field]) || 0;
        existing[field] = String(a + b); // Sum quantities
      });
    }
  });

  const mergedRows = Array.from(mergeMap.values());

  // =========================
  // WRITE TO SHEET
  // =========================
  if (mergedRows.length > 0) {

    const output = [TARGET_COLUMNS];

    mergedRows.forEach(rowObj => {
      const rowArray = TARGET_COLUMNS.map(header => {
        const val = rowObj[header];
        return (val === undefined || val === null) ? "" : String(val);
      });
      output.push(rowArray);
    });

    sheet.clearContents();
    sheet.getRange(1, 1, output.length, output[0].length).setValues(output);
    sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, output[0].length)
      .setFontWeight("Bold")
      .setBackground("#FFF2CC");

    console.log(`✅ Success: Wrote ${mergedRows.length} merged rows.`);
  } else {
    console.log("No matching orders found.");
  }

  SpreadsheetApp.flush();

  updateTrackingStatusAll();
  updateShipmentDetailsInPoDatabase();
}

/**
 * Flattens an object.
 */
function flattenItem(obj, prefix = '', excludeKeys = []) {
  let res = {};
  
  for (const key in obj) {
    if (!obj.hasOwnProperty(key)) continue;
    if (excludeKeys.includes(key)) continue; 

    const val = obj[key];
    const newKey = prefix ? `${prefix}_${key}` : key;

    if (typeof val === 'object' && val !== null && !Array.isArray(val)) {
      const flatObject = flattenItem(val, newKey);
      res = { ...res, ...flatObject };
    } else if (Array.isArray(val)) {
      res[newKey] = val.map(x => (typeof x === 'object' ? JSON.stringify(x) : x)).join(" | ");
    } else {
      res[newKey] = val;
    }
  }
  return res;
}

function syncZohoContacts() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.openById(SPREADSHEET_ID);
  
  // 1. Load Active Channels (The 5 keywords)
  const activeChannels = getActiveChannels(ss);
  if (activeChannels.length === 0) {
    console.log("No Active Channels found. Aborting.");
    return;
  }
  console.log("Searching Zoho for: " + activeChannels.join(", "));

  // 2. Get Token
  const token = getZohoAccessToken();
  if (!token) return;

  const props = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
  const orgId = props.getProperty('ZOHO_ORG_ID');

  // We loop through the channels. 
  // API Limits: Zoho allows plenty of calls per minute, 5 sequential calls is very safe.
  
  let allContacts = [];
  let processedContactIds = new Set(); // To avoid duplicates if keywords overlap

  for (const channelName of activeChannels) {
    
    // 3. Search Loop Per Channel
    let page = 1;
    let hasMorePages = true;
    const encodedQuery = encodeURIComponent(channelName);

    console.log(`>>> Fetching: ${channelName}...`);

    while (hasMorePages) {
      // API: Search by text containing the channel name
      const url = `https://www.zohoapis.in/books/v3/contacts?organization_id=${orgId}&contact_type=customer&contact_name_startswith=${encodedQuery}&page=${page}`;
      
      const options = {
        method: "GET",
        headers: {
          "Authorization": "Zoho-oauthtoken " + token,
          "Content-Type": "application/json"
        },
        muteHttpExceptions: true
      };

      try {
        const response = UrlFetchApp.fetch(url, options);
        const code = response.getResponseCode();

        if (code === 200) {
          const json = JSON.parse(response.getContentText());
          const contacts = json.contacts;

          if (contacts && contacts.length > 0) {
            
            const batch = [];
            contacts.forEach(c => {
              // Deduplicate: If we haven't seen this ID yet
              if (!processedContactIds.has(c.contact_id)) {
                
                batch.push([
                  c.contact_id,
                  c.contact_name,
                  c.company_name,
                  c.outstanding_receivable_amount,
                  c.outstanding_payable_amount,
                  c.unused_credits_receivable_amount,
                  c.unused_credits_payable_amount,
                  c.first_name,
                  c.last_name,
                  c.email,
                  c.mobile,
                  c.gst_no,
                  c.place_of_contact,
                  c.place_of_contact_formatted,
                ]);
                
                processedContactIds.add(c.contact_id);
              }
            });

            if (batch.length > 0) {
              allContacts = allContacts.concat(batch);
            }

            // Pagination Check
            if (json.page_context && json.page_context.has_more_page) {
              page++;
            } else {
              hasMorePages = false;
            }
          } else {
            hasMorePages = false; // No results for this channel
          }
        } else {
          console.error(`Error searching ${channelName}: ${response.getContentText()}`);
          hasMorePages = false;
        }
      } catch (e) {
        console.error(`Exception searching ${channelName}: ${e.message}`);
        hasMorePages = false;
      }
    }
  }

  // 4. Write Results
  let sheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_ZOHO_CUSTOMERS);

  if (allContacts.length > 0) {
    sheet.clearContents(); 

    const headers = [
      "Contact Id", "Contact Name", "Company Name","Receivable", "Payable","Unused Credits Rec.", "Unused Credits Pay.", "First Name", "Last Name", "Email", "Mobile","GST No", "Place of Contact", "Place Formatted"
    ];

    sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, headers.length).setValues([headers]);
    sheet.getRange(2, 1, allContacts.length, allContacts[0].length).setValues(allContacts);
    
    console.log(`Success: Wrote ${allContacts.length} targeted customers to ${SHEET_ZOHO_CUSTOMERS}.`);
  } else {
    console.log("No customers found matching active channels.");
  }
  updateCustomerIdsInPoDatabase();
}

/**
 * SMART TOKEN MANAGER
 * Checks if token exists and is valid. If not, refreshes it using refresh_token.
 * Saves API calls and speeds up execution.
 */
function getZohoAccessToken() {
  const props = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
  const now = new Date().getTime();
  
  // 1. Check existing token
  const storedToken = props.getProperty('ZOHO_ACCESS_TOKEN');
  const expiryTime = Number(props.getProperty('ZOHO_TOKEN_EXPIRY')) || 0;

  // Buffer: Refresh if less than 5 minutes remaining
  if (storedToken && now < (expiryTime - 300000)) {
    return storedToken;
  }

  console.log("Refreshing Zoho Access Token...");

  // 2. Fetch New Token
  const clientId = props.getProperty('ZOHO_CLIENT_ID');
  const clientSecret = props.getProperty('ZOHO_CLIENT_SECRET');
  const refreshToken = props.getProperty('ZOHO_REFRESH_TOKEN');

  if (!clientId || !clientSecret || !refreshToken) {
    console.error("Missing Zoho Credentials");
    return null;
  }

  const url = `https://accounts.zoho.in/oauth/v2/token?grant_type=refresh_token&client_id=${clientId}&client_secret=${clientSecret}&refresh_token=${refreshToken}`;
  
  try {
    const response = UrlFetchApp.fetch(url, { method: 'POST' });
    const json = JSON.parse(response.getContentText());

    if (json.access_token) {
      // 3. Save Token & Expiry
      // Zoho tokens last 1 hour (3600 seconds). We set expiry to now + 1 hour.
      const newExpiry = now + (json.expires_in * 1000); 
      
      props.setProperty('ZOHO_ACCESS_TOKEN', json.access_token);
      props.setProperty('ZOHO_TOKEN_EXPIRY', String(newExpiry));
      
      return json.access_token;
    } else {
      console.error("Error refreshing token: " + JSON.stringify(json));
      return null;
    }
  } catch (e) {
    console.error("Token Fetch Exception: " + e.message);
    return null;
  }
}

// ==========================================
// ZOHO BOOKS: INVOICE SYNC
// ==========================================
function syncZohoInvoicesToDB()
{
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.openById(SPREADSHEET_ID);
  const dbSheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_PO_DB);
  
  // --- [NEW] SAFETY CHECK: REMOVE FILTERS ---
  // This prevents the script from editing the wrong rows if a user has hidden data.
  const filter = dbSheet.getFilter();
  if (filter !== null) 
  {
    console.log("Filter detected. Removing filter to ensure data safety.");
    filter.remove();
  }
  // ------------------------------------------

  // 1. Calculate Date (28 Days Ago)
  // Format: YYYY-MM-DD
  const today = new Date();
  const pastDate = new Date(today);
  pastDate.setDate(today.getDate() - 7); 
  const lastModifiedTime = Utilities.formatDate(pastDate, Session.getScriptTimeZone(), "yyyy-MM-dd");

  console.log(`Fetching Zoho Invoices modified after: ${lastModifiedTime}`);

  // 2. Get Zoho Token
  const token = getZohoAccessToken();
  if (!token) return;

  const props = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
  const orgId = props.getProperty('ZOHO_ORG_ID');

  // 3. Fetch Invoices from Zoho
  const invoiceMap = fetchZohoInvoices(token, orgId, lastModifiedTime);
  
  if (invoiceMap.size === 0) 
  {
    console.log("No updated invoices found in Zoho.");
    return;
  }

  //Logger.log(invoiceMap);

  // 4. Update PO Database
  updateDatabaseWithInvoices(dbSheet, invoiceMap);
}


/**
 * **UPDATED & MORE POWERFUL:** Fetches all valid invoices from Zoho. It now includes
 * a conditional, secondary API call to fetch the 'E-Way Bill Number' for any
 * invoice with a total value greater than 50,000.
 *
 * @param {string} token - The Zoho API authentication token.
 * @param {string} orgId - The Zoho organization ID.
 * @param {string} dateStr - The start date in 'YYYY-MM-DD' format.
 * @return {Map<string, object>} A Map where the key is the reference_number.
 */
function fetchZohoInvoices(token, orgId, dateStr) {
  const baseUrl = `https://www.zohoapis.in/books/v3/invoices?organization_id=${orgId}&date_after=${dateStr}&page=`;
  
  const options = {
    method: "GET",
    headers: { "Authorization": "Zoho-oauthtoken " + token },
    muteHttpExceptions: true
  };

  let page = 1;
  let hasMore = true;
  const map = new Map();

  while (hasMore) {
    try {
      const response = UrlFetchApp.fetch(baseUrl + page, options);
      const code = response.getResponseCode();
      
      if (code === 200) {
        const json = JSON.parse(response.getContentText());
        const invoices = json.invoices;

        if (invoices && invoices.length > 0) {
          invoices.forEach(inv => {
            if (inv.status === "void") return; 

            const refNum = String(inv.reference_number || "").trim();
            
            if (refNum) {
              const pdfApiUrl = `https://books.zoho.in/api/v3/invoices/${inv.invoice_id}?organization_id=${orgId}&accept=pdf`;
              let ewayBillNumber = ""; // Default to blank

              // =========================================================================
              // THE NEW LOGIC IS HERE: Conditionally fetch the E-Way Bill
              // =========================================================================
              
              // Check if the invoice total is greater than 50,000.
              if (inv.total > 50000) {
                Logger.log(`Invoice ${inv.invoice_number} has total > 50k. Fetching E-Way Bill...`);
                
                // Make a second, targeted API call for this specific invoice's details.
                const detailsUrl = `https://www.zohoapis.in/books/v3/invoices/${inv.invoice_id}?organization_id=${orgId}`;
                const detailsResponse = UrlFetchApp.fetch(detailsUrl, options);
                
                if (detailsResponse.getResponseCode() === 200) {
                  const detailsJson = JSON.parse(detailsResponse.getContentText());
                  // Safely navigate the JSON to find the eway_bill_number.
                  if (detailsJson.invoice && detailsJson.invoice.eway_bill_details) {
                    ewayBillNumber = detailsJson.invoice.eway_bill_details.eway_bill_number || "";
                    Logger.log(`Found E-Way Bill: ${ewayBillNumber}`);
                  }
                }
                
                // Be a good API citizen and pause after the extra call.
                Utilities.sleep(1100); 
              }

              // Store all the data in the map.
              map.set(refNum, {
                id: inv.invoice_id,
                status: inv.status,
                number: inv.invoice_number,
                date: inv.date,
                total: inv.total,
                portalUrl: inv.invoice_url,
                pdfUrl: pdfApiUrl,
                ewayBill: ewayBillNumber // Add the new E-Way Bill number
              });
            }
          });
          
          hasMore = (json.page_context && json.page_context.has_more_page);
          if (hasMore) page++;

        } else {
          hasMore = false;
        }
      } else {
        console.error(`Zoho API Error: ${response.getContentText()}`);
        hasMore = false;
      }
    } catch (e) {
      console.error("Invoice Fetch Error: " + e.message);
      hasMore = false;
    }
  }

  const loggableObject = Object.fromEntries(map);
  //Logger.log(JSON.stringify(loggableObject, null, 2));

  console.log(`Fetched ${map.size} valid invoices from Zoho.`);
  return map;
}

/**
 * **UPDATED:** Matches Zoho invoices to the PO Database via the Reference Number
 * and performs an efficient batch update. This version now includes the logic to
 * write the newly fetched 'E-Way Bill Number'.
 *
 * @param {Sheet} sheet - The 'PO_Database' sheet object.
 * @param {Map<string, object>} map - The invoice map from fetchZohoInvoices.
 */
function updateDatabaseWithInvoices(sheet, map) {
  const lastRow = sheet.getLastRow();
  if (lastRow < 2) return;

  // 1. Define Column Indexes (Dynamic lookup is more robust)
  const headers = sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, sheet.getLastColumn()).getValues()[0];
  const COL_EE_REF = headers.indexOf('EE_reference_code') + 1;
  const START_COL = headers.indexOf('Invoice Id') + 1;
  
  if (COL_EE_REF === 0 || START_COL === 0) {
      console.error("Could not find 'EE Reference Code' or 'Invoice Id' headers. Aborting update.");
      return;
  }
  
  // 2. Read existing data to match
  const refValues = sheet.getRange(2, COL_EE_REF, lastRow - 1, 1).getValues();

  // =========================================================================
  // THE CHANGES ARE HERE
  // =========================================================================
  
  // 3. Define the new number of columns to read and write (now 8, including EWB).
  const NUM_COLUMNS_TO_UPDATE = 8; 
  
  const existingInvoiceDataRange = sheet.getRange(2, START_COL, lastRow - 1, NUM_COLUMNS_TO_UPDATE);
  const existingData = existingInvoiceDataRange.getValues();
  
  const finalWriteData = existingData.map((row, i) => {
    const eeRef = String(refValues[i][0]).trim();
    const newDetails = map.get(eeRef);
    
    if (newDetails) {
      // Found an update. Return the new data, now including the ewayBill.
      return [
        newDetails.id,
        newDetails.status,
        newDetails.number,
        newDetails.date,
        newDetails.total,
        newDetails.portalUrl,
        newDetails.pdfUrl,
        newDetails.ewayBill || "" // Add the ewayBill, with a fallback to empty string
      ];
    } else {
      // No update found, KEEP THE OLD DATA for all columns.
      return row; 
    }
  });

  // Write Back the updated 8-column range.
  sheet.getRange(2, START_COL, finalWriteData.length, NUM_COLUMNS_TO_UPDATE).setValues(finalWriteData);
  console.log("Updated PO Database with Zoho Invoice details (including E-Way Bills).");
}

function update_data()

function update_data_manual()
{
  processPurchaseOrders_oneday();

function processPurchaseOrders_oneday() {
  updateZohoItemIDs();
  SpreadsheetApp.flush();
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const configSheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_CHANNEL_CONFIG);
  const logSheet = getOrCreateLogSheet(ss, SHEET_PO_REPO);
  const folder = DriveApp.getFolderById(DRIVE_FOLDER_ID);

  // --- NEW: Setup the Gmail Label ---
  const LABEL_NAME = 'ProcessedPO';
  let processedLabel = GmailApp.getUserLabelByName(LABEL_NAME);
  if (!processedLabel) {
    Logger.log(`Creating missing Gmail label: ${LABEL_NAME}`);
    processedLabel = GmailApp.createLabel(LABEL_NAME);
  }

  // 1. Get Config & Timer Logic
  const lastRow = configSheet.getLastRow();
  if (lastRow < 2) return;
  const configData = configSheet.getRange(2, 1, lastRow - 1, 4).getValues();
  const scriptProperties = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
  let startTime = parseInt(scriptProperties.getProperty('LAST_RUN_TIME') || '0');
  const oneDayAgo = new Date();
  oneDayAgo.setDate(oneDayAgo.getDate() - 1);
  startTime = Math.floor(oneDayAgo.getTime() / 1000);
  
  const currentRunTime = Math.floor(new Date().getTime() / 1000);
  const newLogs = [];
  
  // --- NEW: Track processed IDs during this run to prevent instant duplicates ---
  const processedMessageIds = new Set();

  // 2. Process Channels
  configData.forEach(row => {
    const [channelName, status, rawEmails, subjectKeyword] = row;
    if (!channelName || !rawEmails || String(status).toLowerCase() !== 'active') return;

    const channelKey = channelName.toLowerCase();
    const emailList = rawEmails.split(',').map(e => e.trim()).filter(Boolean);
    if (emailList.length === 0) return;
     
    const fromClause = `from:(${emailList.join(' OR ')})`;
    
    // --- THE CHANGE IS HERE: Exclude emails that already have the label ---
    let query = `${fromClause} -from:me after:${startTime} -label:${LABEL_NAME}`;
    if (subjectKeyword) query += ` subject:("${subjectKeyword}")`;

    try {
      const threads = GmailApp.search(query);
      if (threads.length === 0) return;

      const allThreadMessages = GmailApp.getMessagesForThreads(threads);
      allThreadMessages.forEach(messages => {
        messages.forEach(message => {
          // --- THE SECOND CHANGE IS HERE: Check the in-memory Set ---
          const messageId = message.getId();
          if (processedMessageIds.has(messageId)) return; // Skip if already seen this run
          
          if (Math.floor(message.getDate().getTime() / 1000) <= startTime) return;
          const sender = message.getFrom().toLowerCase();
          if (!emailList.some(e => sender.includes(e.toLowerCase()))) return;

          const attachments = message.getAttachments();
          const subject = message.getSubject();
          const emailBody = message.getPlainBody();
          const metadata = analyzeEmailMetadata(channelKey, subject, subject.toUpperCase(), emailBody);
          
          let successfullyProcessed = false; // Flag to track if we should label it

          if (attachments.length > 0) {
            // --- CASE 1: Attachments EXIST ---
            attachments.forEach(att => {
              const fileName = att.getName();
              try {
                const blob = att.copyBlob();
                if (fileName.toLowerCase().endsWith('.xls')) {
                  blob.setContentType(MimeType.MICROSOFT_EXCEL_LEGACY);
                }

                const file = folder.createFile(blob);
                file.setName(`[${channelName}] ${fileName}`);

                let finalPO = metadata.poNumber === "Not Found" ? extractPOFromText(channelKey, fileName.toUpperCase()) : metadata.poNumber;
                let finalCategory = metadata.category === "New PO" ? determineCategory(fileName.toUpperCase()) : metadata.category;

                newLogs.push([
                  message.getDate(), channelName, sender, subject, fileName,
                  file.getUrl(), finalCategory, finalPO, metadata.storeCode, ""
                ]);
                
                successfullyProcessed = true; // Mark as success

              } catch (e) {
                Logger.log(`ERROR: Failed to save attachment "${fileName}". Error: ${e.message}`);
                newLogs.push([
                  message.getDate(), channelName, sender, subject, fileName,
                  "SAVE FAILED", "Error", metadata.poNumber, metadata.storeCode, e.message
                ]);
              }
            });
          } else {
            // --- CASE 2: NO Attachments ---
            if (metadata.poNumber !== "Not Found") {
              newLogs.push([
                message.getDate(), channelName, sender, subject, "No Attachment",
                "", metadata.category, metadata.poNumber, metadata.storeCode, ""
              ]);
              successfullyProcessed = true; // Mark as success
            }
          }
          
          // --- FINAL STEP: Apply Label and remember the ID ---
          if (successfullyProcessed) {
            try {
              // Apply the label to the specific message's thread
              message.getThread().addLabel(processedLabel);
            } catch(e) {
              Logger.log(`Warning: Failed to apply label to message ${messageId}.`);
            }
            // Add the ID to our set to prevent duplicate processing in the same run
            processedMessageIds.add(messageId);
          }
          
        });
      });
    } catch (e) {
      console.error(`Error processing ${channelName}: ${e.message}`);
    }
  });

  // 3. Batch Write Logs & Update Timer
  if (newLogs.length > 0) {
    newLogs.sort((a, b) => new Date(a[0]) - new Date(b[0]));
    logSheet.getRange(logSheet.getLastRow() + 1, 1, newLogs.length, newLogs[0].length).setValues(newLogs);
    console.log(`Successfully processed ${newLogs.length} new log entries.`);
  }
  scriptProperties.setProperty('LAST_RUN_TIME', currentRunTime.toString());
}

/**
 * **MAIN FUNCTION:** Fetches a contact from Zoho Books by its ID, transforms the
 * data, and creates a corresponding B2B customer in EasyEcom.
 *
 * @param {string} contactId - The Zoho Books contact_id to sync.
 * @return {boolean} True on success, false on failure.
 */

function testtt()
{
  syncZohoContactToEasyEcom("1975394000200114770");
}
function syncZohoContactToEasyEcom(contactId) {
  if (!contactId) {
    Logger.log('ERROR: No Zoho Contact ID provided.');
    return false;
  }
  
  Logger.log(`--- Starting sync for Zoho Contact ID: ${contactId} ---`);

  try {
    // --- Step 1: Fetch Full Contact Details from Zoho Books ---
    const zohoContact = _fetchZohoContactDetails(contactId);
    debugLog(zohoContact,"")
    if (!zohoContact) {
      // The helper function will have already logged the specific error.
      return false; 
    }

    // --- Step 2: Create the Customer in EasyEcom using the Zoho data ---
    const success = _createEasyEcomCustomer(zohoContact);
    
    if (success) {
      fetchEasyEcomCustomers();
      Logger.log('--- Successfully synced Zoho contact to EasyEcom. ---');
      return true;
    } else {
      Logger.log('--- Failed to create customer in EasyEcom. ---');
      return false;
    }

  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log(`An unexpected error occurred during the sync process: ${e.message}`);
    return false;
  }
}


/**
 * **HELPER 1:** Fetches the details for a single contact from the Zoho Books API.
 * @param {string} contactId - The Zoho Books contact_id.
 * @return {object|null} The Zoho contact object, or null on failure.
 */
function _fetchZohoContactDetails(contactId) {
  const authToken = getZohoAccessToken(); // You need to implement this helper function
  const organizationId = '60032126274'; // As provided in your example
  
  const url = `https://www.zohoapis.in/books/v3/contacts/${contactId}?organization_id=${organizationId}`;
  
  const options = {
    'method': 'get',
    'headers': {
      'Authorization': `Zoho-oauthtoken ${authToken}` // Use the correct auth scheme (OAuth is recommended)
    },
    'muteHttpExceptions': true
  };
  
  try {
    const response = UrlFetchApp.fetch(url, options);
    //Logger.log(response);
    const responseData = JSON.parse(response.getContentText());
    
    if (response.getResponseCode() === 200 && responseData.contact) {
      Logger.log(`Successfully fetched contact "${responseData.contact.contact_name}" from Zoho.`);
      return responseData.contact;
    } else {
      throw new Error(`(Code: ${response.getResponseCode()}) ${response.getContentText()}`);
    }
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log(`ERROR fetching from Zoho: ${e.message}`);
    return null;
  }
}


/**
 * **UPDATED:** Creates a B2B customer in EasyEcom using data from a Zoho contact.
 * This version now includes a mapping to convert Zoho's state names (e.g., "Maharashtra")
 * into the numerical State IDs required by the EasyEcom API.
 *
 * @param {object} zohoContact - The contact object returned from the Zoho API.
 * @return {boolean} True on success, false on failure.
 */
function _createEasyEcomCustomer(zohoContact) {
  const token = getEasyEcomToken(); // Assumes this function exists
  const apiKey = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().getProperty('EASY_ECOM_API_KEY');
  if (!token || !apiKey) {
    Logger.log('ERROR: Missing EasyEcom token or API key.');
    return false;
  }
  
  // =========================================================================
  // THE CHANGE IS HERE: State Name to State ID Mapping
  // =========================================================================
  const stateNameToIdMap = {
    "Andhra Pradesh": 1, "Arunachal Pradesh": 2, "Assam": 3, "Bihar": 4,
    "Chhattisgarh": 5, "Goa": 6, "Gujarat": 7, "Haryana": 8, "Himachal Pradesh": 9,
    "Jammu & Kashmir": 10, "Jharkhand": 11, "Karnataka": 12, "Kerala": 13,
    "Madhya Pradesh": 14, "Maharashtra": 15, "Manipur": 16, "Meghalaya": 17,
    "Mizoram": 18, "Nagaland": 19, "Odisha": 20, "Punjab": 21, "Rajasthan": 22,
    "Sikkim": 23, "Tamil Nadu": 24, "Telangana": 25, "Tripura": 26,
    "Uttar Pradesh": 27, "Uttarakhand": 28, "West Bengal": 29, "Delhi": 30,
    "Puducherry": 31, "Andaman & Nicobar Islands": 32, "Chandigarh": 33,
    "Dadra & Nagar Haveli": 34, "Daman & Diu": 35, "Lakshadweep": 37,
    "Dadra & Nagar Haveli and Daman & Diu": 3848, "Ladakh": 3851
  };
  const NOT_AVAILABLE_ID = 3849; // The fallback ID for any state not found in the map.

  const url = "https://api.easyecom.io/Wholesale/CreateCustomer";
  
  // --- Data Mapping Logic ---
  const shippingAddress = zohoContact.shipping_address || {};
  const billingAddress = zohoContact.billing_address || {};

  // Safely get state names from Zoho data.
  const dispatchStateName = shippingAddress.state || '';
  const dispatchStateId = stateNameToIdMap[dispatchStateName] || NOT_AVAILABLE_ID;

  // Combine address lines safely.
  const fullBillingStreet = `${billingAddress.address || ''} ${billingAddress.street2 || ''}`.trim();
  const fullDispatchStreet = `${shippingAddress.address || ''} ${shippingAddress.street2 || ''}`.trim();

  const payload = {
    "companyName": zohoContact.contact_name,
    "taxIdentificationNumber": zohoContact.gst_no || "URP",
    "password": "test@1234",
    "email": zohoContact.email || "avinav@cubelelo.com",
    "contactNumber": String(zohoContact.phone || shippingAddress.phone || "0000000000").replace(/\D/g, '').slice(-10),    "country": "India",
    //"dispatchContactName": zohoContact.contact_name,
    //"billingContactName": zohoContact.company_name,
    "billingStateId": dispatchStateId, // Use the mapped ID
    "billingStreet": fullBillingStreet,
    "billingCity": billingAddress.city,
    "billingPostalCode": billingAddress.zip,
    "currency": "INR",
    "description": `Synced from Zoho Contact ID: ${zohoContact.contact_id}`,
    "dispatchStateId": dispatchStateId, // Use the mapped ID
    "dispatchStreet": fullDispatchStreet,
    "dispatchCity": shippingAddress.city,
    "dispatchPostalCode": shippingAddress.zip
  };
  //Logger.log(payload);
  
  const options = {
    'method': 'post',
    'headers': {
      'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + token,
      'x-api-key': apiKey,
      'Content-Type': 'application/json'
    },
    'payload': JSON.stringify(payload),
    'muteHttpExceptions': true
  };
  
// =========================================================================
  // THE CHANGE IS HERE: The try/catch block now returns objects instead of booleans.
  // =========================================================================
  try {
    const response = UrlFetchApp.fetch(url, options);
    const responseCode = response.getResponseCode();
    const responseText = response.getContentText();
    let responseData;
    
    // Always try to parse the JSON, as even errors contain useful messages.
    try {
      responseData = JSON.parse(responseText);
    } catch (jsonError) {
      // If parsing fails, the response was not valid JSON (e.g., an HTML error page).
      throw new Error(`API returned a non-JSON response (HTTP ${responseCode}): ${responseText.substring(0, 500)}`);
    }

    // =========================================================================
    // THE FIX IS HERE: A robust, two-level check for success.
    // =========================================================================
    
    // A true success requires BOTH a 200 HTTP code AND a 200 internal code.
    if (responseCode === 200 && responseData.code === 200) {
      Logger.log(`Successfully created customer "${payload.companyName}" in EasyEcom. API Message: ${responseData.message}`);
      return true;
    } else {
      // If either check fails, we have an error. Prioritize the message from the JSON.
      const errorMessage = responseData.message || "An unknown API error occurred.";
      throw new Error(`(HTTP ${responseCode}, API Code ${responseData.code}) - ${errorMessage}`);
    }

  } catch (e) {
    // This will now catch all thrown errors and log them clearly.
    Logger.log(`ERROR creating customer in EasyEcom: ${e.message}`);
    return false;
  }
}


zoho invoice creartion .gs

/**
 * **FINAL & COMPLETE:** Called from a front-end with a single EE Reference Code. It:
 * 1. Finds all matching rows in the 'PO_Database' sheet.
 * 2. Creates a draft invoice in Zoho Books.
 * 3. Immediately makes a second API call to mark the new invoice as "Sent".
 * 4. Triggers the e-invoice generation (push to IRP) during the status update.
 * 5. Returns a structured JSON object to the front-end.
 *
 * @param {string} eeReferenceCode - The 'EE Reference Code' to search for in the database.
 * @return {object} A JSON object with a status ('success' or 'error') and a detailed message/data.
 */


/**
 * **FINAL & CORRECTED:** Called from a front-end. It now uses the correct,
 * three-step API process to create a Zoho Invoice:
 * 1. Creates a draft invoice.
 * 2. Pushes the invoice to the IRP for e-invoicing using the dedicated endpoint.
 * 3. Marks the invoice as "Sent".
 *
 * @param {string} eeReferenceCode - The reference code to search for.
 * @return {object} A JSON object with a status and a detailed message.
 */
// =================================================================================
// ZOHO BOOKS - INVOICE CREATION & SYNC-BACK WORKFLOW
// =================================================================================

/**
 * **MAIN BACKEND FUNCTION:** Called from a front-end with a single EE Reference Code. It
 * orchestrates the entire 3-step invoice creation and e-invoicing process, and then
 * triggers a sync to write the results back to the PO_Database.
 *
 * @param {string} eeReferenceCode - The 'EE Reference Code' to search for in the database.
 * @return {object} A JSON object with a status ('success' or 'error') and a detailed message/data.
 */

function test_invoice() {
  createZohoInvoiceByReferenceCode("51024410004364");
}

function getZohoBranchConfigByLocationKey_(locationKey) {
  const key = String(locationKey || "").trim();

  // Default location = Chhattisgarh
  let branchStateCode = "CG";

  // Gujarat location
  if (key === "wo33387329284") {
    branchStateCode = "GJ";
  }

  const branchConfig = getBranchConfigByStateCode_(branchStateCode);

  if (!branchConfig) {
    throw new Error(
      `No branch config found for state: ${branchStateCode}. Run _cacheBranchGstMap() and check Branch List.`
    );
  }

  if (!branchConfig.branchId) {
    throw new Error(`Branch ID missing for state: ${branchStateCode}`);
  }

  return {
    branchStateCode: branchStateCode,
    branchId: branchConfig.branchId,
    vendorId: branchConfig.vendorId,
    branchName: branchConfig.branchName,
    gst: branchConfig.gst
  };
}

function getBranchConfigByStateCode_(stateCode) {
  if (!stateCode) return null;

  const raw = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().getProperty("BRANCH_STATE_MAP");

  if (!raw) {
    throw new Error("Branch state map not cached. Run _cacheBranchGstMap()");
  }

  const map = JSON.parse(raw);
  return map[String(stateCode).trim().toUpperCase()] || null;
}

/**
 * Converts GSTIN or state code into Zoho place_of_supply state code.
 *
 * Accepts:
 *  - GSTIN like 22ABCDE1234F1Z5 → CG
 *  - State code like CG → CG
 */
function getZohoStateCodeFromGstOrState_(value) {
  if (!value) return "";

  const input = String(value).trim().toUpperCase();

  // If already Zoho state code like CG, MH, DL, KA etc.
  if (/^[A-Z]{2}$/.test(input)) {
    return input;
  }

  // If GSTIN, get first 2 digits
  const gstStateCode = input.substring(0, 2);

  const stateMap = {
    "01": "JK",
    "02": "HP",
    "03": "PB",
    "04": "CH",
    "05": "UK",
    "06": "HR",
    "07": "DL",
    "08": "RJ",
    "09": "UP",
    "10": "BR",
    "11": "SK",
    "12": "AR",
    "13": "NL",
    "14": "MN",
    "15": "MZ",
    "16": "TR",
    "17": "ML",
    "18": "AS",
    "19": "WB",
    "20": "JH",
    "21": "OD",
    "22": "CG",
    "23": "MP",
    "24": "GJ",
    "25": "DD",
    "26": "DN",
    "27": "MH",
    "28": "AP",
    "29": "KA",
    "30": "GA",
    "31": "LD",
    "32": "KL",
    "33": "TN",
    "34": "PY",
    "35": "AN",
    "36": "TS",
    "37": "AP",
    "38": "LA"
  };

  return stateMap[gstStateCode] || "";
}


/**
 * Decides whether invoice is intrastate or interstate
 * and returns the correct Zoho tax_id.
 */
function getZohoTaxIdByBranchAndSupplyState_(branchStateCode, supplyStateCode) {
  const props = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();

  const igstTaxId = props.getProperty("ZOHO_IGST_TAX_ID");
  const intrastateTaxId = props.getProperty("ZOHO_INTRASTATE_GST_TAX_ID");

  if (!branchStateCode) {
    throw new Error("Branch state code is missing.");
  }

  // ---------------------------------------------------------
  // If GST / supply state is blank, treat as interstate
  // ---------------------------------------------------------
  const isSupplyStateBlank = !String(supplyStateCode || "").trim();

  const isInterState = isSupplyStateBlank
    ? true
    : String(branchStateCode).trim().toUpperCase() !== String(supplyStateCode).trim().toUpperCase();

  const taxId = isInterState ? igstTaxId : intrastateTaxId;

  if (!taxId) {
    throw new Error(
      `Tax ID missing in Script Properties. Required property: ${
        isInterState ? "ZOHO_IGST_TAX_ID" : "ZOHO_INTRASTATE_GST_TAX_ID"
      }`
    );
  }

  Logger.log(
    `Tax Decision → Branch State: ${branchStateCode}, ` +
    `Supply State: ${isSupplyStateBlank ? "BLANK / Treated as Interstate" : supplyStateCode}, ` +
    `Transaction Type: ${isInterState ? "Interstate / IGST" : "Intrastate / CGST+SGST"}, ` +
    `Tax ID: ${taxId}`
  );

  return {
    taxId: taxId,
    isInterState: isInterState,
    isSupplyStateBlank: isSupplyStateBlank
  };
}

function createZohoInvoiceByReferenceCode(eeReferenceCode) {
  if (!eeReferenceCode) {
    return { status: "error", message: "No EE Reference Code was provided." };
  }

  Logger.log(`--- Starting 3-Step Zoho Invoice & E-Invoice Process for: ${eeReferenceCode} ---`);

  try {
    const token = getZohoAccessToken();

    if (!token) {
      throw new Error("Could not get Zoho Access Token. Please check credentials and setup.");
    }

    const props = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
    const orgId = props.getProperty("ZOHO_ORG_ID");

    if (!orgId) {
      throw new Error("ZOHO_ORG_ID not configured in Script Properties.");
    }

    // ---------------------------------------------------------
    // Step 1: Read PO_Database
    // ---------------------------------------------------------

    const dbSheet = SpreadsheetApp.openById(SPREADSHEET_ID).getSheetByName(SHEET_PO_DB);

    if (!dbSheet) {
      throw new Error(`Sheet not found: ${SHEET_PO_DB}`);
    }

    if (dbSheet.getLastRow() < 2) {
      throw new Error("The PO_Database sheet is empty or has no data.");
    }

    const allData = dbSheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    const headers = allData.shift();

    const refCodeIndex = headers.indexOf("EE_reference_code");
    const contactIdIndex = headers.indexOf("Zoho Contact ID");
    const itemIdIndex = headers.indexOf("Zoho Item ID");
    const costIndex = headers.indexOf("Unit Cost (Tax Exclusive)");
    const shippedQtyIndex = headers.indexOf("EE_item_shipped_quantity");
    const invoiceIdIndex = headers.indexOf("Invoice Id");
    const channelNameIndex = headers.indexOf("Channel Name");
    const gstIndex = headers.indexOf("GST");
    const locationKeyIndex =headers.indexOf("Location_Key");

    if (
      [
        refCodeIndex,
        contactIdIndex,
        itemIdIndex,
        costIndex,
        shippedQtyIndex,
        invoiceIdIndex,
        channelNameIndex,
        gstIndex,
        locationKeyIndex
      ].includes(-1)
    ) {
      throw new Error(
        "One or more required columns could not be found in PO_Database. " +
        "Required: EE_reference_code, Zoho Contact ID, Zoho Item ID, Unit Cost (Tax Exclusive), " +
        "EE_item_shipped_quantity, Invoice Id, Channel Name, GST."
      );
    }

    const matchingRows = allData.filter(row => String(row[refCodeIndex]).trim() === eeReferenceCode);

    if (matchingRows.length === 0) {
      throw new Error(`No rows found for EE Reference Code: ${eeReferenceCode}`);
    }

    // ---------------------------------------------------------
    // Check if invoice already exists
    // ---------------------------------------------------------

    const existingInvoice = matchingRows.find(row => String(row[invoiceIdIndex]).trim() !== "");

    if (existingInvoice) {
      const existingInvoiceId = existingInvoice[invoiceIdIndex];

      Logger.log(`Invoice already exists for ${eeReferenceCode}: ${existingInvoiceId}`);

      return {
        status: "skipped",
        message: `Invoice already exists for ${eeReferenceCode}. Existing Invoice ID: ${existingInvoiceId}`
      };
    }

    const channelName = String(matchingRows[0][channelNameIndex] || "").trim();
    const channelKey = channelName.toLowerCase();

    // ---------------------------------------------------------
    // Determine branch state and supply state
    // ---------------------------------------------------------
    // You can set this in Script Properties:
    // ZOHO_BRANCH_STATE_CODE = CG
    //
    // If not set, default is CG.

    //const branchStateCode = String(props.getProperty("ZOHO_BRANCH_STATE_CODE") || "CG").trim().toUpperCase();

    const locationKey = matchingRows[0][locationKeyIndex];
    const branchConfig = getZohoBranchConfigByLocationKey_(locationKey);

    const branchStateCode = branchConfig.branchStateCode;
    const zohoBranchId = branchConfig.branchId;
    const zohoVendorId = branchConfig.vendorId;

    if (!zohoBranchId) {
      throw new Error(
        `Zoho Branch ID missing for branch state: ${branchStateCode}. ` +
        `Check Script Properties.`
      );
    }
    Logger.log(
    `Zoho Branch Decision → Location Key: ${locationKey || "DEFAULT"}, ` +
    `Branch State: ${branchStateCode}, Branch ID: ${zohoBranchId}, ` +
    `Vendor ID: ${zohoVendorId || "MISSING"}`
    );

    const gstOrSupplyValue = matchingRows[0][gstIndex];
    const rawGstOrSupplyValue = String(gstOrSupplyValue || "").trim();

    let supplyStateCode = "";

    if (rawGstOrSupplyValue) {
      supplyStateCode = getZohoStateCodeFromGstOrState_(rawGstOrSupplyValue);

      if (!supplyStateCode) {
        throw new Error(
         `Could not determine supply state from GST column value: ${gstOrSupplyValue}`
        );
      }
    } else {
      Logger.log(
     `GST / Supply State column is blank for ${eeReferenceCode}. Treating as interstate transaction.`
    );
    }

  const taxDecision = getZohoTaxIdByBranchAndSupplyState_(branchStateCode, supplyStateCode);
  const taxId = taxDecision.taxId;

    // ---------------------------------------------------------
    // Determine Invoice Number / Bill Number
    // ---------------------------------------------------------

    let finalInvoiceNumber = "";
    let finalBillNumber = "";

    if (channelKey === "amazon_fba") {
      Logger.log("Amazon_FBA channel detected. Getting FBA Shipment ID from sheet...");

      const fbaShipmentIdIndex = headers.indexOf("FBA Shipment IDs");

      if (fbaShipmentIdIndex === -1) {
        throw new Error("'FBA Shipment IDs' column not found in PO_Database.");
      }

      const fbaShipmentID = String(matchingRows[0][fbaShipmentIdIndex] || "").trim();

      if (fbaShipmentID) {
        finalInvoiceNumber = fbaShipmentID;
        finalBillNumber = fbaShipmentID;
      } else {
        throw new Error(
          `The 'FBA Shipment IDs' column is empty for EE Reference Code: ${eeReferenceCode}`
        );
      }

      Logger.log(
        `Using Invoice Number: ${finalInvoiceNumber} and Bill Number: ${finalBillNumber}`
      );
    }

    // ---------------------------------------------------------
    // Step 2: Create Zoho line items
    // ---------------------------------------------------------

    const lineItems = matchingRows.map(row => {
      const itemId = row[itemIdIndex];

      if (!itemId) {
        throw new Error(`Missing Zoho Item ID for a row with PO Ref: ${eeReferenceCode}.`);
      }

      const rate = parseFloat(row[costIndex]) || 0;
      const quantity = parseInt(row[shippedQtyIndex], 10) || 0;

      if (quantity <= 0) return null;

      return {
        item_id: itemId,
        rate: rate.toFixed(2),
        quantity: quantity,
        tax_id: taxId
      };
    }).filter(Boolean);

    Logger.log(lineItems);

    if (lineItems.length === 0) {
      throw new Error("No items with a shipped quantity > 0 were found.");
    }

    // ---------------------------------------------------------
    // Add Shipping Charges as separate line item
    // ---------------------------------------------------------

    const shippingIndex = headers.indexOf("Shipping Charge");

    if (shippingIndex !== -1) {
      const shippingCharge = parseFloat(matchingRows[0][shippingIndex]) || 0;

      if (shippingCharge > 0) {
        const shippingItemId = props.getProperty("ZOHO_SHIPPING_ITEM_ID");

        if (!shippingItemId) {
          throw new Error("ZOHO_SHIPPING_ITEM_ID not configured in Script Properties.");
        }

        Logger.log(`Adding Shipping Charges: ${shippingCharge}`);

        lineItems.push({
          item_id: shippingItemId,
          rate: shippingCharge.toFixed(2),
          quantity: 1,
          tax_id: taxId
        });
      }
    } else {
      Logger.log("Shipping Charge column not found in PO_Database.");
    }

    // ---------------------------------------------------------
    // Step 3: Create draft invoice
    // ---------------------------------------------------------

    const customerId = matchingRows[0][contactIdIndex];

    if (!customerId) {
      throw new Error("Zoho Contact ID is missing for this PO.");
    }

    const createPayload = {
    customer_id: customerId,
    reference_number: eeReferenceCode,
    branch_id: zohoBranchId,
    line_items: lineItems
    };

  // Pass place_of_supply only when available
  if (supplyStateCode) {
  createPayload.place_of_supply = supplyStateCode;
  }

    // ONLY pass invoice_number for Amazon FBA
    if (channelKey === "amazon_fba") {
      createPayload.invoice_number = finalInvoiceNumber;
    }

    let createUrl = `https://www.zohoapis.in/books/v3/invoices?organization_id=${orgId}`;

    if (channelKey === "amazon_fba") {
      createUrl += `&ignore_auto_number_generation=true`;
    }

    Logger.log(JSON.stringify(createPayload));

    const createOptions = {
      method: "post",
      headers: {
        Authorization: `Zoho-oauthtoken ${token}`
      },
      contentType: "application/json",
      payload: JSON.stringify(createPayload),
      muteHttpExceptions: true
    };

    const createResponse = UrlFetchApp.fetch(createUrl, createOptions);
    const createResponseText = createResponse.getContentText();
    const createResponseData = JSON.parse(createResponseText);

    if (createResponse.getResponseCode() !== 201) {
      throw new Error(`Failed to create draft invoice. Zoho API Error: ${createResponseText}`);
    }

    const newInvoiceId = createResponseData.invoice.invoice_id;
    const createdInvoiceNumber = createResponseData.invoice.invoice_number;

    Logger.log(
      `Step 1/3: Successfully created DRAFT invoice ${createdInvoiceNumber} ` +
      `(ID: ${newInvoiceId}).`
    );

    // ---------------------------------------------------------
    // Step 4: Push invoice to IRP
    // ---------------------------------------------------------

    Logger.log(`Step 2/3: Pushing invoice ${newInvoiceId} to IRP...`);

    const pushUrl =
      `https://www.zohoapis.in/books/v3/invoices/${newInvoiceId}/einvoice/push?organization_id=${orgId}`;

    const pushOptions = {
      method: "post",
      headers: {
        Authorization: `Zoho-oauthtoken ${token}`
      },
      contentType: "application/json",
      payload: JSON.stringify({}),
      muteHttpExceptions: true
    };

    const pushResponse = UrlFetchApp.fetch(pushUrl, pushOptions);
    const pushResponseText = pushResponse.getContentText();
    const pushResponseData = JSON.parse(pushResponseText);

    const isSuccessStatusCode =
      pushResponse.getResponseCode() >= 200 &&
      pushResponse.getResponseCode() < 300;

    if (isSuccessStatusCode && pushResponseData.code === 0) {
      Logger.log(`Step 2/3: Successfully pushed to IRP. Message: ${pushResponseData.message}`);

      if (channelKey !== "amazon_fba") 
      {
        processEwayBill_(createResponseData.invoice, branchStateCode, supplyStateCode);

      }

    } else {
      const errorMessage = pushResponseData.message || pushResponseText;

      throw new Error(
        `Invoice was created, but failed to push to IRP. Zoho's Response: ${errorMessage}`
      );
    }

    // ---------------------------------------------------------
    // Step 5: Mark invoice as sent
    // ---------------------------------------------------------

    Logger.log(`Step 3/3: Marking invoice ${newInvoiceId} as Sent...`);

    const updateStatusUrl =
      `https://www.zohoapis.in/books/v3/invoices/${newInvoiceId}/status/sent?organization_id=${orgId}`;

    const updateOptions = {
      method: "post",
      headers: {
        Authorization: `Zoho-oauthtoken ${token}`
      },
      contentType: "application/json",
      payload: JSON.stringify({}),
      muteHttpExceptions: true
    };

    const updateResponse = UrlFetchApp.fetch(updateStatusUrl, updateOptions);

    if (updateResponse.getResponseCode() !== 200) {
      throw new Error(
        `Invoice was pushed to IRP, but failed to mark as Sent. Error: ${updateResponse.getContentText()}`
      );
    }

    Logger.log("Step 3/3: Successfully marked invoice as Sent.");

    // ---------------------------------------------------------
    // Step 6: Create Purchase Bill for Amazon FBA
    // ---------------------------------------------------------

    let billCreationMessage = "";

    if (channelKey === "amazon_fba") {
  Logger.log("Channel is Amazon_FBA. Proceeding to create a Purchase Bill.");

  if (!supplyStateCode) {
    throw new Error(
      `Cannot create Amazon FBA Purchase Bill because supply state is missing for ${eeReferenceCode}.`
    );
  }

  // Bill branch should be the destination/supply state branch, e.g. MH
  const billBranchConfig = getBranchConfigByStateCode_(supplyStateCode);

  if (!billBranchConfig || !billBranchConfig.branchId) {
    throw new Error(
      `Could not determine Purchase Bill Branch ID for supply state: ${supplyStateCode}. ` +
      `Check Branch List and run _cacheBranchGstMap().`
    );
  }

  const branch_id = billBranchConfig.branchId;

  // Vendor should be the source/supply branch vendor, e.g. GJ vendor
  const vendor_id = zohoVendorId;

  if (!vendor_id) {
    throw new Error(
      `Could not determine Purchase Bill Vendor ID for source branch state: ${branchStateCode}. ` +
      `Check Vendor ID in Branch List.`
    );
  }

  // Tax for purchase bill:
  // Bill branch = supplyStateCode, Vendor state = branchStateCode
  const billTaxDecision = getZohoTaxIdByBranchAndSupplyState_(
    supplyStateCode,
    branchStateCode
  );

  const billTaxId = billTaxDecision.taxId;

  const billLineItems = lineItems.map(item => ({
    item_id: item.item_id,
    rate: item.rate,
    quantity: item.quantity,
    tax_id: billTaxId
  }));

  const billPayload = {
    vendor_id: vendor_id,
    reference_number: eeReferenceCode,
    branch_id: branch_id,
    bill_number: finalBillNumber,
    line_items: billLineItems
  };

  Logger.log("Purchase Bill Payload: " + JSON.stringify(billPayload));

  const billOptions = {
    method: "post",
    headers: {
      Authorization: `Zoho-oauthtoken ${token}`
    },
    contentType: "application/json",
    payload: JSON.stringify(billPayload),
    muteHttpExceptions: true
  };

  const billResponse = UrlFetchApp.fetch(
    `https://www.zohoapis.in/books/v3/bills?organization_id=${orgId}`,
    billOptions
  );

  const billResponseCode = billResponse.getResponseCode();
  const billResponseText = billResponse.getContentText();

  if (billResponseCode === 201) {
    const billResponseData = JSON.parse(billResponseText);

    billCreationMessage =
      ` A corresponding Purchase Bill (${billResponseData.bill.bill_number}) was also created.`;

    Logger.log(
      `Successfully created Purchase Bill. ` +
      `Bill Branch State: ${supplyStateCode}, Bill Branch ID: ${branch_id}, ` +
      `Vendor Source State: ${branchStateCode}, Vendor ID: ${vendor_id}.`
    );

  } else {
    throw new Error(
      `Invoice was finalized, but failed to create the Purchase Bill. Error: ${billResponseText}`
    );
  }
  }

    // ---------------------------------------------------------
    // Final Sync
    // ---------------------------------------------------------

    syncZohoInvoicesToDB();

    const successMessage =
      `Successfully created Zoho Invoice ${createdInvoiceNumber}, pushed to IRP, and marked as Sent.` +
      billCreationMessage;

    return {
      status: "success",
      message: successMessage,
      data: createResponseData.invoice
    };

  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log(`ERROR during Zoho Invoice Creation: ${e.message}`);

    return {
      status: "error",
      message: e.message
    };
  }
}

function processEwayBill_(invoiceObj, branchStateCode = "CG", supplyStateCode = "")
 {
  const token = getZohoAccessToken();
  const orgId = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().getProperty("ZOHO_ORG_ID");

  branchStateCode = String(branchStateCode || "CG").trim().toUpperCase();

  supplyStateCode = String(supplyStateCode || "").trim().toUpperCase();
  const taxDecision = getZohoTaxIdByBranchAndSupplyState_(branchStateCode, supplyStateCode);

  const isB2B = invoiceObj.gst_treatment === "business_gst";
  const invoiceValue = parseFloat(invoiceObj.total || 0);
  const isInterState = taxDecision.isInterState;

  Logger.log(
    `Eway Check → B2B: ${isB2B}, Value: ${invoiceValue}, ` +
    `Branch State: ${branchStateCode}, Supply State: ${supplyStateCode}, ` +
    `Interstate: ${isInterState}`
  );

  if (!(isB2B && invoiceValue > 50000 && isInterState)) {
    Logger.log("⏭️ Skipping Eway Bill (Conditions not met)");

    return {
      status: "skipped",
      reason: "Conditions not met",
      data: {
        isB2B,
        invoiceValue,
        isInterState,
        branchStateCode,
        supplyStateCode
      }
    };
  }

  Logger.log("✅ Conditions met. Creating Eway Bill Part A...");

  if (!supplyStateCode) {
    throw new Error("place_of_supply missing in invoice");
  }

  const url = `https://www.zohoapis.in/books/v3/ewaybills?organization_id=${orgId}`;

  const transporterId = getTransporterIdByName_("Delhivery");

  const payload = {
    transaction_type: "regular",
    sub_supply_type: "supply",
    entity_id: invoiceObj.invoice_id,
    entity_type: "invoice",
    ship_to_state_code: supplyStateCode,
    transporter_id: transporterId,
    transportation_mode: "road",
    distance: 0,
    action: "save_generate"
  };

  const options = {
    method: "post",
    headers: {
      Authorization: `Zoho-oauthtoken ${token}`
    },
    contentType: "application/x-www-form-urlencoded",
    payload: {
      JSONString: JSON.stringify(payload)
    },
    muteHttpExceptions: true
  };

  const response = UrlFetchApp.fetch(url, options);
  const code = response.getResponseCode();
  const text = response.getContentText();

  Logger.log("Eway Bill Response: " + text);

  if (code >= 200 && code < 300) {
    return {
      status: "success",
      message: "Eway Bill Part A created",
      data: JSON.parse(text)
    };
  }

  throw new Error("Eway Bill Failed: " + text);
}



function getTransporterIdByName_(name) {

  const token = getZohoAccessToken();
  const orgId = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().getProperty('ZOHO_ORG_ID');

  const url = `https://www.zohoapis.in/books/v3/ewaybills/transporters?organization_id=${orgId}`;

  const response = UrlFetchApp.fetch(url, {
    method: "get",
    headers: {
      "Authorization": `Zoho-oauthtoken ${token}`
    }
  });

  const data = JSON.parse(response.getContentText());

  const transporter = (data.transporters || []).find(t =>
    t.transporter_name.toLowerCase().includes(name.toLowerCase())
  );

  if (!transporter) {
    throw new Error(`Transporter not found: ${name}`);
  }

  return transporter.transporter_id; // ✅ correct ID
}
