/**
 * **OPTIMIZED & ROBUST:** Fetches the latest 10 invoices sorted by date to find
 * the highest invoice number. This is much faster than fetching all invoices and
 * more reliable than sorting by the invoice number string.
 *
 * @return {string|null} The new invoice number string, or null on failure.
 */
function _getNewZohoInvoiceNumber(token, orgId) {

  
  const invoicePrefix = 'BSPL/25-26/';
  
  // =========================================================================
  // THE FIX IS HERE: Fetch a small batch sorted by DATE.
  // =========================================================================
  const url = `https://www.zohoapis.in/books/v3/invoices?organization_id=${orgId}` +
              `&invoice_number_startswith=${encodeURIComponent(invoicePrefix)}` +
              `&sort_column=date&sort_order=D&per_page=20`; // Fetch latest 10 by invoice date
  
  const options = {
    'method': 'get',
    'headers': { 'Authorization': `Zoho-oauthtoken ${token}` },
    'muteHttpExceptions': true
  };
  
  try {
    const response = UrlFetchApp.fetch(url, options);
    if (response.getResponseCode() !== 200) {
      throw new Error(`Zoho API returned an error: ${response.getContentText()}`);
    }

    const data = JSON.parse(response.getContentText());
    
    // If no invoices with our prefix exist, this is the first one.
    if (!data.invoices || data.invoices.length === 0) {
      Logger.log(`No existing invoices found with prefix '${invoicePrefix}'. Starting with 1.`);
      return `${invoicePrefix}1`;
    }
    
    // --- Step 2: Find the highest number from the batch of recent invoices ---
    Logger.log(`Scanning the latest ${data.invoices.length} invoices to find the max number.`);
    
    const allNumbers = data.invoices.map(inv => {
      const match = inv.invoice_number.match(/BSPL\/25-26\/(\d+)/i);
      return match && match[1] ? parseInt(match[1], 10) : 0;
    });
    
    // Use Math.max() to find the true numerical maximum from the fetched batch.
    const lastNumber = Math.max(...allNumbers);
    const newNumber = lastNumber + 1;
    
    Logger.log(`Found max number ${lastNumber} from the recent batch. New number is ${newNumber}.`);
    return `${invoicePrefix}${newNumber}`;

  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log("Error fetching last invoice number: " + e.message);
    return null;
  }
}

// =================================================================================
// ZOHO BOOKS - ITEM ID SYNC
// =================================================================================

/**
 * **MAIN FUNCTION:** Fetches items from Zoho Books filtered by name (e.g., "Drift"),
 * matches them against the 'Master SKU Mapping' sheet, and updates the 'Zoho Item ID' column.
 */
function updateZohoItemIDs() {
  
  
  Logger.log('--- Starting Zoho Item ID Sync Process ---');

  // --- Step 1: Get credentials and fetch the filtered items from Zoho ---
  const token = getZohoAccessToken(); // Assumes this helper function exists
  if (!token) {
    Logger.log('Could not get Zoho token. Aborting.');
    return;
  }
  
  // Fetch all items from Zoho where the name contains "Drift".
  const zohoItemMap = _fetchZohoItems(token, "");
  if (zohoItemMap.size === 0) {
    Logger.log('No items containing "Drift" were found in Zoho Books.');
    return;
  }

  // --- Step 2: Read the Master SKU Mapping sheet ---
  const sheet = SpreadsheetApp.openById(SPREADSHEET_ID).getSheetByName(SHEET_INVENTORY);
  if (sheet.getLastRow() < 2) {
    Logger.log('Master SKU Mapping sheet is empty. Nothing to update.');
    return;
  }
  
  const allData = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
  const headers = allData.shift(); // Get headers and remove from data array

  // Find the column indexes dynamically. This is robust against column reordering.
  const masterSkuIndex = headers.indexOf('Master SKU');
  const zohoItemIdIndex = headers.indexOf('Zoho Item ID');

  if (masterSkuIndex === -1 || zohoItemIdIndex === -1) {
    Logger.log("Error: Could not find 'Master SKU' or 'Zoho Item ID' columns in the mapping sheet.");
    return;
  }

  // --- Step 3: Prepare the updates by matching Master SKUs to Zoho item names ---
  let updatedCount = 0;
  const updates = allData.map(row => {
    const masterSku = String(row[masterSkuIndex]).trim();
    
    // Look up the Master SKU in the map of items we fetched from Zoho.
    // The assumption is that the Zoho Item 'name' IS the 'Master SKU'.
    if (masterSku && zohoItemMap.has(masterSku)) {
      const itemId = zohoItemMap.get(masterSku);
      
      // If the ID is new, increment our counter.
      if (row[zohoItemIdIndex] !== itemId) {
        updatedCount++;
      }
      return [itemId]; // Return the ID to be placed in the Zoho Item ID column
    } else {
      // If no match is found, return the existing value to avoid overwriting it.
      return [row[zohoItemIdIndex]];
    }
  });

  // --- Step 4: Perform a single, efficient batch write operation ---
  if (updates.length > 0) {
    // Write the 'updates' array to the 'Zoho Item ID' column.
    sheet.getRange(2, zohoItemIdIndex + 1, updates.length, 1).setValues(updates);
    Logger.log(`Sync complete. Found matches and updated/verified ${updatedCount} Zoho Item IDs.`);
  }
}


/**
 * **HELPER:** Fetches all paginated items from Zoho Books that match a name filter.
 * @param {string} token - The Zoho API authentication token.
 * @param {string} filterText - The text to search for in the item names (e.g., "Drift").
 * @return {Map<string, string>} A Map where the key is the Item Name and the value is the Item ID.
 */
function _fetchZohoItems(token, filterText) {
  const props = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
  const orgId = props.getProperty('ZOHO_ORG_ID');  const encodedFilter = encodeURIComponent(filterText);
  const baseUrl = `https://www.zohoapis.in/books/v3/items?organization_id=${orgId}&name_contains=${encodedFilter}&page=`;
  
  const options = {
    method: "GET",
    headers: { "Authorization": "Zoho-oauthtoken " + token },
    muteHttpExceptions: true
  };

  const itemMap = new Map();
  let page = 1;
  let hasMore = true;

  Logger.log(`Fetching Zoho items with name containing "${filterText}"...`);
  while (hasMore) {
    try {
      const response = UrlFetchApp.fetch(baseUrl + page, options);
     Logger.log(response);

      if (response.getResponseCode() === 200) {
        const json = JSON.parse(response.getContentText());
        if (json.items && json.items.length > 0) {
          json.items.forEach(item => {
            // Create a map where the item name is the key and the ID is the value.
            itemMap.set(item.sku, item.item_id);
          });
          
          if (json.page_context && json.page_context.has_more_page) {
            page++;
          } else {
            hasMore = false;
          }
        } else {
          hasMore = false;
        }
      } else {
        Logger.log(`Zoho API Error: ${response.getContentText()}`);
        hasMore = false;
      }
    } catch (e) {
      Logger.log("Zoho Item Fetch Error: " + e.message);
      hasMore = false;
    }
  }
  
  Logger.log(`Fetched a total of ${itemMap.size} matching items from Zoho.`);
  return itemMap;
}

function FETCH_LAST_14_DAYS_QUOTATIONS() {
  try {
    const token = getZohoAccessToken();

    const props = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
    const ORG_ID = props.getProperty('ZOHO_ORG_ID');
    const BASE_URL = "https://www.zohoapis.in/books/v3/estimates";
    const DAYS = 14;

    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    let sheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_QUOTATIONS);

    const headers = [
      "Estimate ID",
      "Customer ID",
      "Customer Name",
      "Quotation Date",
      "Quote Number",
      "Reference Number",
      "Zoho Item ID",
      "SKU",
      "Item Name",
      "Rate",
      "Quantity",
      "Shipping Charges",
      "Tax Amount"
    ];

    sheet.clearContents();
    sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, headers.length).setValues([headers]);

    let page = 1;
    let allRows = [];

    const tz = ss.getSpreadsheetTimeZone();
    const dateAfter = new Date();
    dateAfter.setDate(dateAfter.getDate() - DAYS);
    const dateAfterStr = Utilities.formatDate(dateAfter, tz, "yyyy-MM-dd");

    const options = {
      method: "GET",
      headers: { "Authorization": "Zoho-oauthtoken " + token },
      muteHttpExceptions: true
    };

    while (true) {
      const url =
        `${BASE_URL}?organization_id=${ORG_ID}` +
        `&status=draft` +
        `&date_after=${dateAfterStr}` +
        `&page=${page}` +
        `&per_page=200`;

      const res = UrlFetchApp.fetch(url, options);
      const statusCode = res.getResponseCode();
      const json = JSON.parse(res.getContentText());

      if (statusCode !== 200) {
        throw new Error(json.message || "Failed to fetch quotations list");
      }

      if (!json.estimates || json.estimates.length === 0) break;

      json.estimates.forEach(est => {

        const detailUrl =
          `https://www.zohoapis.in/books/v3/estimates/${est.estimate_id}` +
          `?organization_id=${ORG_ID}`;

        const detailRes = UrlFetchApp.fetch(detailUrl, options);
        const detailCode = detailRes.getResponseCode();
        const detailJson = JSON.parse(detailRes.getContentText());

        if (detailCode !== 200) {
          throw new Error(
            `Failed to fetch estimate ${est.estimate_id}: ${detailJson.message}`
          );
        }

        const e = detailJson.estimate;
        if (!e || !e.line_items) return;

        const shippingCharge = e.shipping_charge || 0;
        const taxAmount = e.tax_total || 0;

        e.line_items.forEach(li => {
          allRows.push([
            e.estimate_id || "",
            e.customer_id || "",
            e.customer_name || "",
            e.date || "",
            e.estimate_number || "",
            e.reference_number || "",
            li.item_id || "",
            li.sku || "",
            li.name || "",
            li.rate || "",
            li.quantity || "",
            shippingCharge,
            taxAmount
          ]);
        });

      });

      if (!json.page_context || !json.page_context.has_more_page) break;
      page++;
    }

    if (allRows.length > 0) {
      sheet
        .getRange(2, 1, allRows.length, headers.length)
        .setValues(allRows);
    }

    return {
      status: "success",
      message: `Fetched ${allRows.length} quotation line items from last ${DAYS} days`,
      count: allRows.length
    };

  } catch (err) {
    Logger.log(`ERROR in FETCH_LAST_14_DAYS_QUOTATIONS: ${err.message}`);

    return {
      status: "error",
      message: err.message
    };
  }
}


function ENSURE_MASTER_SKU_MAPPINGS_BATCH(mappings) {
  if (!Array.isArray(mappings) || mappings.length === 0) {
    return { status: "ignored", message: "No mappings provided." };
  }

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const sheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_INVENTORY);
  if (!sheet) {
    return { status: "error", message: "Master SKU Mapping sheet not found." };
  }

  const lastRow = sheet.getLastRow();
  const existingData =
    lastRow > 1
      ? sheet.getRange(2, 1, lastRow - 1, 3).getValues()
      : [];

  // Build lookup set: channel|item|sku
  const existingSet = new Set(
    existingData.map(r =>
      `${r[0]}|${r[1]}|${r[2]}`.toLowerCase().trim()
    )
  );

  const rowsToInsert = [];

  mappings.forEach(m => {
    const key =
      `${m.channel}|${m.channelItemCode}|${m.masterSku}`.toLowerCase().trim();

    if (!existingSet.has(key)) {
      rowsToInsert.push([
        m.channel,
        m.channelItemCode,
        m.masterSku
      ]);
      existingSet.add(key); // prevent duplicates in same batch
    }
  });

  if (rowsToInsert.length > 0) {
    sheet
      .getRange(sheet.getLastRow() + 1, 1, rowsToInsert.length, 3)
      .setValues(rowsToInsert);
  }


  return {
    status: rowsToInsert.length ? "added" : "ignored",
    addedCount: rowsToInsert.length
  };
}

function SEND_AND_ACCEPT_ESTIMATE(data) {
  try {

    // ------------------ Validation ------------------
    if (!data || !data.estimateId || !Array.isArray(data.items) || data.items.length === 0) {
      return { status: "error", message: "Invalid data received from frontend." };
    }

    const estimateId = data.estimateId;
    const token = getZohoAccessToken();
    const ORG_ID = "60032126274";

    const options = {
      method: "POST",
      headers: {
        "Authorization": "Zoho-oauthtoken " + token
      },
      muteHttpExceptions: true
    };

    // ------------------ STEP 1: MARK AS SENT ------------------
    const sentUrl =
      `https://www.zohoapis.in/books/v3/estimates/${estimateId}/status/sent` +
      `?organization_id=${ORG_ID}`;

    const sentResp = UrlFetchApp.fetch(sentUrl, options);
    const sentCode = sentResp.getResponseCode();

    if (sentCode !== 200 && sentCode !== 409) {
      const sentResult = JSON.parse(sentResp.getContentText());
      throw new Error(`Failed to mark estimate as sent: ${sentResult.message}`);
    }

    Utilities.sleep(600);

    // ------------------ STEP 2: MARK AS ACCEPTED ------------------
    const acceptUrl =
      `https://www.zohoapis.in/books/v3/estimates/${estimateId}/status/accepted` +
      `?organization_id=${ORG_ID}`;

    const acceptResp = UrlFetchApp.fetch(acceptUrl, options);
    const acceptResult = JSON.parse(acceptResp.getContentText());

    if (acceptResp.getResponseCode() !== 200) {
      throw new Error(`Failed to accept estimate: ${acceptResult.message}`);
    }
    FETCH_LAST_14_DAYS_QUOTATIONS();
    SpreadsheetApp.flush();

    // ------------------ STEP 3: ADD TO PO DATABASE ------------------
    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    const poSheet = ss.getSheetByName("PO_Database");
    if (!poSheet) throw new Error("PO_Database sheet not found.");

    const today = Utilities.formatDate(
      new Date(),
      ss.getSpreadsheetTimeZone(),
      "yyyy-MM-dd"
    );
    
    const name = (data.customerName || "").trim();

    const channelName =
    /^bulk_/i.test(name) ? "Bulk" :
    /^event_/i.test(name) ? "Event" :
    "General";

    const storeCode = name.replace(/^(bulk_|event_)/i, "").trim();

    const poNumber = data.referenceNumber || data.quotationNumber;

    const poRows = [];
    const skuMappings = [];

    data.items.forEach(item => {

      poRows.push([
        "New",
        today,
        channelName,
        poNumber,
        storeCode,
        "",
        "",
        item.sku || "",
        item.sku || "",
        item.itemName || "",
        Number(item.quantity),
        "",
        Number(item.rate),
        "",
        item.zohoItemId || "",
        Number(item.quantity),
        "",
        data.customerId || ""
      ]);

      if (item.sku) {
        skuMappings.push({
          channel: "Bulk",
          channelItemCode: item.sku,
          masterSku: item.sku
        });
      }

    });

    // Insert rows
    const startRow = poSheet.getLastRow() + 1;

    poSheet
      .getRange(startRow, 1, poRows.length, poRows[0].length)
      .setValues(poRows);

    SpreadsheetApp.flush();


    // ------------------ STEP 3B: UPDATE SHIPPING CHARGE ------------------

    const shippingCharge = Number(data.shippingCharges || data.shippingCharge || 0);

    if (shippingCharge > 0) {

      const headers = poSheet.getRange(1,1,1,poSheet.getLastColumn()).getValues()[0];

      const shippingCol = headers.indexOf("Shipping Charge");

      if (shippingCol !== -1) {

        const shippingValues = new Array(poRows.length)
          .fill([shippingCharge]);

        poSheet
          .getRange(startRow, shippingCol + 1, poRows.length, 1)
          .setValues(shippingValues);

      } else {
        Logger.log("Shipping Charge column not found.");
      }

    }

    SpreadsheetApp.flush();


    // ------------------ STEP 4: UPDATE CUSTOMER IDS ------------------
    updateCustomerIdsInPoDatabase();


    // ------------------ STEP 5: ENSURE MASTER SKU MAPPING ------------------
    if (skuMappings.length > 0) {

      const mappingResult = ENSURE_MASTER_SKU_MAPPINGS_BATCH(skuMappings);

      SpreadsheetApp.flush();

      Logger.log("SKU Mapping Result: " + JSON.stringify(mappingResult));
    }
    updateZohoItemIDs();

    syncInventoryAndCalculateAllocation();

      // 3. Return the latest quotations list to the frontend
    const sheet_quote = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName(SHEET_QUOTATIONS);
    const data_quote = sheet_quote.getDataRange().getValues();
    const headers_quote = data_quote[0];
    const rows_quote = data_quote.slice(1);

    const freshQuotations = formatQuotationsForFrontend_(rows_quote, headers_quote);

    const responseData = JSON.parse(freshQuotations.getContentText());

    return { 
    status: 'success', 
    data: responseData.data,
    message: `Estimate ${quotationData.quotationNumber || estimateId} accepted, removed from local, and refreshed from Zoho.` 
  };
  }

 catch (err) {

    Logger.log(`ERROR in SEND_AND_ACCEPT_ESTIMATE: ${err.message}`);

    return {
      status: "error",
      message: err.message
    };

  }
}

// =================================================================================
// NIMBUS POST - AUTHENTICATION
// =================================================================================

/**
 * **NEW & ROBUST:** Fetches the authentication token from the Nimbus Post API.
 * This function is self-contained and uses standard Apps Script methods.
 *
 * @return {string|null} The authentication token string on success, or null on failure.
 */
function getNimbusPostToken() {

  Logger.log("ENTERED getNimbusPostToken");

  const props = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();

  const email = props.getProperty('NIMBUS_POST_EMAIL');
  const password = props.getProperty('NIMBUS_POST_PASSWORD');

  if (!email || !password) {
    throw new Error("NimbusPost credentials missing");
  }

  const TOKEN_KEY = "NIMBUS_TOKEN";
  const EXPIRY_KEY = "NIMBUS_TOKEN_EXPIRY";

  const existingToken = props.getProperty(TOKEN_KEY);
  const expiry = props.getProperty(EXPIRY_KEY);

  const now = new Date().getTime();

  // --------------------------------------------------
  // 1. RETURN EXISTING TOKEN IF VALID
  // --------------------------------------------------
  if (existingToken && expiry && now < Number(expiry)) {
    Logger.log("Using stored Nimbus token");
    return existingToken;
  }

  Logger.log("Fetching new Nimbus token...");

  // --------------------------------------------------
  // 2. FETCH NEW TOKEN
  // --------------------------------------------------
  const response = UrlFetchApp.fetch(
    "https://ship.nimbuspost.com/api/users/login",
    {
      method: "post",
      contentType: "application/json",
      payload: JSON.stringify({
        email: email,
        password: password
      }),
      muteHttpExceptions: true
    }
  );

  const responseText = response.getContentText();
  Logger.log("NIMBUS TOKEN RESPONSE: " + responseText);

  const json = JSON.parse(responseText);

  // ⚠️ Nimbus usually returns token inside data
  const token = json?.data;

  if (!token) {
    throw new Error("Nimbus token not received");
  }

  // --------------------------------------------------
  // 3. STORE TOKEN + EXPIRY
  // --------------------------------------------------
  // Nimbus token expiry not explicitly given → assume ~24 hours
  const expiryTime = now + (23 * 60 * 60 * 1000); // 23 hrs safe buffer

  props.setProperty(TOKEN_KEY, token);
  props.setProperty(EXPIRY_KEY, expiryTime.toString());

  Logger.log("New Nimbus token stored");

  return token;
}

function getShiprocketToken() {

  Logger.log("ENTERED getShiprocketToken");

  const props = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();

  const email = props.getProperty('SHIPROCKET_EMAIL');
  const password = props.getProperty('SHIPROCKET_PASSWORD');

  if (!email || !password) {
    throw new Error("Shiprocket credentials missing");
  }

  const TOKEN_KEY = "SHIPROCKET_TOKEN";
  const EXPIRY_KEY = "SHIPROCKET_TOKEN_EXPIRY";

  const existingToken = props.getProperty(TOKEN_KEY);
  const expiry = props.getProperty(EXPIRY_KEY);

  const now = new Date().getTime();

  // --------------------------------------------------
  // 1. RETURN EXISTING TOKEN IF VALID
  // --------------------------------------------------
  if (existingToken && expiry && now < Number(expiry)) {
    Logger.log("Using stored token");
    return existingToken;
  }

  Logger.log("Fetching new token...");

  // --------------------------------------------------
  // 2. FETCH NEW TOKEN
  // --------------------------------------------------
  const response = UrlFetchApp.fetch(
    "https://apiv2.shiprocket.in/v1/external/auth/login",
    {
      method: "post",
      contentType: "application/json",
      payload: JSON.stringify({
        email: email,
        password: password
      }),
      muteHttpExceptions: true
    }
  );

  const responseText = response.getContentText();
  Logger.log("TOKEN RESPONSE: " + responseText);

  const json = JSON.parse(responseText);

  if (!json.token) {
    throw new Error("Token not received");
  }

  const token = json.token;

  // --------------------------------------------------
  // 3. STORE TOKEN + EXPIRY
  // --------------------------------------------------
  const expiryTime = now + (55 * 60 * 1000); // 55 mins

  props.setProperty(TOKEN_KEY, token);
  props.setProperty(EXPIRY_KEY, expiryTime.toString());

  Logger.log("New token stored");

  return token;
}



function createShipment(eeReferenceCode,courier_id) {

  if (!eeReferenceCode) {
    return { status: "error", message: "No EE Reference Code provided" };
  }

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.openById(SPREADSHEET_ID);
  const dbSheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_PO_DB);

  const data = dbSheet.getDataRange().getValues();
  const headers = data.shift();

  const refIdx = headers.indexOf("EE_reference_code");
  const channelIdx = headers.indexOf("Channel Name");
  const boxIdx = headers.indexOf("Box Data");

  const row = data.find(r => String(r[refIdx]).trim() === eeReferenceCode);

  if (!row) {
    Logger.log("Order Not found");
    return { status: "error", message: "Order not found" };
  }

  const channel = String(row[channelIdx]).trim();
  const boxCount = Number(row[boxIdx]) || 0;

  const excluded = [
    "Instamart","Zepto","BB","RBL",
    "FlipkartMinutes","Blinkit","Amazon_FBA"
  ];

  const useShiprocket = !excluded.includes(channel) && boxCount === 1;
  Logger.log(channel);
  Logger.log(boxCount);

  Logger.log(useShiprocket);

  if (useShiprocket) {
    return createShiprocketShipment(eeReferenceCode);
  } else {
    return createNimbusPostShipment(eeReferenceCode,courier_id);
  }
}

function createShiprocketShipment(eeReferenceCode) {

  Logger.log(`--- Starting Shiprocket Shipment Creation for: ${eeReferenceCode} ---`);

  /*const lock = LockService.getScriptLock();
  if (!lock.tryLock(30000)) {
    return { status: "skipped", message: "Already processing" };
  }
  */

  let rowsToMark = [];
  let dbSheet;

  // ---------------- HELPERS ----------------
  const toStr = (val) => val ? String(val).trim() : "";
  const toInt = (val, def = 1) => {
    const n = parseInt(val);
    return isNaN(n) ? def : n;
  };
  const toFloat = (val, def = 0) => {
    const n = parseFloat(val);
    return isNaN(n) ? def : n;
  };

  try {

    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.openById(SPREADSHEET_ID);
    dbSheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_PO_DB);

    const dbData = dbSheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    const headers = dbData.shift();

    const refIdx = headers.indexOf("EE_reference_code");
    const awbIdx = headers.indexOf("AWB");

    // ---------------- DUPLICATE CHECK ----------------
    const existing = dbData.find(r =>
      String(r[refIdx]).trim() === eeReferenceCode &&
      String(r[awbIdx]).trim() !== ""
    );

    if (existing) {
      Logger.log('skipped');
      return {
        status: "skipped",
        message: "Shipment already exists",
        awb: existing[awbIdx]
      };
    }

    // ---------------- MARK PROCESSING ----------------
    rowsToMark = dbData
      .map((r, i) => String(r[refIdx]).trim() === eeReferenceCode ? i + 2 : null)
      .filter(Boolean);

    rowsToMark.forEach(r => {
      dbSheet.getRange(r, awbIdx + 1).setValue("PROCESSING");
    });

    // ---------------- LOAD DATA ----------------
    const customerMap = _loadEECustomerData(ss);
    const packingData = _loadPackingData(ss, eeReferenceCode);
    const orderData = _loadOrderData(ss, eeReferenceCode);


    const cleanName = (name) => {return (name || "").replace(/^Bulk_/, "").trim();};
    const splitName = (name) => {const parts = name.split(" ");return {first: parts[0] || "Customer",last: parts.slice(1).join(" ") || "."};};

    const customer = customerMap.get(orderData.customerId);
    if (!customer) {
      Logger.log("Customer NOT FOUND for ID: " + orderData.customerId);
      throw new Error("Customer not found");
    }
    const cleanedName = cleanName(customer['Company Name']);
    const nameObj = splitName(cleanedName);

    

    const getVal = (row, col) => row[headers.indexOf(col)];
    const firstItem = orderData.items[0];

    // ---------------- ORDER VALUE ----------------
    const invoiceDate = new Date(getVal(firstItem, 'Invoice Date'));
    const invoiceValue = toFloat(getVal(firstItem, 'Invoice Total'), 0);
    const baseShipping = toFloat(getVal(firstItem, 'Shipping Charge'), 0);
    const shippingCharge = baseShipping * 1.05; // +5%
    const finalOrderValue = invoiceValue;

    // ---------------- PACKING ----------------
    const box = packingData[0]; // take first row only
    if (!box) {
      throw new Error("Packing data missing");
      }
    const weightGrams = toFloat(box['Box Weight'], 500);
    const length = toInt(box['Box Length'], 10);
    const breadth = toInt(box['Box Width'], 10);
    const height = toInt(box['Box Height'], 10);
    
    // convert to kg
    let weightKg = weightGrams / 1000;
    // safety fallback
    if (weightKg <= 0) weightKg = 0.5;

    // ---------------- ITEMS ----------------
    const items = orderData.items.map(row => ({
      name: toStr(getVal(row, 'Item Name')),
      sku: toStr(getVal(row, 'Master SKU')),
      units: toInt(getVal(row, 'Qty'), 1),
      selling_price: toFloat(getVal(row, 'Unit Cost (Tax Exclusive)'), 0),
      tax: "5"
    }));

    // ---------------- TOKEN ----------------
    const token = getShiprocketToken();
    if (!token) throw new Error("Token failed");

    // ---------------- FINAL PAYLOAD ----------------
    const payload = {
      request_pickup: true,
      print_label: true,
      generate_manifest: true,
      insurance: false,
      is_insured: 0, 

      order_id: eeReferenceCode,
      order_date: Utilities.formatDate(invoiceDate, "Asia/Kolkata", "yyyy-MM-dd"),

      billing_customer_name: nameObj.first,
      billing_last_name: nameObj.last,
      billing_address: toStr(customer['Billing Street']),
      billing_city: toStr(customer['Billing City']),
      billing_pincode: toInt(customer['Billing Zip']),
      billing_state: toStr(customer['Billing State']),
      billing_country: "India",
      billing_email: toStr(customer['Support Email']),
      billing_phone: toStr(customer['Support Contact']).replace(/\.0$/, ""),

      shipping_is_billing: true,

      order_items: items,

      payment_method: "Prepaid",
      sub_total: finalOrderValue,
      shipping_charges : shippingCharge,


      weight: weightKg.toFixed(2),
      length: length,
      breadth: breadth,
      height: height,

      pickup_location: "warehouse-2"
    };

    Logger.log("FORWARD PAYLOAD: " + JSON.stringify(payload));

    // ---------------- API CALL ----------------
    const res = UrlFetchApp.fetch(
      "https://apiv2.shiprocket.in/v1/external/shipments/create/forward-shipment",
      {
        method: "post",
        headers: {
          Authorization: `Bearer ${token}`,
          "Content-Type": "application/json"
        },
        payload: JSON.stringify(payload),
        muteHttpExceptions: true
      }
    );

    Logger.log("FORWARD RESPONSE: " + res.getContentText());

    

    const json = JSON.parse(res.getContentText());
    const payloadRes = json.payload || {};
    const awb = payloadRes.awb_code;
    const courier = payloadRes.courier_name || "Shiprocket";
    const labelUrl = payloadRes.label_url;

    if (!awb) throw new Error("AWB not generated");

    const trackingUrl = `https://shiprocket.co/tracking/${awb}`;

    // ---------------- UPDATE DB ----------------
    const carrierIdx = headers.indexOf('Carrier');
    const trackingIdx = headers.indexOf('Tracking Status');
    const trackingUrlIdx = headers.indexOf('Tracking URL');
    const labelIdx = headers.indexOf('Label URL');
    const bookedDateIdx = headers.indexOf('Booked Date');
    const pickupDateIdx = headers.indexOf('Pickup Date');

  rowsToMark.forEach(r => {

  const now = new Date();

  // ---------------- TODAY DATE ----------------
  const today = new Date(now);

  // ---------------- PICKUP DATE LOGIC ----------------
  const hourIST = Utilities.formatDate(now, "Asia/Kolkata", "HH");
  
  let pickupDate = new Date(now);

  if (parseInt(hourIST) >= 14) {
    pickupDate.setDate(pickupDate.getDate() + 1);
  }

  // ---------------- UPDATE ----------------
  dbSheet.getRange(r, awbIdx + 1).setValue(awb);
  dbSheet.getRange(r, carrierIdx + 1).setValue(courier + " (SR)");

  if (trackingIdx !== -1) {
    dbSheet.getRange(r, trackingIdx + 1).setValue("AWB Assigned");
  }

  if (bookedDateIdx !== -1) {
    dbSheet.getRange(r, bookedDateIdx + 1).setValue(today);
  }

  if (pickupDateIdx !== -1) {
    dbSheet.getRange(r, pickupDateIdx + 1).setValue(pickupDate);
  }

  if (trackingUrlIdx !== -1) {
    dbSheet.getRange(r, trackingUrlIdx + 1).setValue(trackingUrl);
  }

  if (labelIdx !== -1) {
    dbSheet.getRange(r, labelIdx + 1).setValue(labelUrl);
  }
  });

  return {
      status: "success",
      awb,
      courier,
      label: labelUrl,
      tracking: trackingUrl
    };

  }
  catch (e) {

    if (rowsToMark.length && dbSheet) {
      const headers = dbSheet.getDataRange().getValues()[0];
      const awbIdx = headers.indexOf("AWB");
      rowsToMark.forEach(r => {
        dbSheet.getRange(r, awbIdx + 1).setValue("");
      });
    }

    return { status: "error", message: e.message };

  } finally {
    //lock.releaseLock();
  }
}

function createNimbusPostShipment(eeReferenceCode,courier_id) {

  if (!eeReferenceCode) {
    return { status: "error", message: "No EE Order Reference ID provided." };
  }

  const lock = LockService.getScriptLock();
  if (!lock.tryLock(30000)) {
    return {
      status: "skipped",
      message: "Shipment creation already in progress."
    };
  }

  Logger.log(`--- Nimbus Shipment Start: ${eeReferenceCode} ---`);

  let rowsToMark = [];
  let awbIndex = -1;
  let refIdIndex = -1;

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.openById(SPREADSHEET_ID);
  const dbSheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_PO_DB);

  try {

    // --------------------------------------------------
    // READ DB
    // --------------------------------------------------
    const dbData = dbSheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    const headers = dbData.shift();

    refIdIndex = headers.indexOf('EE_reference_code');
    awbIndex = headers.indexOf('AWB');

    if (refIdIndex === -1 || awbIndex === -1) {
      throw new Error("Missing required columns");
    }

    // --------------------------------------------------
    // CHECK IF ALREADY CREATED
    // --------------------------------------------------
    const blockingRow = dbData.find(row => {
      return (
        String(row[refIdIndex]).trim() === eeReferenceCode &&
        String(row[awbIndex]).trim() !== ""
      );
    });

    if (blockingRow) {
      return {
        status: "skipped",
        message: "Shipment already exists",
        awb: blockingRow[awbIndex]
      };
    }

    // --------------------------------------------------
    // MARK PROCESSING
    // --------------------------------------------------
    rowsToMark = dbData
      .map((row, i) =>
        String(row[refIdIndex]).trim() === eeReferenceCode ? i + 2 : null
      )
      .filter(Boolean);

    rowsToMark.forEach(r => {
      dbSheet.getRange(r, awbIndex + 1).setValue("PROCESSING");
    });

    // --------------------------------------------------
    // LOAD DATA
    // --------------------------------------------------
    const customerMap = _loadEECustomerData(ss);
    const packingData = _loadPackingData(ss, eeReferenceCode);
    const orderData = _loadOrderData(ss, eeReferenceCode);

    if (!orderData.items.length) {
      throw new Error("No items found");
    }

    if (!customerMap.has(orderData.customerId)) {
      throw new Error("Customer not found");
    }

    // --------------------------------------------------
    // BUILD PAYLOAD
    // --------------------------------------------------
    const payload = _buildNimbusPayload(
      eeReferenceCode,
      orderData,
      customerMap.get(orderData.customerId),
      packingData,
      dbSheet,
      courier_id
    );

    Logger.log("PAYLOAD: " + JSON.stringify(payload));

    // --------------------------------------------------
    // 🔥 API CALL (WITH RETRY)
    // --------------------------------------------------
    const responseData = nimbusFetchWithRetry(
      "https://ship.nimbuspost.com/api/shipmentcargo/create",
      payload
    );

    if (!responseData.status) {
      throw new Error(responseData.message || "Nimbus API error");
    }

    const nimbus = responseData.data;
    const awbNumber = nimbus.awb_number;

    const token = getNimbusPostToken(); // fresh or cached

    // --------------------------------------------------
    // LABEL
    // --------------------------------------------------
    const mpsLabelUrl = getNimbusMpsLabel([awbNumber], token);
    const trackingUrl = `https://ship.nimbuspost.com/shipping/tracking/${awbNumber}`;

    // --------------------------------------------------
    // UPDATE SHEET
    // --------------------------------------------------
    const carrierIndex = headers.indexOf('Carrier');
    const trackingIndex = headers.indexOf('Tracking Status');
    const trackingUrlIndex = headers.indexOf('Tracking URL');
    const bookedDateIndex = headers.indexOf('Booked Date');
    const pickupDateIndex = headers.indexOf('Pickup Date');
    const labelIndex = headers.indexOf('Label URL');

    rowsToMark.forEach(row => {

      const now = new Date();

      let pickupDate = new Date(now);
      const hourIST = parseInt(
        Utilities.formatDate(now, "Asia/Kolkata", "HH"),
        10
      );

      if (hourIST >= 14) pickupDate.setDate(pickupDate.getDate() + 1);
      if (pickupDate.getDay() === 0) pickupDate.setDate(pickupDate.getDate() + 1);

      dbSheet.getRange(row, carrierIndex + 1)
        .setValue(nimbus.courier_name + " (NP)");

      dbSheet.getRange(row, awbIndex + 1)
        .setValue(awbNumber);

      if (trackingIndex !== -1) {
        dbSheet.getRange(row, trackingIndex + 1)
          .setValue(nimbus.status);
      }

      if (trackingUrlIndex !== -1) {
        dbSheet.getRange(row, trackingUrlIndex + 1)
          .setValue(trackingUrl);
      }

      if (bookedDateIndex !== -1) {
        dbSheet.getRange(row, bookedDateIndex + 1)
          .setValue(now);
      }

      if (pickupDateIndex !== -1) {
        dbSheet.getRange(row, pickupDateIndex + 1)
          .setValue(pickupDate);
      }

      if (labelIndex !== -1 && mpsLabelUrl) {
        dbSheet.getRange(row, labelIndex + 1)
          .setValue(mpsLabelUrl);
      }
    });

    return {
      status: "success",
      message: "Shipment created",
      awb: awbNumber
    };

  } catch (e) {

    // --------------------------------------------------
    // CLEANUP
    // --------------------------------------------------
    if (rowsToMark.length && awbIndex !== -1) {
      rowsToMark.forEach(r => {
        dbSheet.getRange(r, awbIndex + 1).setValue("");
      });
    }

    Logger.log("ERROR: " + e.message);

    return {
      status: "error",
      message: e.message
    };

  } finally {
    lock.releaseLock();
  }
}

function callNimbus(url, payload, token) {
  const response = UrlFetchApp.fetch(url, {
    method: "post",
    headers: {
      Authorization: `Bearer ${token}`,
      "Content-Type": "application/json"
    },
    payload: JSON.stringify(payload),
    muteHttpExceptions: true
  });

  const code = response.getResponseCode();
  const text = response.getContentText();

  Logger.log("Nimbus HTTP CODE: " + code);
  Logger.log("Nimbus RAW RESPONSE: " + text);

  try {
    return JSON.parse(text);
  } catch (e) {
    return {
      status: false,
      message: "Invalid JSON response from Nimbus: " + text
    };
  }
}
function nimbusFetchWithRetry(url, payload) {
  let token = getNimbusPostToken();

  let res = callNimbus(url, payload, token);

  const msg = String(res.message || "").toLowerCase();

  const authFailed =
    !res.status &&
    (
      msg.includes("invalid token") ||
      msg.includes("invalid authorization") ||
      msg.includes("unauthorized") ||
      msg.includes("authorization")
    );

  if (authFailed) {
    Logger.log("Nimbus auth failed. Clearing stored token and retrying...");

    const props = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
    props.deleteProperty("NIMBUS_TOKEN");
    props.deleteProperty("NIMBUS_TOKEN_EXPIRY");

    token = getNimbusPostToken();
    res = callNimbus(url, payload, token);
  }

  return res;
}
function test_mps()
{
  var token = getNimbusPostToken();
  getNimbusMpsLabel([303108022],token);

}

function getNimbusMpsLabel(masterAwbs, token) {

  if (!masterAwbs || masterAwbs.length === 0) return "";

  try {

    const response = UrlFetchApp.fetch(
      "https://ship.nimbuspost.com/api/shipmentcargo/generate_mps_label",
      {
        method: "post",
        headers: {
          Authorization: `Bearer ${token}`,
          "Content-Type": "application/json"
        },
        payload: JSON.stringify({
          master_awbs: masterAwbs
        }),
        muteHttpExceptions: true
      }
    );

    const json = JSON.parse(response.getContentText());

    if (json.status && json.data) {
      Logger.log(json.data);
      return json.data; // MPS label URL
    }

    Logger.log("MPS label failed: " + response.getContentText());
    return "";

  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log("MPS error: " + e.message);
    return "";
  }
}

// --- DATA GATHERING HELPERS ---

function _loadEECustomerData(ss) {
  const sheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_EE_CUSTOMERS);
  const data = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
  const headers = data.shift();
  const map = new Map();
  // Dynamically find columns
  const idIndex = headers.indexOf('Customer ID');
  // ... find other necessary customer column indexes ...
  data.forEach(row => {
    const customerId = row[idIndex];
    if (customerId) {
      // Store the entire row object for easy access
      map.set(customerId.toString(), Object.fromEntries(headers.map((key, i) => [key, row[i]])));
    }
  });
  return map;
}

function _loadPackingData(ss, eeReferenceCode) {
  const sheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_MASTER_DATA);
  const data = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
  const headers = data.shift();
  const refCodeIndex = headers.indexOf('Reference Code');
  
  return data
    .filter(row => String(row[refCodeIndex]).trim() === eeReferenceCode)
    .map(row => Object.fromEntries(headers.map((key, i) => [key, row[i]])));
}

function _loadOrderData(ss, eeReferenceCode) {
  const sheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_PO_DB);
  const data = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
  const headers = data.shift();
  const refIdIndex = headers.indexOf('EE_reference_code');
  const customerIdIndex = headers.indexOf('EE Customer ID');
  
  const items = data.filter(row => String(row[refIdIndex]).trim() === eeReferenceCode);
  const customerId = items.length > 0 ? items[0][customerIdIndex] : null;

  return { items: items, customerId: customerId.toString() };
}

// --- PAYLOAD BUILDER HELPER ---

function _buildNimbusPayload(eeReferenceCode,orderData, customerDetails, packingData,dbSheet,courier_id) {
  // --- Consignee & Invoice Details ---
  const firstItem = orderData.items[0];
  const orderHeaders = dbSheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, 40).getValues()[0]; // Get headers once
  
  const getVal = (row, colName) => row[orderHeaders.indexOf(colName)];

  const invoiceNumber = getVal(firstItem, 'Invoice Number');
  const invoiceDate = new Date(getVal(firstItem, 'Invoice Date'));
  const invoiceValue = parseFloat(getVal(firstItem, 'Invoice Total'));
  const ewbRaw = getVal(firstItem, 'EWB');
  const ewb = ewbRaw ? String(ewbRaw).trim() : "";

  // 🚨 EWB Validation
  if (invoiceValue >= 50000 && !ewb) {
    throw new Error(`EWB is mandatory for invoice value ≥ 50,000. Missing for Order: ${eeReferenceCode}`);
  }



  // --- Group Packing Data by Box ID to create the 'products' array ---
  const boxes = packingData.reduce((acc, item) => {
    const boxId = item['Box ID'];
    if (!acc[boxId]) {
      acc[boxId] = {
        box_weight: 0,
        box_length: 0,
        box_breadth: 0,
        box_height: 0,
        box_price: 0
      };
    }
    acc[boxId].box_weight = parseFloat(item['Box Weight']);
    acc[boxId].box_length = Math.max(acc[boxId].box_length, parseFloat(item['Box Length']));
    acc[boxId].box_breadth = Math.max(acc[boxId].box_breadth, parseFloat(item['Box Width']));
    acc[boxId].box_height = Math.max(acc[boxId].box_height, parseFloat(item['Box Height']));
    acc[boxId].box_price += parseFloat(item['Value']);
    return acc;
  }, {});

  const productsArray = Object.values(boxes).map(box => ({
    "product_name": "Puzzles", // Or derive from item names if needed
    "product_hsn_code": "95036090", // Or derive from a master data sheet
    "product_lbh_unit": "cm",
    "no_of_box": "1",
    "product_tax_per": "5",
    "product_price": box.box_price.toFixed(2),
    "product_weight_unit": "gram",
    "product_length": box.box_length,
    "product_breadth": box.box_breadth,
    "product_height": box.box_height,
    "product_weight": box.box_weight
  }));

  // --- Construct the Final Payload ---
  const payload = {
    "order_id": eeReferenceCode,
    "payment_method": "prepaid",
    "consignee_name": customerDetails['Company Name'],
    "consignee_company_name": customerDetails['Company Name'],
    "consignee_phone": customerDetails['Support Contact'],
    "consignee_email": customerDetails['Support Email'],
      // GST blank if value is URP
    "consignee_gst_number":
    String(customerDetails['GST'] || "").trim().toUpperCase() === "URP"
      ? ""
      : customerDetails['GST'],
    "consignee_address": customerDetails['Billing Street'],
    "consignee_pincode": customerDetails['Billing Zip'],
    "consignee_city": customerDetails['Billing City'],
    "consignee_state": customerDetails['Billing State'],
    "no_of_invoices": "1",
    "no_of_boxes": productsArray.length.toString(),
    "courier_id": String(courier_id || "110"), //Default fallback to Delhivery Bulk
    "request_auto_pickup": "yes",
    "invoice": [{
      "invoice_number": invoiceNumber,
      "invoice_date": Utilities.formatDate(invoiceDate, "GMT", "dd-MM-yyyy"),
      "invoice_value": invoiceValue,
      "ebn_number": ewb || ""
    }],
    "pickup": {
      "warehouse_name": "Brainlytic Solutions Private Limited", // Hard-coded as per example
      "name": "Mohan Dewangan",
      "address": "Khasra No. 325/5 325/22, Ring Road No, 1, DD Nagar, Raipura,",
      "address_2": "Near Shree Siddhi Vinayak Marriage Palace, Vinayaka Vihar",
      "city": "Raipur",
      "state": "Chhattisgarh",
      "pincode": "492013",
      "phone": "8103733766",
      "gst_number": "22AAICB3513C1ZF"
    },
    "products": productsArray
  };
  
  return payload;
}

// =.===============================================================================
// NIMBUS POST - BULK TRACKING STATUS UPDATE (OPTIMIZED)
// =================================================================================

/**
 * **MAIN FUNCTION:** Fetches the latest tracking status from Nimbus Post for all
 * non-delivered shipments and performs an efficient batch update on the 'PO_Database' sheet.
 */


function handleNimbusWebhook(data) 
{

  try {

    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    const sheet = ss.getSheetByName("PO_Database");

    const awb = String(data.awb_number).trim();
    const status = data.status || "";
    const message = data.message || "";
    const eventTime = data.event_time || "";
    const location = data.location || "";

    const range = sheet.getDataRange();
    const values = range.getValues();
    const headers = values[0];

    const awbIndex = headers.indexOf("AWB");
    const statusIndex = headers.indexOf("Tracking Status");
    const latestStatusIndex = headers.indexOf("Latest Status");
    const statusDateIndex = headers.indexOf("Latest Status Date");
    const locationIndex = headers.indexOf("Current Location");
    const deliveredIndex = headers.indexOf("Delivered Date");

    if (awbIndex === -1) {
      return responseJSON({status:'error',message:'AWB column missing'});
    }

    for (let i = 1; i < values.length; i++) {

      if (String(values[i][awbIndex]).trim() === awb) {

        if (statusIndex !== -1)
          sheet.getRange(i+1,statusIndex+1).setValue(status);

        if (latestStatusIndex !== -1)
          sheet.getRange(i+1,latestStatusIndex+1).setValue(message);

        if (statusDateIndex !== -1)
          sheet.getRange(i+1,statusDateIndex+1).setValue(eventTime);

        if (locationIndex !== -1)
          sheet.getRange(i+1,locationIndex+1).setValue(location);

        if (deliveredIndex !== -1 && status.toLowerCase() === "delivered")
          sheet.getRange(i+1,deliveredIndex+1).setValue(eventTime);

      }

    }

    return responseJSON({status:"success"});

  } catch(err) {

    return responseJSON({
      status:"error",
      message:err.toString()
    });

  }

}

function tere()
{
  getBoxSummaryByEEReference("AZ250568");
}


function getBoxSummaryByEEReference(eeReferenceCode) {
  const boxMap = {};

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.openById(SPREADSHEET_ID);
  const packingData = _loadPackingData(ss, eeReferenceCode);

  packingData.forEach(row => {
    const boxId   = row['Box ID'];
    const length  = Number(row['Box Length']);
    const width   = Number(row['Box Width']);
    const height  = Number(row['Box Height']);
    const weight  = Number(row['Box Weight']);

    if (!boxId) return;

    if (!boxMap[boxId]) {
      boxMap[boxId] = {
        boxId,
        length,
        width,
        height,
        weight
      };
    }
  });

  const data = Object.values(boxMap).map(box => ({
    "Box ID": box.boxId,
    "Weight": `${Math.round(box.weight / 1000)}`,
    "Dimensions": `${box.length}x${box.width}x${box.height}`
  }));

  Logger.log(data);

  return {
    status: 'success',
    data
  };
}

function saveEasyEcomShipmentDetails(payload) {

  // 1. Get Auth Token
  const token = getEasyEcomToken();
  if (!token) {
    return {
      status: "error",
      message: "Auth Token Failed."
    };
  }

  // 2. Get API Key
  const scriptProperties = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
  const X_API_KEY = scriptProperties.getProperty('EASY_ECOM_API_KEY');

  // 3. API Endpoint
  const url = "https://api.easyecom.io/oms/b2b/v1/save-shipment-details";

  // 4. API Request Options
  const options = {
    method: "POST",
    headers: {
      "Authorization": "Bearer " + token,
      "x-api-key": X_API_KEY,
      "Content-Type": "application/json"
    },
    payload: JSON.stringify(payload),
    muteHttpExceptions: true
  };

  // 5. Send Request
  const response = UrlFetchApp.fetch(url, options);
  const responseCode = response.getResponseCode();
  const responseText = response.getContentText();

  Logger.log("EasyEcom Shipment Response Code: " + responseCode);
  Logger.log("EasyEcom Shipment Response: " + responseText);

  // 6. Parse Response
  let result;
  try {
    result = JSON.parse(responseText);
  } catch (e) {
    result = { rawResponse: responseText };
  }

  return {
    statusCode: responseCode,
    response: result
  };
}

function updateTrackingStatusAll() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const dbSheet = ss.getSheetByName('PO_Database');

  if (!dbSheet) {
    Logger.log("PO_Database sheet not found");
    return;
  }

  if (dbSheet.getLastRow() < 2) {
    Logger.log('No data to process');
    return;
  }

  const data = dbSheet.getDataRange().getValues();
  const headers = data.shift();

  const mainStatusIdx = headers.indexOf('Status');
  const awbIdx = headers.indexOf('AWB');
  const statusIdx = headers.indexOf('Tracking Status');
  const carrierIdx = headers.indexOf('Carrier');

  if (awbIdx === -1 || statusIdx === -1 || carrierIdx === -1) {
    Logger.log("Required columns missing. Required: AWB, Tracking Status, Carrier");
    return;
  }

  const awbToRows = new Map();
  const nimbusAwbs = new Set();
  const shiprocketAwbs = new Set();

  const finalStatuses = [
    'delivered',
    'rto delivered',
    'cancelled'
  ];

  let alreadyDeliveredFixedCount = 0;

  // ---------------- COLLECT AWBs ----------------
  data.forEach((row, i) => {

    const awb = String(row[awbIdx] || "").trim();
    const trackingStatus = String(row[statusIdx] || "").trim().toLowerCase();
    const carrier = String(row[carrierIdx] || "").trim().toUpperCase();

    const mainStatus = mainStatusIdx !== -1
      ? String(row[mainStatusIdx] || "").trim().toLowerCase()
      : "";

    if (!awb) return;

    // -----------------------------------------------------
    // Fix rows where Tracking Status is already delivered,
    // but main Status is still Dispatched / not Delivered
    // -----------------------------------------------------
    if (
      trackingStatus === 'delivered' &&
      mainStatusIdx !== -1 &&
      mainStatus !== 'delivered'
    ) {
      const sheetRow = i + 2; // +2 because headers removed and sheet starts at row 1
      dbSheet.getRange(sheetRow, mainStatusIdx + 1).setValue("Delivered");
      alreadyDeliveredFixedCount++;

      Logger.log(`Updated main Status to Delivered for AWB ${awb}`);
    }

    // Do not fetch final shipments again
    if (finalStatuses.includes(trackingStatus)) return;

    if (!awbToRows.has(awb)) {
      awbToRows.set(awb, []);
    }

    awbToRows.get(awb).push(i);

    if (carrier.includes("(SR)")) {
      shiprocketAwbs.add(awb);
    } else if (carrier.includes("(NP)")) {
      nimbusAwbs.add(awb);
    } else {
      Logger.log(`Skipped AWB ${awb}: Carrier does not contain (NP) or (SR). Carrier: ${carrier}`);
    }

  });

  if (awbToRows.size === 0) {
    Logger.log(
      `No active shipments to fetch. Already-delivered status fixes done: ${alreadyDeliveredFixedCount}`
    );
    return;
  }

  Logger.log(`Nimbus AWBs: ${nimbusAwbs.size}`);
  Logger.log(`Shiprocket AWBs: ${shiprocketAwbs.size}`);

  const updates = {};

  // =====================================================
  // 🚀 NIMBUS TRACKING - BATCHED MAX 100 AWBs
  // =====================================================
  if (nimbusAwbs.size > 0) {

    const token = getNimbusPostToken();

    if (!token) {
      Logger.log("Nimbus token not found");
      return;
    }

    const nimbusAwbArray = Array.from(nimbusAwbs);
    const BATCH_SIZE = 100;

    for (let i = 0; i < nimbusAwbArray.length; i += BATCH_SIZE) {

      const batch = nimbusAwbArray.slice(i, i + BATCH_SIZE);
      const batchNumber = Math.floor(i / BATCH_SIZE) + 1;

      try {

        const res = UrlFetchApp.fetch(
          "https://api.nimbuspost.com/v1/shipments/track/bulk",
          {
            method: "POST",
            contentType: "application/json",
            headers: {
              Authorization: "Bearer " + token
            },
            payload: JSON.stringify({
              awb: batch
            }),
            muteHttpExceptions: true
          }
        );

        const responseText = res.getContentText();

        let result;

        try {
          result = JSON.parse(responseText);
        } catch (jsonErr) {
          Logger.log(`Nimbus non-JSON response for batch ${batchNumber}: ${responseText}`);
          continue;
        }

        if (!result.status || !Array.isArray(result.data)) {
          Logger.log(`Nimbus Post API Error for batch ${batchNumber}: ${responseText}`);
          continue;
        }

        Logger.log(
          `Nimbus batch ${batchNumber} fetched. Sent: ${batch.length}, Received: ${result.data.length}`
        );

        result.data.forEach(entry => {

          const awb = String(entry.awb_number || "").trim();
          const history = Array.isArray(entry.history) ? entry.history : [];
          const latest = history[0] || {};

          if (!awbToRows.has(awb)) return;

          awbToRows.get(awb).forEach(rowIndex => {

            updates[rowIndex] = {
              status: entry.status || "",
              edd: entry.edd || "",
              message: latest.message || "",
              date: latest.event_time || "",
              location: latest.location || "",
              delivered: entry.delivered_date || ""
            };

          });

        });

        Utilities.sleep(500); // avoid Nimbus rate limits

      } catch (e) {
        Logger.log(`Nimbus error in batch ${batchNumber}: ${e.message}`);
      }

    }
  }

  // =====================================================
  // 🚀 SHIPROCKET TRACKING
  // =====================================================
  if (shiprocketAwbs.size > 0) {

    const token = getShiprocketToken();

    if (!token) {
      Logger.log("Shiprocket token not found");
      return;
    }

    shiprocketAwbs.forEach(awb => {

      try {

        const res = UrlFetchApp.fetch(
          `https://apiv2.shiprocket.in/v1/external/courier/track/awb/${awb}`,
          {
            method: "get",
            headers: {
              Authorization: `Bearer ${token}`
            },
            muteHttpExceptions: true
          }
        );

        const responseText = res.getContentText();

        let json;

        try {
          json = JSON.parse(responseText);
        } catch (jsonErr) {
          Logger.log(`Shiprocket non-JSON response for AWB ${awb}: ${responseText}`);
          return;
        }

        const shipment = json?.tracking_data?.shipment_track?.[0];
        const activities = json?.tracking_data?.shipment_track_activities || [];
        const latest = activities[0] || {};

        if (!shipment) {
          Logger.log(`Shiprocket no shipment data for AWB ${awb}: ${responseText}`);
          return;
        }

        if (!awbToRows.has(awb)) return;

        awbToRows.get(awb).forEach(rowIndex => {

          updates[rowIndex] = {
            status: shipment?.current_status || "",
            edd: shipment?.edd || "",
            message: latest?.activity || "",
            date: latest?.date || "",
            location: latest?.location || "",
            delivered: shipment?.delivered_date || ""
          };

        });

        Utilities.sleep(150); // prevent Shiprocket rate limit

      } catch (e) {
        Logger.log(`Shiprocket error for AWB ${awb}: ${e.message}`);
      }

    });
  }

  // =====================================================
  // 🚀 WRITE BACK TO SHEET
  // =====================================================
  const colMap = {
    status: headers.indexOf('Tracking Status'),
    edd: headers.indexOf('EDD'),
    message: headers.indexOf('Latest Status'),
    date: headers.indexOf('Latest Status Date'),
    location: headers.indexOf('Current Location'),
    delivered: headers.indexOf('Delivered Date'),
    postatus: headers.indexOf('Status')
  };

  let count = 0;
  let deliveredStatusUpdatedCount = 0;

  Object.entries(updates).forEach(([rowIndex, dataObj]) => {

    const row = Number(rowIndex) + 2;

    if (colMap.status !== -1) {
      dbSheet.getRange(row, colMap.status + 1).setValue(dataObj.status || "");
    }

    if (colMap.edd !== -1) {
      dbSheet.getRange(row, colMap.edd + 1).setValue(dataObj.edd || "");
    }

    if (colMap.message !== -1) {
      dbSheet.getRange(row, colMap.message + 1).setValue(dataObj.message || "");
    }

    if (colMap.date !== -1) {
      dbSheet.getRange(row, colMap.date + 1).setValue(dataObj.date || "");
    }

    if (colMap.location !== -1) {
      dbSheet.getRange(row, colMap.location + 1).setValue(dataObj.location || "");
    }

    if (colMap.delivered !== -1 && dataObj.delivered) {
      dbSheet.getRange(row, colMap.delivered + 1).setValue(dataObj.delivered);
    }

    // Update main Status to Delivered if tracking response says delivered
    const latestTrackingStatus = String(dataObj.status || "").trim().toLowerCase();

    if (
      colMap.postatus !== -1 &&
      (
        latestTrackingStatus === "delivered" ||
        latestTrackingStatus === "rto delivered" ||
        dataObj.delivered
      )
    ) {
      dbSheet.getRange(row, colMap.postatus + 1).setValue("Delivered");
      deliveredStatusUpdatedCount++;
    }

    count++;

  });

  Logger.log(`Updated tracking for ${count} rows`);
  Logger.log(`Already-delivered Status fixes: ${alreadyDeliveredFixedCount}`);
  Logger.log(`Main Status marked Delivered from fresh tracking: ${deliveredStatusUpdatedCount}`);
}

function selfShipOrder(data) {
  const { eeReferenceCode, awb, courier, trackingUrl, labelUrl } = data;
  if (!eeReferenceCode || !courier) {
    return { status: 'error', message: 'EE Reference Code and Courier Name are required' };
  }

  try {
    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.openById(SPREADSHEET_ID);
    const dbSheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_PO_DB);
    const sheetData = dbSheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    const headers = sheetData[0];

    const refCol = headers.indexOf('EE_reference_code');
    const awbIdx = headers.indexOf("AWB");
    const carrierIdx = headers.indexOf('Carrier');
    const trackingIdx = headers.indexOf('Tracking Status');
    const trackingUrlIdx = headers.indexOf('Tracking URL');
    const labelIdx = headers.indexOf('Label URL');
    const bookedDateIdx = headers.indexOf('Booked Date');
    const pickupDateIdx = headers.indexOf('Pickup Date');

    if (refCol === -1) return { status: 'error', message: 'EE_reference_code column not found' };

    const now = new Date();
    const today = new Date(now);
    const hourIST = parseInt(Utilities.formatDate(now, "Asia/Kolkata", "HH"));
    
    let pickupDate = new Date(now);
    if (hourIST >= 14) {
      pickupDate.setDate(pickupDate.getDate() + 1);
    }

    let updated = false;
    for (let i = 1; i < sheetData.length; i++) {
      if (String(sheetData[i][refCol]).trim() === String(eeReferenceCode).trim()) {
        if (awbIdx !== -1) dbSheet.getRange(i + 1, awbIdx + 1).setValue(awb || "-");
        if (carrierIdx !== -1) dbSheet.getRange(i + 1, carrierIdx + 1).setValue(courier + " (Self)");
        if (trackingIdx !== -1) dbSheet.getRange(i + 1, trackingIdx + 1).setValue("AWB Assigned");
        if (bookedDateIdx !== -1) dbSheet.getRange(i + 1, bookedDateIdx + 1).setValue(today);
        if (pickupDateIdx !== -1) dbSheet.getRange(i + 1, pickupDateIdx + 1).setValue(pickupDate);
        if (trackingUrlIdx !== -1) dbSheet.getRange(i + 1, trackingUrlIdx + 1).setValue(trackingUrl || "");
        if (labelIdx !== -1) dbSheet.getRange(i + 1, labelIdx + 1).setValue(labelUrl || "");
        updated = true;
      }
    }

    if (updated) {
      return {
        status: "success",
        message: `Order ${eeReferenceCode} marked as Self Shipped via ${courier}`,
        awb,
        courier,
        label: labelUrl,
        tracking: trackingUrl
      };
    }
    return { status: 'error', message: 'Order not found in database: ' + eeReferenceCode };
  } catch (e) {
    return { status: 'error', message: 'Error in selfShipOrder: ' + e.toString() };
  }
}
