function testGenerateEWayBillPartA() {
  const invoiceId = "1975394000268251193";

  const token = getZohoAccessToken(); 
  
  // Step 1: Create Zoho Record
  const ewayBillId = createEWayBillRecord(invoiceId,token);
  
  if (ewayBillId) {
    Logger.log("Step 1 Success: Record Created. Zoho ID: " + ewayBillId);
    
    // Step 2: Push to Portal
    const pushResult = pushToGovernmentPortal(ewayBillId,token);
    
    if (pushResult.code === 0) {
      Logger.log("Step 2 Success: Part A Slip Number: " + pushResult.ewaybill.part_a_slip_number);
    } else {
      // Common errors: "Invalid GSTIN", "PIN code distance mismatch"
      Logger.log("Step 2 Failed: " + pushResult.message);
    }
  }
}
/**
 * Step 1: Saves transportation details (Part A) to Zoho
 */
function createEWayBillRecord(invoiceId,token) {
  const url = `https://www.zohoapis.in/books/v3/ewaybills?organization_id=60032126274`;
  
  const payload = {

    "invoice_id": invoiceId,      // Try this first
    "transaction_type": "invoice",
    "document_type": "invoice",
    "transportation_details": {
      "transporter_id": "1975394000002734361", // Replace with valid Transporter GSTIN
      "distance": 150,
      "transport_mode": "road"
    }
  };
  Logger.log(payload);

  const options = {
    "method": "POST",
    "headers": {
      "Authorization": "Zoho-oauthtoken " + token,
      "Content-Type": "application/json"
    },
    "payload": JSON.stringify(payload),
    "muteHttpExceptions": true
  };

  const response = UrlFetchApp.fetch(url, options);
  const json = JSON.parse(response.getContentText());

  if (json.code === 0) {
    return json.ewaybill.ewaybill_id;
  } else {
    Logger.log("Error creating record: " + json.message);
    return null;
  }
}

/**
 * Step 2: Pushes Part A to the government portal via Zoho GSP
 */
function pushToGovernmentPortal(ewayBillId,token) {
  const url = `https://www.zohoapis.in/books/v3/ewaybills/${ewayBillId}/generate?organization_id=60032126274`;
  
  const options = {
    "method": "POST",
    "headers": {
      "Authorization": "Zoho-oauthtoken " + token
    },
    "muteHttpExceptions": true
  };

  const response = UrlFetchApp.fetch(url, options);
  return JSON.parse(response.getContentText());
}



amazon.gs

// =================================================================================
// AMAZON FBA - TWO-STAGE INBOUND SHIPMENT WORKFLOW
// =================================================================================
//

function getAmazonAccessToken() {
  var scriptProperties = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
  // ... (rest of the function is identical, no changes needed)
  var clientId = scriptProperties.getProperty('AMAZON_CLIENT_ID');
  var clientSecret = scriptProperties.getProperty('AMAZON_CLIENT_SECRET');
  var refreshToken = scriptProperties.getProperty('AMAZON_REFRESH_TOKEN');
  var url = 'https://api.amazon.com/auth/o2/token';
  var options = {
    'method': 'post',
    'contentType': 'application/x-www-form-urlencoded',
    'muteHttpExceptions': true,
    'payload': { 'grant_type': 'refresh_token', 'refresh_token': refreshToken, 'client_id': clientId, 'client_secret': clientSecret }
  };
  try {
    var response = UrlFetchApp.fetch(url, options);
    var responseData = JSON.parse(response.getContentText());
    if (responseData.access_token) { return responseData.access_token; } 
    else { Logger.log('Error getting access token: ' + response.getContentText()); return null; }
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Exception fetching access token: ' + e.message); return null; }
}



// ============================================================================
// SP API functions to create plan and shipments on Amazon for FBA Inbound
// ============================================================================
const AMAZON = {
  endpoint: 'https://sellingpartnerapi-eu.amazon.com',
  marketplaceId: 'A21TJRUUN4KGV',
  apiPath: '/inbound/fba/2024-03-20'
};

//Get Inbound ID
function createAmazonFbaInboundPlan(data,poRef) {
  try {
    const token = getAmazonAccessToken();
    if (!token) throw new Error('Amazon access token missing');

    const endpoint = AMAZON.endpoint;

    // ==================================================
    // STEP 0 — Reuse inbound plan if already known
    // ==================================================

    if (data.inboundPlanId) {
      Logger.log(
        `Inbound Plan ID provided in input for PO ${poRef}: ${data.inboundPlanId}. Reusing.`
      );

      return {
        status: 'success',
        message: 'Inbound plan reused from input data.',
        data: {
          inboundPlanId: data.inboundPlanId,
          reused: true,
          source: 'input'
        }
      };
    }


    // ==================================================
    // STEP 1 — Create inbound plan (only if needed)
    // ==================================================
    const { inboundPlanId, operationId } =
      createInboundPlan_(token, endpoint, poRef, data.items,data.locationKey);

    // STEP 1.5 — Poll async creation
    pollOperation_(token, endpoint, operationId);

    Logger.log("Updating Database");

    // STEP 2 — Persist in DB
    updatePoDatabase_(poRef, inboundPlanId,"","");

    return {
      status: 'success',
      message: 'Amazon FBA inbound plan created successfully.',
      data: {
        inboundPlanId,
        reused: false,
        source: 'created'
      }
    };

  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log(`Amazon FBA inbound plan failed: ${e.message}`);

    return {
      status: 'error',
      message: e.message
    };
  }
}

//Get Placement Option ID and Shipment ID
function generateAndListAmazonPlacementDirect(poRef) {
  try {
    const token = getAmazonAccessToken();
    if (!token) throw new Error('Amazon access token missing');

    const endpoint = AMAZON.endpoint;

    // ==================================================
    // STEP 0 — Fetch inboundPlanId from PO DB
    // ==================================================
    const { inboundPlanId } = getFbaIdsFromDB_(poRef);
    if (!inboundPlanId) {
      throw new Error(`Inbound Plan ID not found for PO ${poRef}`);
    }

    // ==================================================
    // STEP 1 — Fetch items + warehouseId from PO DB
    // ==================================================
    const { items, warehouseId } = getPoItemsFromDB_(poRef);

    // ==================================================
    // STEP 2 — Generate placement options
    // ==================================================
    const url =
      `${endpoint}${AMAZON.apiPath}/inboundPlans/${inboundPlanId}/placementOptions`;

    const payload = {
      customPlacement: [
        {
          warehouseId: warehouseId,
          items: items.map(i => ({
            msku: i.articleCode,
            quantity: i.qty,
            labelOwner: 'SELLER',
            prepOwner: 'NONE'
          }))
        }
      ]
    };

    Logger.log(JSON.stringify(payload, null, 2));

    

    const res = fetchSigned_(
      token,
      { method: 'POST', url, payload },
      [202]
    );

    // ==================================================
    // STEP 3 — Poll async operation
    // ==================================================
    pollOperation_(token, endpoint, res.operationId);
    

    const { placementOptionId, shipmentId } = listPlacementOptions_(token, endpoint, inboundPlanId);
    updatePoDatabase_(poRef, "", shipmentId, placementOptionId);

    return {
      status: 'success',
      message: 'Amazon placement options generated successfully.',
      data: {
        inboundPlanId,
        placementOperationId: res.operationId,
        warehouseId
      }
    };

  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log(`generateAmazonPlacementDirect failed for PO ${poRef}: ${e.message}`);

    return {
      status: 'error',
      message: e.message
    };
  }
}

function setPackingInformationAndConfirmPlacementDirect(poRef) {
  try {
    // ==================================================
    // STEP 0 — Auth + endpoint
    // ==================================================
    const token = getAmazonAccessToken();
    if (!token) throw new Error('Amazon access token missing');

    const endpoint = AMAZON.endpoint;

    

    // ==================================================
    // STEP 1 — Fetch FBA IDs from PO DB
    // ==================================================
    const {
      inboundPlanId,
      placementId,
      shipmentId
    } = getFbaIdsFromDB_(poRef);

    if (!inboundPlanId) {
      throw new Error(`Inbound Plan ID missing for PO ${poRef}`);
    }
    if (!placementId) {
      throw new Error(`Placement ID missing for PO ${poRef}`);
    }
    if (!shipmentId) {
      throw new Error(`Shipment ID missing for PO ${poRef}`);
    }

    // ==================================================
    // STEP 2 — Load + convert packing data
    // ==================================================
    const packingRows =
      _loadPackingData(SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet(), poRef);

    if (!packingRows.length) {
      throw new Error(`No packing data found for PO ${poRef}`);
    }

    const boxes = buildBoxesFromPackingData_(packingRows);
    Logger.log('Packing boxes:');
    Logger.log(boxes);

    // ==================================================
    // STEP 3 — Set packing information (MANUAL_PROCESS)
    // ==================================================
    const packOpId = setPackingInformation_(
      token,
      endpoint,
      inboundPlanId,
      shipmentId,   // using shipmentId (post-placement flow)
      boxes
    );

    pollOperation_(token, endpoint, packOpId);

    const genTransopID = generateTransportationOptions_(token, endpoint, inboundPlanId,placementId, shipmentId);
     pollOperation_(token, endpoint, genTransopID);

 

    // ==================================================
    // STEP 4 — Confirm placement option
    // ==================================================
    const confirmOpId = confirmPlacement_(
      token,
      endpoint,
      inboundPlanId,
      placementId
    );

    pollOperation_(token, endpoint, confirmOpId);
    

    // ==================================================
    // STEP 5 — Fetch shipment confirmation ID ✅
    // ==================================================
    const shipmentConfirmationId =
      getShipmentConfirmationId_(
        token,
        endpoint,
        inboundPlanId,
        shipmentId
      );

    // (Optional) store in DB
    updatePoDatabase_(poRef, "", "", "", shipmentConfirmationId);

    const options = listTransportationOptions_(token,endpoint,inboundPlanId,shipmentId);
    
    const atsTransportationOptionId = getATSTransportationOptionId_(options);
    
    const confirmTransOpId = confirmTransportationOption_(token,endpoint,inboundPlanId,shipmentId,atsTransportationOptionId);
    
    pollOperation_(token, endpoint, confirmTransOpId);

    getShipmentConfirmationId_(
        token,
        endpoint,
        inboundPlanId,
        shipmentId
      );

    return {
      status: 'success',
      message: `Packing + placement confirmed for PO ${poRef}`,
      data: {
        inboundPlanId,
        placementId,
        shipmentId
      }
    };


  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log(
      `setPackingInformationAndConfirmPlacementDirect failed for PO ${poRef}: ${e.message}`
    );

    return {
      status: 'error',
      message: e.message
    };
  }
}

function getShipmentConfirmationId_(token,endpoint,inboundPlanId,shipmentId) 
{
  const url =`${endpoint}${AMAZON.apiPath}` +`/inboundPlans/${inboundPlanId}/shipments/${shipmentId}`;

  const res = fetchSigned_(token,{ method: 'GET', url },[200]);
  Logger.log(res);

  const confirmationId =
    res.shipmentConfirmationId ||
    res.shipmentConfirmation?.shipmentConfirmationId ||
    null;

  if (!confirmationId) {
    throw new Error(
      `ShipmentConfirmationId not found for shipment ${shipmentId}`
    );
  }

  return confirmationId;
}

function listTransportationOptions_(token,  endpoint,  inboundPlanId,  shipmentId)
  {
   const url =
    `${endpoint}/inbound/fba/2024-03-20/inboundPlans/${inboundPlanId}` +
    `/transportationOptions?shipmentId=${shipmentId}`;

  const res = fetchSigned_(
    token,
    { method: 'GET', url },
    [200]
  );

  return res.transportationOptions || [];
}

function confirmPlacement_(token, endpoint, inboundPlanId, placementOptionId) {
  const url = `${endpoint}${AMAZON.apiPath}/inboundPlans/${inboundPlanId}/placementOptions/${placementOptionId}/confirmation`;
  return fetchSigned_(token, { method: 'POST', url, payload: {} }, [202]).operationId;
}


function confirmTransportationOption_(token,endpoint,inboundPlanId,shipmentId,transportationOptionId)
{
  const url =
    `${endpoint}${AMAZON.apiPath}` +
    `/inboundPlans/${inboundPlanId}` +
    `/transportationOptions/confirmation`;

  const payload = {
    transportationSelections: [
      {
        shipmentId,
        transportationOptionId
      }
    ]
  };

  const res = fetchSigned_(
    token,
    { method: 'POST', url, payload },
    [202]
  );

  return res.operationId;
}


function setPackingInformation_(token, endpoint, inboundPlanId, shipmentId, boxes) {
  const url =
    `${endpoint}${AMAZON.apiPath}/inboundPlans/${inboundPlanId}/packingInformation`;

  const payload = {
    packageGroupings: [
      {
        shipmentId: shipmentId, // ✅ REQUIRED for India
        boxes: boxes.map(b => ({
          quantity: b.quantity || 1,
          contentInformationSource: 'MANUAL_PROCESS',
          dimensions: {
            unitOfMeasurement: 'CM',
            length: Number(b.lengthCm),
            width: Number(b.widthCm),
            height: Number(b.heightCm)
          },
          weight: {
            unit: 'KG',
            value: Number(b.weightKg)
          }
        }))
      }
    ]
  };

  const response = fetchSigned_(token,{ method: 'POST', url, payload},[202]);

  return response.operationId;
}

function createInboundPlan_(token, endpoint, poNumber, items, locationKey = null) {
  const url = `${endpoint}${AMAZON.apiPath}/inboundPlans`;

  const scriptProperties = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();

  // If locationKey is present, use alternate ship-from address
  const shipFromAddressKey = locationKey
    ? 'FBA_SHIP_FROM_ADDRESS_1'
    : 'FBA_SHIP_FROM_ADDRESS';

  const sourceAddressRaw = scriptProperties.getProperty(shipFromAddressKey);

  if (!sourceAddressRaw) {
    throw new Error(`Missing Script Property: ${shipFromAddressKey}`);
  }

  const sourceAddress = JSON.parse(sourceAddressRaw);

  const payload = {
    destinationMarketplaces: [AMAZON.marketplaceId],
    name: String(poNumber),
    sourceAddress,
    items: items.map(i => ({
      msku: i.articleCode,
      quantity: i.qty,
      labelOwner: 'SELLER',
      prepOwner: 'NONE'
    }))
  };

  const response = fetchSigned_(
    token,
    { method: 'POST', url, payload },
    [201, 202]
  );

  /*
    201 → synchronous success (rare)
    202 → async success (common)
  */

  if (!response.inboundPlanId) {
    throw new Error(
      `Inbound plan creation failed: ${JSON.stringify(response)}`
    );
  }

  return {
    inboundPlanId: response.inboundPlanId,
    operationId: response.operationId || null
  };
}

// ============================================================================
// HELPER NEW
// ============================================================================

function getPoItemsFromDB_(poRef) {
  const sh = SpreadsheetApp
    .getActive()
    .getSheetByName(SHEET_PO_DB);

  const data = sh.getDataRange().getValues();
  const headers = data.shift();

  const poIdx    = headers.indexOf('EE Order Ref ID');
  const skuIdx   = headers.indexOf('Item Code');
  const qtyIdx   = headers.indexOf('Qty');
  const storeIdx = headers.indexOf('Store Code');

  if ([poIdx, skuIdx, qtyIdx, storeIdx].includes(-1)) {
    throw new Error('Required columns missing in PO_Database');
  }

  const rows = data.filter(
    r => String(r[poIdx]).trim() === String(poRef).trim()
  );

  if (!rows.length) {
    throw new Error(`No rows found for PO ${poRef}`);
  }

  const warehouseId = String(rows[0][storeIdx]).trim();

  const items = rows
    .map(r => ({
      articleCode: String(r[skuIdx]).trim(),
      qty: Number(r[qtyIdx])
    }))
    .filter(i => i.articleCode && i.qty > 0);

  if (!items.length) {
    throw new Error(`No valid items found for PO ${poRef}`);
  }

  return { items, warehouseId };
}

function getFbaIdsFromDB_(poRef) {
  const sh = SpreadsheetApp
    .getActive()
    .getSheetByName(SHEET_PO_DB);

  if (!sh) throw new Error(`Sheet ${SHEET_PO_DB} not found`);

  const data = sh.getDataRange().getValues();
  const headers = data.shift();

  const poIdx        = headers.indexOf('EE Order Ref ID');
  const inboundIdx   = headers.indexOf('Inbound Plan ID');
  const placementIdx = headers.indexOf('Placement ID');
  const shipmentIdx  = headers.indexOf('Shipment ID');

  if ([poIdx, inboundIdx, placementIdx, shipmentIdx].includes(-1)) {
    throw new Error(
      'Required columns missing: EE Order Ref ID / Inbound Plan ID / Placement ID / Shipment ID'
    );
  }

  for (const row of data) {
    if (String(row[poIdx]).trim() === String(poRef).trim()) {
      return {
        inboundPlanId:  String(row[inboundIdx]   || '').trim() || null,
        placementId:    String(row[placementIdx] || '').trim() || null,
        shipmentId:     String(row[shipmentIdx]  || '').trim() || null
      };
    }
  }

  return {
    inboundPlanId: null,
    placementId: null,
    shipmentId: null
  };
}

function buildBoxesFromPackingData_(rows) {
  const map = {};
  rows.forEach(r => {
    const id = r['Box ID'];
    if (!map[id]) {
      map[id] = {
        quantity: 0,
        lengthCm: r['Box Length'],
        widthCm: r['Box Width'],
        heightCm: r['Box Height'],
        weightKg: r['Box Weight']/1000
      };
    }
    map[id].quantity++;
  });
  return Object.values(map);
}

function updatePoDatabase_(po, inboundPlanId, shipmentId, placementId, shipmentConfirmationId) {
  const sh = SpreadsheetApp
    .getActive()
    .getSheetByName(SHEET_PO_DB);

  if (!sh) throw new Error(`Sheet ${SHEET_PO_DB} not found`);

  const data = sh.getDataRange().getValues();
  const headers = data[0];

  const poIdx     = headers.indexOf('PO Number');
  const planIdx   = headers.indexOf('Inbound Plan ID');
  const shipIdx   = headers.indexOf('Shipment ID');
  const placeIdx  = headers.indexOf('Placement ID');
  const fbashipIdx  = headers.indexOf('FBA Shipment IDs');

  if (poIdx === -1) {
    throw new Error('Column "EE Order Ref ID" missing in PO DB');
  }

  let updatedCount = 0;

  for (let i = 1; i < data.length; i++) {
    if (String(data[i][poIdx]).trim() !== String(po).trim()) continue;

    const rowNum = i + 1;

    // ✏️ Update ONLY if value is provided
    if (inboundPlanId && planIdx !== -1) {
      sh.getRange(rowNum, planIdx + 1).setValue(inboundPlanId);
    }

    if (shipmentId && shipIdx !== -1) {
      sh.getRange(rowNum, shipIdx + 1).setValue(shipmentId);
    }

    if (placementId && placeIdx !== -1) {
      sh.getRange(rowNum, placeIdx + 1).setValue(placementId);
    }

    if (shipmentConfirmationId && fbashipIdx !== -1) {
      sh.getRange(rowNum, fbashipIdx + 1).setValue(shipmentConfirmationId);
    }

    updatedCount++;
  }

  if (updatedCount === 0) {
    Logger.log(`No rows found for PO ${po} in PO database`);
    return;
  }

  Logger.log(
    `Updated ${updatedCount} rows for PO ${po}` +
    `${inboundPlanId ? ` | inboundPlanId=${inboundPlanId}` : ''}` +
    `${shipmentId ? ` | shipmentId=${shipmentId}` : ''}` +
    `${placementId ? ` | placementId=${placementId}` : ''}`
  );
}

function getATSTransportationOptionId_(transportationOptions) 
{
  if (!transportationOptions || !transportationOptions.length) {
    throw new Error('No transportation options available');
  }

  const atsOption = transportationOptions.find(opt =>
    opt.shippingSolution === 'AMAZON_PARTNERED_CARRIER' ||
    opt.carrier?.alphaCode === 'AMAZNEMP'
  );

  if (!atsOption) {
    throw new Error('ATS transportation option not found');
  }

  return atsOption.transportationOptionId;
}


function listPlacementOptions_(token, endpoint, inboundPlanId) {
  const url =
    `${endpoint}${AMAZON.apiPath}/inboundPlans/${inboundPlanId}/placementOptions`;

  const response = fetchSigned_(
    token,
    { method: 'GET', url },
    [200]
  );

  const placementOptions = response.placementOptions || [];

  if (!placementOptions.length) {
    throw new Error('No placement options returned for inbound plan');
  }

  // India usually returns exactly one placement option
  const option = placementOptions[0];

  const placementOptionId = option.placementOptionId;
  const shipmentId = (option.shipmentIds && option.shipmentIds[0]) || null;

  if (!placementOptionId) {
    throw new Error('placementOptionId missing in placement option');
  }

  if (!shipmentId) {
    throw new Error('shipmentId missing in placement option');
  }

  return {
    placementOptionId,
    shipmentId
  };
}


function requestShipmentLabels_(
  token,
  endpoint,
  inboundPlanId,
  shipmentId,
  boxCount
) {
  const url =
    `${endpoint}${AMAZON.apiPath}/inboundPlans/${inboundPlanId}` +
    `/shipments/${shipmentId}/labels`;

  const payload = {
    labelType: 'PACKAGE_LABEL',
    pageType: 'A4',
    numberOfPackages: boxCount
  };

  const res = fetchSigned_(
    token,
    { method: 'POST', url, payload },
    [202]
  );

  return res.operationId;
}


function downloadLabelDocument_(token, endpoint, documentId) {
  const url =
    `${endpoint}${AMAZON.apiPath}/documents/${documentId}`;

  const res = fetchSigned_(token, { method: 'GET', url }, [200]);

  // res.url → pre-signed S3 URL (PDF)
  return res.url;
}

function downloadFbaShipmentLabels(poRef) {
  const token = getAmazonAccessToken();
  const endpoint = AMAZON.endpoint;

  const { inboundPlanId, shipmentId } = getFbaIdsFromDB_(poRef);

  const packingRows =
    _loadPackingData(SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet(), poRef);

  const boxCount = packingRows.length;

  const opId = requestShipmentLabels_(
    token,
    endpoint,
    inboundPlanId,
    shipmentId,
    boxCount
  );

  const result = pollOperation_(token, endpoint, opId);

  const documentId = result.documents?.[0]?.documentId;
  if (!documentId) {
    throw new Error('Label document not generated');
  }

  return downloadLabelDocument_(token, endpoint, documentId);
}

function getInboundPlanItems_(token, endpoint, inboundPlanId) {
  const url =
    `${endpoint}${AMAZON.apiPath}/inboundPlans/${inboundPlanId}`;

  const res = fetchSigned_(
    token,
    { method: 'GET', url },
    [200]
  );

  if (!res.items || !res.items.length) {
    throw new Error(`No items found in inbound plan ${inboundPlanId}`);
  }

  return res.items.map(i => ({
    articleCode: i.msku,
    qty: i.quantity
  }));
}


function generatePlacementOptions_(token, endpoint, inboundPlanId, warehouseId, items) {
  const url = `${endpoint}${AMAZON.apiPath}/inboundPlans/${inboundPlanId}/placementOptions`;

  const payload = {
    customPlacement: [{
      warehouseId,
      items: items.map(i => ({
        msku: i.articleCode,
        quantity: i.qty,
        labelOwner: 'SELLER',
        prepOwner: 'NONE'
      }))
    }]
  };

  return fetchSigned_(token, { method: 'POST', url, payload }, [202]).operationId;
}

function generateTransportationOptions_(token, endpoint, inboundPlanId, placementOptionId, shipmentId) 
{
  const url =`${endpoint}/inbound/fba/2024-03-20/inboundPlans/${inboundPlanId}/transportationOptions`;

  const payload = {
    placementOptionId: placementOptionId,
    shipmentTransportationConfigurations: [
      {
        shipmentId: shipmentId,
        shipmentTransportationType: 'SP',
        contactInformation: {
          name: 'Mohan Dewangan',
          phoneNumber: '8103733766',
          email: 'avinav@cubelelo.com'
        },
        readyToShipWindow: {
          start: getReadyToShipDate_()
        }
      }
    ]
  };

  const res = fetchSigned_(token,{ method: 'POST', url, payload },[202]);

  return res.operationId;
}

function getReadyToShipDate_() {
  const d = new Date();
  d.setDate(d.getDate() + 1); // tomorrow
  d.setSeconds(0);
  d.setMilliseconds(0);
  return d.toISOString();
}



// ============================================================================
// OPERATION POLLING
// ============================================================================
function pollOperation_(token, endpoint, operationId, max = 25, waitMs = 12000) {
  const url = `${endpoint}${AMAZON.apiPath}/operations/${operationId}`;
  for (let i = 0; i < max; i++) {
    const res = fetchSigned_(token, { method: 'GET', url }, [200]);
    const status = String(res.operationStatus || '').toUpperCase();
    if (['SUCCESS', 'COMPLETED'].includes(status)) return;
    if (['FAILED', 'ERROR'].includes(status)) throw new Error(JSON.stringify(res));
    Utilities.sleep(waitMs);
  }
  throw new Error(`Operation ${operationId} timed out`);
}

// ============================================================================
// SIGNED FETCH WRAPPER
// ============================================================================

function fetchSigned_(token, req, okStatuses) {
  const options = {
    method: req.method,
    headers: {
      'x-amz-access-token': token,
      'Content-Type': 'application/json'
    },
    muteHttpExceptions: true
  };

  if (req.payload) {
    options.payload = JSON.stringify(req.payload);
  }
  Logger.log(req.url);
  Logger.log(options.payload);


  const res = UrlFetchApp.fetch(req.url, options);
  Logger.log(res);
  const status = res.getResponseCode();
  const body = res.getContentText();

  if (!okStatuses.includes(status)) {
    throw new Error(`SP-API failed (${status}): ${body}`);
  }

  return body ? JSON.parse(body) : {};
}



appointment.gs


/**
 * Processes ONLY Blinkit Appointment Pass emails.
 * Ignores all other channels and email types.
 */
/**
 * Processes ONLY Blinkit Appointment Pass emails.
 * Runs safely every 15 minutes using an independent timer property.
 */



function processBlinkitAppointmentPasses() {

  try {

    const scriptProperties = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
    const LAST_RUN_KEY = 'BLINKIT_APPOINTMENT_LAST_RUN';

    let startTime = parseInt(scriptProperties.getProperty(LAST_RUN_KEY) || '0', 10);

    // First-run fallback → look back 120 hours
    if (startTime === 0) {
      const fallbackDate = new Date();
      fallbackDate.setHours(fallbackDate.getHours() - 24);
      startTime = Math.floor(fallbackDate.getTime() / 1000);
    }

    const currentRunTime = Math.floor(Date.now() / 1000);

    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.openById(SPREADSHEET_ID);
    const configSheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_CHANNEL_CONFIG);
    const logSheet = getOrCreateLogSheet(ss, SHEET_PO_REPO);
    const folder = DriveApp.getFolderById(DRIVE_FOLDER_ID);

    if (!configSheet) {
      return { status: "error", message: "Channel Config sheet not found." };
    }

    const configData = configSheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    const newLogs = [];
    let processedCount = 0;

    configData.forEach(row => {

      const [channelName, status, rawEmails, subjectKeyword] = row;

      if (!channelName || channelName.toLowerCase() !== 'blinkit') return;
      if (String(status).toLowerCase() !== 'active') return;
      if (!rawEmails) return;

      const emailList = rawEmails.split(',')
        .map(e => e.trim().toLowerCase())
        .filter(Boolean);

      if (!emailList.length) return;

      const fromClause = `from:(${emailList.join(' OR ')})`;
      let query = `${fromClause} -from:me after:${startTime}`;
      if (subjectKeyword) query += ` subject:("${subjectKeyword}")`;

      const threads = GmailApp.search(query);
      if (!threads.length) return;

      const threadMessages = GmailApp.getMessagesForThreads(threads);

      threadMessages.forEach(messages => {
        messages.forEach(message => {

          const messageTime = Math.floor(message.getDate().getTime() / 1000);
          if (messageTime <= startTime) return;

          const sender = message.getFrom().toLowerCase();
          if (!emailList.some(e => sender.includes(e))) return;

          const subject = message.getSubject();
          if (!subject.toUpperCase().includes('APPOINTMENT PASS')) return;

          const appointmentDetails = _parseBlinkitAppointmentPass(message, folder);

          newLogs.push([
            message.getDate(),
            channelName,
            sender,
            subject,
            `QR Pass - ${appointmentDetails.appointmentId}`,
            appointmentDetails.qrCodeUrl,
            "Appointment Pass",
            appointmentDetails.poNumbers,
            "",
            appointmentDetails.appointmentId,
            appointmentDetails.appointmentDate,
            appointmentDetails.reportingTime,
            appointmentDetails.emailHtml
          ]);

          processedCount++;
        });
      });

    });

    // Write logs
    if (newLogs.length) {
      logSheet
        .getRange(logSheet.getLastRow() + 1, 1, newLogs.length, newLogs[0].length)
        .setValues(newLogs);

      SpreadsheetApp.flush();
      extractAppointmentPassDetails();
      scriptProperties.setProperty(LAST_RUN_KEY, String(currentRunTime));
    }

    return {
      status: "success",
      message: processedCount > 0
        ? `${processedCount} Blinkit appointment pass(es) processed successfully.`
        : "No new Blinkit appointment passes found.",
      processedCount: processedCount,
      scannedTill: new Date(currentRunTime * 1000)
    };

  } catch (e) {

    return {
      status: "error",
      message: "Error processing Blinkit appointment passes.",
      error: e.message
    };
  }
}

function updateZeptoASN(data) {
  const { eeReferenceCode, asnNumber } = data;
  if (!eeReferenceCode || !asnNumber) {
    return { status: 'error', message: 'Missing required fields' };
  }

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.openById(SPREADSHEET_ID);
  const sheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_PO_DB);
  const rows = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
  const headers = rows[0];

  const eeRefIdx = headers.indexOf("EE_reference_code");
  let asnIdx = headers.indexOf("Appointment ID");

  let updated = false;
  for (let i = 1; i < rows.length; i++) {
    if (String(rows[i][eeRefIdx]).trim() === String(eeReferenceCode).trim()) {
      if (asnIdx !== -1) {
        sheet.getRange(i + 1, asnIdx + 1).setValue(asnNumber);
      }
      updated = true;
    }
  }

  if (updated) {
    return { status: 'success', message: 'ASN updated and status moved to Ready to Ship' };
  } else {
    return { status: 'error', message: 'Order not found' };
  }
}

function updateInstamartAppointmentDetails(data) {
  const { eeReferenceCode, appointmentId, appointmentDate, appointmentTime } = data;
  if (!eeReferenceCode || (!appointmentId && !appointmentDate && !appointmentTime)) {
    return { status: 'error', message: 'Missing required fields' };
  }

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.openById(SPREADSHEET_ID);
  const sheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_PO_DB);
  const rows = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
  const headers = rows[0];

  const eeRefIdx = headers.indexOf("EE_reference_code");
  const apptIdIdx = headers.indexOf("Appointment ID");
  const apptDateIdx = headers.indexOf("Appointment Date");
  const apptTimeIdx = headers.indexOf("Appointment Time");

  if (eeRefIdx === -1 || apptIdIdx === -1 || apptDateIdx === -1 || apptTimeIdx === -1) {
    return { status: 'error', message: 'Required columns not found in PO_Database' };
  }

  let updated = false;
  for (let i = 1; i < rows.length; i++) {
    if (String(rows[i][eeRefIdx]).trim() === String(eeReferenceCode).trim()) {
      if (appointmentId) sheet.getRange(i + 1, apptIdIdx + 1).setValue(appointmentId);
      if (appointmentDate) sheet.getRange(i + 1, apptDateIdx + 1).setValue(appointmentDate);
      if (appointmentTime) sheet.getRange(i + 1, apptTimeIdx + 1).setValue(appointmentTime);
      updated = true;
    }
  }

  if (updated) {
    return { status: 'success', message: 'Appointment details updated successfully' };
  } else {
    return { status: 'error', message: 'Order not found' };
  }
}


function extractAppointmentPassDetails() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.openById(SPREADSHEET_ID);
  const repoSheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_PO_REPO);
  const dbSheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_PO_DB);

  if (!repoSheet || !dbSheet) return;

  const lastRow = repoSheet.getLastRow();
  if (lastRow < 2) return;

  const repoData = repoSheet.getRange(1, 1, lastRow, repoSheet.getLastColumn()).getValues();
  const headers = repoData[0];
  const dataRows = repoData.slice(1);

  const categoryIndex = headers.indexOf("Category");
  const statusIndex = headers.indexOf("Status");
  const poNumIndex = headers.indexOf("PO Number");
  const fileUrlIndex = headers.indexOf("Drive Link");
  const appointmentIdIndex = headers.indexOf("Appointment ID");
  const appointmentDateIndex = headers.indexOf("Appointment Date");
  const appointmentTimeIndex = headers.indexOf("Appointment Time");

  if (
    categoryIndex === -1 ||
    statusIndex === -1 ||
    poNumIndex === -1 ||
    appointmentIdIndex === -1 ||
    appointmentDateIndex === -1 ||
    appointmentTimeIndex === -1
  ) {
    Logger.log("Required columns not found.");
    return;
  }

  const dbHeaders = dbSheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, dbSheet.getLastColumn()).getValues()[0];
  const dbAppointmentColumnIndex = dbHeaders.indexOf("Appointment ID");

  if (dbAppointmentColumnIndex === -1) {
    Logger.log("Appointment columns not found in PO DB sheet.");
    return;
  }

  const rowsToUpdate = {};

  // 🔥 ONLY APPOINTMENT PASS LOGIC
  dataRows.forEach((row, index) => {

    const category = String(row[categoryIndex] || "").trim().toLowerCase();
    const currentStatus = String(row[statusIndex] || "").trim();
    const rowIndexInSheet = index + 2;

    if (category === "appointment pass" && currentStatus === "") {

      const poNumber = String(row[poNumIndex] || "").trim();
      if (!poNumber) return;

      const appointmentId = row[appointmentIdIndex] || "Not Found";
      const appointmentDate = row[appointmentDateIndex] || "Not Found";
      const appointmentTime = row[appointmentTimeIndex] || "Not Found";
      const fileUrl = row[fileUrlIndex] || "";

      const dbRowIndexes = findRowIndexesByPoNumber(dbSheet, poNumber);

      if (dbRowIndexes.length > 0) {

        const appointmentValues = [
          appointmentId,
          appointmentDate,
          appointmentTime,
          fileUrl
        ];

        dbRowIndexes.forEach(dbRowIndex => {
          dbSheet
            .getRange(dbRowIndex, dbAppointmentColumnIndex + 1, 1, 4)
            .setValues([appointmentValues]);
        });

        rowsToUpdate[rowIndexInSheet] = "Extracted";

      } else {

        rowsToUpdate[rowIndexInSheet] = "Skipped (PO Not Found in DB)";

      }

    }

  });

  // ✅ Update status column in Repo sheet
  for (const rowIndex in rowsToUpdate) {
    repoSheet
      .getRange(parseInt(rowIndex, 10), statusIndex + 1)
      .setValue(rowsToUpdate[rowIndex]);
  }

  SpreadsheetApp.flush();

  Logger.log("Appointment Pass processing completed.");
}


/**
 * **NEW HELPER:** Parses the email body of a Blinkit Appointment Pass to extract key details.
 *
 * @param {string} emailBody - The plain text content of the email.
 * @return {object} An object containing the extracted appointment details.
 */
/**
 * **NEW & UPGRADED HELPER:** Parses a Blinkit Appointment Pass. It now:
 * 1. Accepts the full GmailMessage object.
 * 2. Extracts all text details from the body.
 * 3. Finds the inline QR code image, saves it to Drive, and returns its URL.
 *
 * @param {GmailMessage} message - The full Gmail message object.
 * @param {Folder} folder - The Google Drive folder to save the QR code image to.
 * @return {object} An object containing all extracted appointment details, including the qrCodeUrl.
 */

function _parseBlinkitAppointmentPass(message, folder) {
  const emailBody = message.getPlainBody(); // Text
  const emailHtml = message.getBody();      // HTML (QR lives here)

  const details = {
    appointmentId: "Not Found",
    appointmentDate: "",
    reportingTime: "",
    poNumbers: "",
    qrCodeUrl: ""
  };

  // ----------------------------------------------------
  // TEXT PARSING
  // ----------------------------------------------------
  const idMatch = emailBody.match(/Appointment ID\s*\n\s*(\d+)/i);
  if (idMatch) details.appointmentId = idMatch[1].trim();

  const dateMatch = emailBody.match(/Appointment Date\s*\n\s*(\d{4}-\d{2}-\d{2})/i);
  if (dateMatch) details.appointmentDate = dateMatch[1].trim();

  const timeMatch = emailBody.match(/Reporting Time\s*\n\s*(\d{2}:\d{2}\s*(?:AM|PM))/i);
  if (timeMatch) details.reportingTime = timeMatch[1].trim();

  const poMatch = emailBody.match(/following POs:[\s\S]*?(\d+)/i);
  if (poMatch) details.poNumbers = poMatch[1];

  // ----------------------------------------------------
  // QR CODE EXTRACTION (FIXED)
  // ----------------------------------------------------
  try {
    /**
     * Match ANY img inside the qr-section
     * This avoids brittle URL assumptions
     */
    const qrImgMatch = emailHtml.match(
      /<div class="qr-section">[\s\S]*?<img[^>]+src="([^"]+)"/i
    );

    if (!qrImgMatch || !qrImgMatch[1]) {
      Logger.log("QR image not found in HTML");
      details.qrCodeUrl = "NOT FOUND";
      return details;
    }

    // HTML entities decode (&amp; → &)
    const qrImageUrl = qrImgMatch[1].replace(/&amp;/g, '&');

    const imageBlob = UrlFetchApp.fetch(qrImageUrl, {
      followRedirects: true,
      muteHttpExceptions: true
    }).getBlob();

    const imageName = `QR_APPT_${details.appointmentId || 'UNKNOWN'}.jpeg`;
    const file = folder.createFile(imageBlob).setName(imageName);

    details.qrCodeUrl = file.getUrl();
    Logger.log(`QR code saved successfully: ${imageName}`);

  } catch (err) {
    Logger.log(`QR extraction failed: ${err.message}`);
    details.qrCodeUrl = "SAVE FAILED";
  }

  return details;
}

function sendRBLAppointmentRequestEmail(data) {

  const { orders } = data;

  if (!orders || !Array.isArray(orders) || orders.length === 0) {
    return { status: "error", message: "No orders provided" };
  }

  try {

    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.openById(SPREADSHEET_ID);
    const sheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_PO_DB);

    const dataRange = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    const headers = dataRange[0];
    const rows = dataRange.slice(1);

    const col = name => headers.indexOf(name);

    const IDX = {
      REF: col("EE_reference_code"),
      APPT_REQ_ID: col("Appointment Request ID"),
      APPT_REQ_TS: col("Appointment Request Timestamp")
    };

    validateHeaders(IDX);

    // =============================
    // CONFIG + META
    // =============================
    const channelConfig = fetchChannelConfig("RBL");
    if (!channelConfig?.to) {
      throw new Error("RBL config missing in Channel_Config");
    }

    const requestId = generateRequestId();
    const now = new Date();
    const appointmentDate = getAppointmentDate_rbl();

    const VENDOR_CODE = "40002051";

    let tableRows = [];
    let eligibleOrders = [];
    let pdfLinks = [];

    // =============================
    // FETCH MASTER PACKING DATA
    // =============================
    const packingSheet = ss.getSheetByName("Master_Packing_Data");
    if (!packingSheet) throw new Error("Master_Packing_Data not found");

    const packingData = packingSheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    const packingHeaders = packingData[0];

    const pcol = name => packingHeaders.indexOf(name);

    const P_IDX = {
      REF: pcol("Reference Code"),
      SKU: pcol("SKU"),
      BOX_ID: pcol("Box ID"),
      QTY: pcol("Item Quantity"),
    };

    validateHeaders(P_IDX);

    // =============================
    // LOOP ORDERS
    // =============================
    orders.forEach(order => {

      const poRef = order.poReference || "";
      const invoice = order.invoiceNumber || "";
      const refCode = order.id;

      // -------------------------
      // BUILD SKU → ARTICLE MAP
      // -------------------------
      const skuMap = {};
      (order.items || []).forEach(item => {

        if (!item.sku) return;

        skuMap[item.sku] = {
          articleCode: item.articleCode || item.sku,
          name: item.itemName || ""
        };

      });

      // -------------------------
      // PDF LINKS
      // -------------------------
      if (order.invoiceurl) {
        pdfLinks.push({
          label: `Invoice - ${invoice || poRef}`,
          url: order.invoiceurl
        });
      }

      if (order.poPdfUrl) {
        pdfLinks.push({
          label: `PO - ${poRef}`,
          url: order.poPdfUrl
        });
      }

      // -------------------------
      // FILTER PACKING DATA
      // -------------------------
      const filtered = packingData.slice(1).filter(r =>
        String(r[P_IDX.REF]).trim() === String(refCode).trim()
      );

      if (filtered.length === 0) return;

      // -------------------------
      // STEP 1: SKU + BOX_ID
      // -------------------------
      const boxLevel = {};

      filtered.forEach(r => {

        const sku = r[P_IDX.SKU];
        const boxId = r[P_IDX.BOX_ID];
        const qty = Number(r[P_IDX.QTY] || 0);

        const key = `${sku}|${boxId}`;

        if (!boxLevel[key]) {
          boxLevel[key] = {
            sku,
            totalQty: 0
          };
        }

        boxLevel[key].totalQty += qty;

      });

      // -------------------------
      // STEP 2: SKU + CASE SIZE
      // -------------------------
      const finalGrouped = {};

      Object.values(boxLevel).forEach(b => {

        const caseSize = b.totalQty;
        const key = `${b.sku}|${caseSize}`;

        if (!finalGrouped[key]) {
          finalGrouped[key] = {
            sku: b.sku,
            caseSize: caseSize,
            boxCount: 0,
            totalQty: 0
          };
        }

        finalGrouped[key].boxCount += 1;
        finalGrouped[key].totalQty += caseSize;

      });

      // -------------------------
      // BUILD TABLE
      // -------------------------
      Object.values(finalGrouped).forEach(g => {

        const itemData = skuMap[g.sku] || {
          articleCode: g.sku,
          name: ""
        };

        tableRows.push(`
          <tr>
            <td style="padding:8px;border:1px solid #ddd;">${VENDOR_CODE}</td>
            <td style="padding:8px;border:1px solid #ddd;">${poRef}</td>
            <td style="padding:8px;border:1px solid #ddd;">${invoice}</td>
            <td style="padding:8px;border:1px solid #ddd;">${itemData.articleCode}</td>
            <td style="padding:8px;border:1px solid #ddd;">${itemData.name}</td>
            <td style="padding:8px;border:1px solid #ddd;text-align:center;">${g.caseSize}</td>
            <td style="padding:8px;border:1px solid #ddd;text-align:center;">${g.boxCount}</td>
            <td style="padding:8px;border:1px solid #ddd;text-align:center;">${g.totalQty}</td>
            <td style="padding:8px;border:1px solid #ddd;text-align:center;">${appointmentDate}</td>
          </tr>
        `);

      });

      // -------------------------
      // TRACKING
      // -------------------------
      const matchedRows = [];

      for (let i = 0; i < rows.length; i++) {
        if (String(rows[i][IDX.REF]).trim() === String(refCode).trim()) {
          matchedRows.push(i + 2);
        }
      }

      if (matchedRows.length > 0) {
        eligibleOrders.push({
          rowIndexes: matchedRows,
          requestId,
          requestTs: now,
          poNumber: poRef
        });
      }

    });

    if (tableRows.length === 0) {
      return { status: "error", message: "No packing data found" };
    }

    // =============================
    // REMOVE DUPLICATE LINKS
    // =============================
    pdfLinks = [...new Map(pdfLinks.map(x => [x.url, x])).values()];

    const pdfSection = pdfLinks.length > 0
      ? `
      <p><b>Documents:</b></p>
      <ul>
        ${pdfLinks.map(l => `
          <li><a href="${l.url}" target="_blank">${l.label}</a></li>
        `).join("")}
      </ul>`
      : "";

    // =============================
    // EMAIL BODY
    // =============================
    const htmlBody = `
    <div style="font-family:Arial,sans-serif;">
      <h2>RBL / Hamleys - Appointment Request</h2>

      <p>Dear Team,</p>
      <p>Please provide appointment for the below shipment. The packing details of the shipments is shared below.</p>

      <table style="border-collapse:collapse;width:100%;font-size:13px;">
        <thead>
          <tr style="background:#f3f3f3;">
            <th style="border:1px solid #ddd;padding:8px;">Vendor</th>
            <th style="border:1px solid #ddd;padding:8px;">PO</th>
            <th style="border:1px solid #ddd;padding:8px;">Invoice</th>
            <th style="border:1px solid #ddd;padding:8px;">Article</th>
            <th style="border:1px solid #ddd;padding:8px;">Description</th>
            <th style="border:1px solid #ddd;padding:8px;">Case Size</th>
            <th style="border:1px solid #ddd;padding:8px;">Boxes</th>
            <th style="border:1px solid #ddd;padding:8px;">Qty</th>
            <th style="border:1px solid #ddd;padding:8px;">Appt Date</th>
          </tr>
        </thead>
        <tbody>
          ${tableRows.join("")}
        </tbody>
      </table>

      ${pdfSection}

      <p><b>Request ID:</b> ${requestId}</p>

      <p>Regards<br>Team Cubelelo</p>
    </div>`;

    // SEND EMAIL
    GmailApp.sendEmail(channelConfig.to, `RBL Appointment Request | ${requestId}`, "", {
      cc: channelConfig.cc || "",
      htmlBody: htmlBody
    });

    // UPDATE TRACKING
    if (eligibleOrders.length > 0) {
      updateRequestTracking(sheet, rows.length, IDX, eligibleOrders, requestId);
    }

    // LOG
    writeToLog(
      requestId,
      "Success",
      eligibleOrders.map(o => o.poNumber).join(", "),
      `To:${channelConfig.to}`,
      "RBL appointment email sent (final v2)"
    );

    return {
      status: "success",
      requestId,
      rows: tableRows.length
    };

  } catch (e) {

    writeToLog("RBL", "Failed", "-", "-", e.message);

    return {
      status: "error",
      message: e.message
    };
  }
}

function processChannelAppointments(channelName, manualSaleOrderList = null, mode = "FULL") 
{
  const lock = LockService.getScriptLock();
  if (!lock.tryLock(30000)) {
    return { status: "error", message: "System busy. Try again." };
  }

  try {

    const channel = Object.values(EMAIL_CONFIG)
      .find(c => c.NAME === channelName);

    if (!channel) throw new Error("Invalid channel");

    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.openById(SPREADSHEET_ID);
    const sheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_PO_DB);

    const data = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    const headers = data[0];
    const rows = data.slice(1);

    const col = name => headers.indexOf(name);

    const IDX = {
      CHANNEL: col("Channel Name"),
      ORDER_STATUS: col("EE_order_status"),
      AWB: col("AWB"),
      INVOICE_ID: col("Invoice Id"),
      PO_NUMBER: col("PO Number"),
      PO_DATE: col("PO Date"),
      EXPIRY_DATE: col("PO Expiry Date"),
      STORE_CODE: col("Store Code"),
      QTY: col("Qty"),
      BOXES: col("Box Data"),
      SALE_ORDER_NO: col("EE_reference_code"),
      APPT_REQ_ID: col("Appointment Request ID"),
      APPT_REQ_TS: col("Appointment Request Timestamp")
    };

    validateHeaders(IDX);

    const manualSet = manualSaleOrderList ? new Set(manualSaleOrderList) : null;

    const saleOrderMap = {};
    let hasOpenOrders = false;

    rows.forEach((row,i)=>{

      if(row[IDX.CHANNEL] !== channel.NAME) return;

      const status = String(row[IDX.ORDER_STATUS]||"").trim();
      const awb = String(row[IDX.AWB]||"").trim();
      const invoice = String(row[IDX.INVOICE_ID]||"").trim();
      const apptReq = String(row[IDX.APPT_REQ_ID]||"").trim();

      const saleOrder = String(row[IDX.SALE_ORDER_NO]||"").trim();
      if(!saleOrder) return;

      if(!manualSet && status==="Open") hasOpenOrders = true;

      let isTarget = true;
      if(manualSet) isTarget = manualSet.has(saleOrder);

      const boxCount = Number(row[IDX.BOXES]||0);

      if(
        isTarget &&
        awb === "" &&
        invoice !== "" &&
        status === "Confirmed" &&
        boxCount !== 0 &&
        apptReq === ""
      ){

        if(!saleOrderMap[saleOrder]){
          saleOrderMap[saleOrder] = {
            saleOrderNo:saleOrder,
            poNumber:row[IDX.PO_NUMBER],
            poDate:row[IDX.PO_DATE],
            expiryDate:row[IDX.EXPIRY_DATE],
            storeCode:row[IDX.STORE_CODE],
            totalQty:0,
            totalBoxes:boxCount,
            rowIndexes:[]
          };
        }

        saleOrderMap[saleOrder].totalQty += Number(row[IDX.QTY]||0);
        saleOrderMap[saleOrder].rowIndexes.push(i+2);
      }

    });

    const eligibleOrders = Object.values(saleOrderMap);
    const requestId = generateRequestId();

    if (mode !== "REMINDER" && !manualSet && hasOpenOrders) {
      writeToLog("SYSTEM","Blocked","-","-","Batch blocked due to open orders");
      return {status:"error",message:"Open orders exist"};
    }

    if (mode !== "REMINDER" && eligibleOrders.length === 0) {

  writeToLog(
    "SYSTEM",
    "Skipped",
    "-",
    "-",
    `No eligible ${channel.NAME} orders found`
  );

  return { status: "error", message: "No eligible orders found." };
  }

    const channelConfig = fetchChannelConfig(channel.NAME);

    // sendBigBasketEmails bypassed

    if(!channelConfig?.to) throw new Error("Channel email config missing");

  if (channel.NAME === "Zepto") {

  const pendingOrders = getZeptoPendingFromPODB();

  // ================= REMINDER MODE =================
  if (mode === "REMINDER") {

    if (pendingOrders.length === 0) {
      return { status: "error", message: "No pending appointments found." };
    }

    // ✅ ALWAYS SYNC MASTER SHEET
    const sheetUrl = syncMasterSheetWithPOData(pendingOrders);

    const htmlTable = buildZeptoAppointmentTable(pendingOrders);

    const htmlBody = `
    <div style="font-family:Roboto,Arial;font-size:14px">

    <p>Dear Team,</p>

    <p>
    This is a reminder for pending appointment confirmations.
    Kindly update the confirmed date for the below POs.
    </p>

    ${htmlTable}

    <p>
    Please update the confirmed date in the sheet:<br>
    <a href="${sheetUrl}" target="_blank">${sheetUrl}</a>
    </p>

    <p>
    Regards<br>
    Team Cubelelo
    </p>

    </div>`;

    GmailApp.sendEmail(channelConfig.to, `Zepto Appointment Reminder | Pending ${pendingOrders.length} POs`, "", {
      cc: channelConfig.cc || "",
      htmlBody: htmlBody
    });

    writeToLog(
      "REMINDER",
      "Success",
      pendingOrders.map(o => o.poNumber).join(", "),
      `To:${channelConfig.to}`,
      "Zepto reminder sent (master sheet synced)",
      sheetUrl
    );

    return {
      status: "success",
      type: "REMINDER",
      count: pendingOrders.length
    };
  }

  // ================= FULL MODE =================

  const newOrders = eligibleOrders;

  if (newOrders.length === 0 && pendingOrders.length === 0) {
    return { status: "error", message: "No orders found." };
  }

  const requestId = generateRequestId();

  // ✅ assign only to new orders
  newOrders.forEach(o => {
    o.requestId = requestId;
    o.requestTs = new Date();
  });

  const finalOrders = [...pendingOrders, ...newOrders];

  const sheetUrl = syncMasterSheetWithPOData(finalOrders);

  const htmlTable = buildZeptoAppointmentTable(finalOrders);

  const htmlBody = buildEmailBody(htmlTable, requestId, sheetUrl);

  GmailApp.sendEmail(channelConfig.to, `Zepto Appointment Request | ${requestId}`, "", {
    cc: channelConfig.cc || "",
    htmlBody: htmlBody
  });

  updateRequestTracking(sheet, rows.length, IDX, newOrders, requestId);

  writeToLog(
    requestId,
    "Success",
    finalOrders.map(o => o.poNumber).join(", "),
    `To:${channelConfig.to}`,
    "Zepto full request sent",
    sheetUrl
  );

  return {
    status: "success",
    type: "FULL",
    requestId
  };
  }

    // ================= INSTAMART =================

    let htmlTable = buildAppointmentEmailTable(eligibleOrders);

    let attachment = null;

    if(channel.MODE==="file"){
      attachment = createAppointmentFile(
        eligibleOrders,
        requestId,
        channel,
        channelConfig.to,
        channelConfig.cc
      );
    }

    const htmlBody = buildEmailBody(htmlTable,requestId,"");

    GmailApp.sendEmail(channelConfig.to, `${channel.NAME} Appointment Request | ${requestId}`, "", {
      cc: channelConfig.cc || "",
      htmlBody: htmlBody,
      attachments: attachment ? [attachment] : []
    });

    updateRequestTracking(sheet,rows.length,IDX,eligibleOrders,requestId);

    writeToLog(
      requestId,
      "Success",
      eligibleOrders.map(o=>o.saleOrderNo).join(", "),
      `To:${channelConfig.to}`,
      `${channel.NAME} email sent`
    );

    return {status:"success",requestId,count:eligibleOrders.length};

  }
  catch(err){
    writeToLog("SYSTEM","Failed","-","-",err.message);
    return {status:"error",message:err.message};
  }
  finally{
    lock.releaseLock();
  }
}

 * ==========================================================
 * BIGBASKET EMAIL ENGINE
 * ==========================================================

// sendBigBasketEmails deprecated


/**
 * ==========================================================
 * REQUEST TRACKING UPDATE
 * ==========================================================
 */

function updateRequestTracking(sheet,rowCount,IDX,orders,requestId){

  const idRange = sheet.getRange(2,IDX.APPT_REQ_ID+1,rowCount,1);
  const tsRange = sheet.getRange(2,IDX.APPT_REQ_TS+1,rowCount,1);

  const idValues = idRange.getValues();
  const tsValues = tsRange.getValues();

  const now = new Date();

  orders.forEach(o=>{
    o.rowIndexes.forEach(r=>{
      const i = r-2;
      if(i>=0 && i<idValues.length){
        idValues[i][0]=requestId;
        tsValues[i][0]=now;
      }
    });
  });

  idRange.setValues(idValues);
  tsRange.setValues(tsValues);
}


/**
 * ==========================================================
 * FILE / SHEET CREATION
 * ==========================================================
 */

function createZeptoAppointmentSheet(orders,requestId,to,cc){

  const appointmentDate = getAppointmentDate();

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.create(`Zepto_Appointment_${requestId}`);
  const sheet = ss.getActiveSheet();

  const headers=[
    "PO Number","PO Date","Expiry Date","Store Code","Vendor Name",
    "Qty","Boxes","Appointment Requested Date","Confirmed Date"
  ];


  sheet.getRange(1,1,1,headers.length).setValues([headers]);

  const rows = orders.map(o=>[
    o.poNumber,
    o.poDate,
    o.expiryDate,
    o.storeCode,
    EMAIL_CONFIG.ZEPTO.VENDOR,
    o.totalQty,
    o.totalBoxes,
    appointmentDate,
    ""
  ]);

  sheet.getRange(2,1,rows.length,headers.length).setValues(rows);

  const file = DriveApp.getFileById(ss.getId());
  const folder = DriveApp.getFolderById(DRIVE_FOLDER_ID);

  file.moveTo(folder);

  shareFile(file,to);
  shareFile(file,cc);

  return ss.getUrl();
}


function createAppointmentFile(orders,requestId,channel,to,cc){

  const tz = Session.getScriptTimeZone();
  const appointmentDate = getAppointmentDate();

  const headers=[
    "PO Number","PO Date","Expiry Date","Store Code","Vendor Name",
    "Qty","Boxes","Appointment Requested Date","Confirmed Date"
  ];

  const rows = orders.map(o=>[
    o.poNumber,
    Utilities.formatDate(new Date(o.poDate),tz,"dd-MM-yyyy"),
    Utilities.formatDate(new Date(o.expiryDate),tz,"dd-MM-yyyy"),
    o.storeCode,
    channel.VENDOR,
    o.totalQty,
    o.totalBoxes,
    appointmentDate,
    ""
  ]);

  const csv=[headers.join(","),...rows.map(r=>r.join(","))].join("\n");

  const blob = Utilities.newBlob(
    csv,
    "text/csv",
    `${channel.NAME}_Appointment_${requestId}.csv`
  );

  const folder = DriveApp.getFolderById(DRIVE_FOLDER_ID);
  const file = folder.createFile(blob);

  shareFile(file,to);
  shareFile(file,cc);

  return blob;
}


/**
 * ==========================================================
 * HELPERS
 * ==========================================================
 */

function getAppointmentDate(){

  const tz = Session.getScriptTimeZone();

  let d = new Date();
  d.setDate(d.getDate()+10);

  while(d.getDay()===0) d.setDate(d.getDate()+1);

  return Utilities.formatDate(d,tz,"dd-MM-yyyy");
}

function getAppointmentDate_rbl(){

  const tz = Session.getScriptTimeZone();

  let d = new Date();
  d.setDate(d.getDate()+7);

  while(d.getDay()===0) d.setDate(d.getDate()+1);

  return Utilities.formatDate(d,tz,"dd-MM-yyyy");
}

function generateRequestId(){
  return "REQ-"+Math.floor(Date.now()/1000);
}

function validateHeaders(obj){
  Object.entries(obj).forEach(([k,v])=>{
    if(v===-1) throw new Error(`Missing column: ${k}`);
  });
}

function shareFile(file,emails){

  if(!emails) return;

  emails.split(",").forEach(e=>{
    if(e.trim()) file.addEditor(e.trim());
  });
}

</p>

${sheetUrl ? `
<p>Update in sheet:<br>
<a href="${sheetUrl}" target="_blank">${sheetUrl}</a></p>
`:``}

<p>Request ID:<b>${requestId}</b></p>

<p>Regards<br>Team Cubelelo</p>

</div>`;
}

</table>`;
}

/**
 * ==========================================================
 * CHANNEL CONFIG FETCH
 * ==========================================================
 */

function fetchChannelConfig(channelName){

const sheet = SpreadsheetApp
.getActiveSpreadsheet()
.getSheetByName(SHEET_CHANNEL_CONFIG);

const data = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
const headers = data[0].map(h=>String(h).toLowerCase());

const colChannel=headers.indexOf("channel name");
const colTo=headers.indexOf("appointment to");
const colCC=headers.indexOf("appointment cc");

for(let i=1;i<data.length;i++){

const rowChannel = String(data[i][colChannel]||"").toLowerCase();

if(rowChannel.includes(channelName.toLowerCase())){
return{
to:data[i][colTo],
cc:data[i][colCC]
};
}
}

return null;
}

function writeToLog(requestId,status,poNumbers,recipients,notes,fileUrl=""){

const ss = SpreadsheetApp.openById(SPREADSHEET_ID);
let sheet = ss.getSheetByName(EMAIL_LOGS);

if(!sheet){

sheet = ss.insertSheet(EMAIL_LOGS);

sheet.appendRow([
"Timestamp",
"Request ID",
"Status",
"PO Numbers",
"Recipients",
"Notes",
"File URL"
]);
}

sheet.appendRow([
new Date(),
requestId,
status,
poNumbers,
recipients,
notes,
fileUrl
]);

}


function getZeptoPendingFromPODB() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.openById(SPREADSHEET_ID);
  const sheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_PO_DB);

  const data = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
  const headers = data[0];

  const col = name => headers.indexOf(name);

  const IDX = {
    CHANNEL: col("Channel Name"),
    PO: col("PO Number"),
    STORE: col("Store Code"),
    QTY: col("Qty"),
    BOX: col("Box Data"),
    PO_DATE: col("PO Date"),
    EXPIRY: col("PO Expiry Date"),
    APPT_ID: col("Appointment Request ID"),
    APPT_DATE: col("Appointment Date") // IMPORTANT
  };

  validateHeaders(IDX);

  const map = {};

  for (let i = 1; i < data.length; i++) {

    if (data[i][IDX.CHANNEL] !== "Zepto") continue;

    const apptId = String(data[i][IDX.APPT_ID] || "").trim();
    const apptDate = data[i][IDX.APPT_DATE];
    const apptTs = data[i][headers.indexOf("Appointment Request Timestamp")];

    // ✅ Pending condition
    if (!apptId || apptDate) continue;

    const po = String(data[i][IDX.PO]).trim();

    if (!map[po]) {
  map[po] = {
    poNumber: po,
    storeCode: data[i][IDX.STORE],
    totalQty: 0,
    totalBoxes: data[i][IDX.BOX],
    poDate: data[i][IDX.PO_DATE],
    expiryDate: data[i][IDX.EXPIRY],
    requestId: apptId,
    requestTs: apptTs
  };
}

    map[po].totalQty += Number(data[i][IDX.QTY] || 0);
  }

  return Object.values(map);
}

function syncMasterSheetWithPOData(pendingOrders) {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.openById(MASTER_APPOINTMENT_SHEET_ID);
  let sheet = ss.getSheetByName(MASTER_SHEET_NAME);

  if (!sheet) {
    sheet = ss.insertSheet(MASTER_SHEET_NAME);
  }

  const headers = [
    "PO Number","Store Code","Qty","Boxes","PO Date","Expiry Date",
    "Appointment Requested","Confirmed Date","Request ID","Request Timestamp"
  ];

  const tz = Session.getScriptTimeZone();
  const appointmentDate = getAppointmentDate();

  const rows = pendingOrders.map(o => [
    o.poNumber,
    o.storeCode,
    o.totalQty,
    o.totalBoxes,
    Utilities.formatDate(new Date(o.poDate), tz, "dd-MMM-yyyy"),
    Utilities.formatDate(new Date(o.expiryDate), tz, "dd-MMM-yyyy"),
    appointmentDate,
    "",
    o.requestId || "",
    o.requestTs || ""
  ]);

  // ✅ only clear old data, not structure
  if (sheet.getLastRow() > 1) {
    sheet.getRange(2,1,sheet.getLastRow(),headers.length).clearContent();
  }

  sheet.getRange(1,1,1,headers.length).setValues([headers]);

  if (rows.length > 0) {
    sheet.getRange(2,1,rows.length,headers.length).setValues(rows);
  }

  return ss.getUrl();
}
